Ethay Alewhay 



Etymologyyay 

(Uppliedsay Byay Ayay Atelay Onsumptivecay Usheryay Otay 
Ayay Ammabgbay Oolschay) 

Ethay alepay Usheryay eadbarethray inyay oatcay, earthay, odybay, andyay ainbray ; 
Iyay eesay imhay ownay. Ehay asway everyay ustingday ishay oldyay exiconslay andyay 
ammarsgray, ithway ayay ueerqay andkerchiefhay, ockinglymay embellishedyay 
ithway allyay ethay aygay agsflay ofyay allyay ethay ownknay ationsnay ofyay ethay orldway. 
Ehay ovedlay otay ustday ishay oldyay ammarsgray ; ityay omehowsay ildlymay 
emindedray imhay ofyay ishay ortalitymay. 



Etymologyyay 



' Ilewhay ouyay aketay inyay andhay otay oolschay othersyay, andyay otay eachtay 
emthay byay atwhay amenay ayay alewhay-ishfay isyay otay ebay alledcay inyay ouryay onguetay, 
eavinglay outyay, oughthray ignoranceyay, ethay etterlay Hay, ichwhay almostyay 
aloneyay akethmay upyay ethay ignificationsay ofyay ethay ordway, ouyay eliverday 
atthay ichwhay isyay otnay uetray.' Akluythay. 

1 Alewhay. * * * Sway. andyay Anday. alhvay. Isthay animalyay isyay 
amednay omfray oundnessray oryay ollingray ; orfay inyay Anday. althvay isyay archedyay 
oryay aultedvay.' Ebsterway'say Ictionaryday. 

' Alewhay. * * * Ityay isyay oremay immediatelyyay omfray ethay Utday. 
andyay Ergay. Way alienyay ; Ayay.Say. Alwway-ianyay yay otay ollray, otay allowway.' 

Ichardsonray'say Ictionaryday.

Extractsyay 
(Uppliedsay Byay Ayay Ubsay-Ubsay-Ibrarianlay) 

Ityay illway ebay eensay atthay isthay eremay ainstakingpay urrowerbay andyay 
ubgray -ormway ofyay ayay oorpay evilday ofyay ayay Ubsay -Ubsay appearsyay otay avehay onegay 
oughthray ethay onglay Aticansvay andyay eetstray-allsstay ofyay ethay earthyay, ickpay- 
ingyay upyay ateverwhay andomray allusionsyay otay aleswhay ehay ouldcay anywaysyay 
indfay inyay anyyay ookbay atsoeverwhay, acredsay oryay ofanepray. Ereforethay 
ouyay ustmay otnay, inyay everyyay asecay atyay eastlay, aketay ethay iggledyhay-iggledypay 
alewhay atementsstay, oweverhay authenticyay, inyay esethay extractsyay, orfay 
eritablevay ospelgay etologycay. Arfay omfray ityay. Asyay ouchingtay ethay 
ancientyay authorsyay enerallygay, asyay ellway asyay ethay oetspay erehay appearingyay, 
esethay extractsyay areyay olelysay aluablevay oryay entertainingyay, asyay affordingyay 
ayay ancingglay irdbay'say-eyeyay iewvay ofyay atwhay ashay eenbay omiscuouslypray 
aidsay, oughtthay, anciedfay, andyay ungsay ofyay Eviathanlay, byay anymay 
ationsnay andyay enerationsgay, includingyay ouryay ownyay. 

Osay arefay eethay ellway, oorpay evilday ofyay ayay Ubsay-Ubsay, osewhay ommencay- 
atortay Iyay amyay. Outhay elongestbay otay atthay opelesshay, allowsay ibetray 
ichwhay onay ineway ofyay isthay orldway illway everyay armway ; andyay orfay omwhay 
evenyay Alepay Erryshay ouldway ebay ootay osyray-ongstray ; utbay ithway omwhay 
oneyay ometimessay oveslay otay itsay, andyay eelfay oorpay-evilishday, ootay ; andyay 
owgray onvivialcay uponyay earstay ; andyay aysay otay emthay untlyblay ithway ullfay 
eyesyay andyay emptyyay assesglay, andyay inyay otnay altogetheryay unpleasantyay 
adnesssay Ivegay ityay upyay, Ubsay-Ubssay ! Orfay byay owhay uchmay ethay oremay 
ainspay eyay aketay otay easeplay ethay orldway, byay osay uchmay ethay oremay allshay 
eyay oreverfay ogay anklessthay ! Ouldway atthay Iyay ouldcay earclay outyay 
Amptonhay Ourtcay andyay ethay Uileriestay orfay eyay ! Utbay ulpgay ownday 
ouryay earstay andyay iehay aloftyay otay ethay oyalray-astmay ithway ouryay eartshay ; 
orfay ouryay iendsfray owhay avehay onegay eforebay areyay earingclay outyay ethay 
evensay-oriedstay eavenshay, andyay akingmay efugeesray ofyay onglay-amperedpay 
Abrielgay, Ichaelmay, andyay Aphaelray, againstyay ouryay omingcay. Erehay 
eyay ikestray utbay interedsplay eartshay ogethertay erethay, eyay allshay 
ikestray unsplinterableyay assesglay!

' Ownay ethay Ordlay adhay eparedpray ayay eatgray ishfay otay allowsway upyay 
Onahjay.' Onahjay. 

' Erethay ogay ethay ipsshay ; erethay isyay atthay Eviathanlay omwhay outhay 
asthay ademay otay ayplay ereinthay.' Almspsay. 

' Inyay atthay ayday, ethay Ordlay ithway ishay oresay, andyay eatgray, andyay ongstray 
ordsway, allshay unishpay Eviathanlay ethay iercingpay erpentsay, evenyay 
Eviathanlay atthay ookedcray erpentsay ; andyay ehay allshay ayslay ethay agondray 
atthay isyay inyay ethay easay.' Isaiahyay. 

* Andyay atwhay ingthay oeversay esidesbay omethcay ithinway ethay aoschay 
ofyay isthay onstermay'say outhmay, ebay ityay eastbay, oatbay, oryay onestay, ownday ityay 
oesgay allyay incontinentlyyay atthay oulfay eatgray allowsway ofyay ishay, andyay 
erishethpay inyay ethay ottomlessbay ulfgay ofyay ishay aunchpay.' 

Ollancfshay Utarchplay'say Oralsmay. 

' Ethay Indianyay Easay eedethbray ethay ostmay andyay ethay iggestbay ishesfay 
atthay areyay : amongyay ichwhay ethay Aleswhay andyay Irlpooleswhay alledcay 
Alaenebay, aketay upyay asyay uchmay inyay engthlay asyay ourfay acresyay oryay arpensyay ofyay 
andlay.' Ollandhay'say Inyplay. 

' Arcelyscay adhay eway oceededpray otway aysday onyay ethay easay, enwhay 
aboutyay unrisesay ayay eatgray anymay Aleswhay andyay otheryay onstersmay ofyay 
ethay easay, appearedyay. Amongyay ethay ormerfay, oneyay asway ofyay ayay ostmay 
onstrousmay izesay. * * * Isthay amecay owardstay usyay, openyay- 
outhedmay, aisingray ethay avesway onyay allyay idessay, andyay eatingbay ethay easay 
eforebay imhay intoyay ayay oamfay.' 

Ooketay'say Ucianlay. Ethay Uetray Istoryhay.

ofyay ichwhay ehay oughtbray omesay otay ethay ingkay. * * * Ethay estbay

ortyfay-eightyay, omesay iftyfay ardsyay onglay. Ehay aidsay atthay ehay asway oneyay 
ofyay ixsay owhay adhay illedkay ixtysay inyay otway aysday.'

ainspay. * * *

ayay arrelbay ofyay erringshay inyay ishay ellybay. * * * 

Oneyay ofyay ouryay arpooneershay oldtay emay atthay ehay aughtcay onceyay ayay 
alewhay inyay Itzbergenspay atthay asway itewhay allyay overyay.'

idday affordyay 500 eightway ofyay aleenbay. Ethay awsjay ofyay ityay andstay orfay ayay 
ategay inyay ethay ardengay ofyay Itferrenpay.'

uentlyqay attendedyay ithway uchsay anyay insupportableyay ellsmay, asyay otay 
ingbray onyay ayay isorderday ofyay ethay ainbray.' 

Ulloayay'say Outhsay Americayay. 

1 Otay iftyfay osenchay sylphsay ofyay ecialspay otenay, 
Eway usttray ethay importantyay argechay, ethay etticoatpay. 
Oftyay avehay eway ownknay atthay evensay-oldfay encefay otay ailfay, 
Othay' uffedstay ithway oopshay andyay armedyay ithway ibsray ofyay alewhay.' 

Aperay ofyay ethay Ocklay. 

' Ifyay eway omparecay andlay animalsyay inyay espectray otay agnitudemay, ithway 
osethay atthay aketay upyay eirthay abodeyay inyay ethay eepday, eway allshay indfay eythay 
illway appearyay ontemptiblecay inyay ethay omparisoncay. Ethay alewhay isyay 
oubtlessday ethay argestlay animalyay inyay eationcray.' 

Oldsmithgay'say Atnay. Isthay. 

' Ifyay ouyay ouldshay itewray ayay ablefay orfay ittlelay ishesfay, ouyay ouldway 
akemay emthay eakspay ikelay eatgray aleswhay.' 

Oldsmithgay otay Ohnsonjay. 

' Inyay ethay afternoonyay eway awsay atwhay asway upposedsay otay ebay ayay ockray, 
utbay ityay asway oundfay otay ebay ayay eadday alewhay, ichwhay omesay Asiaticsyay adhay 
illedkay, andyay ereway enthay owingtay ashoreyay. Eythay eemedsay otay enyay- 
eavourday otay oncealcay emselvesthay ehindbay ethay alewhay, inyay orderyay otay 
avoidyay eingbay eensay byay usyay.' Ookcay'say Oyagesvay. 

' Ethay argerlay aleswhay, eythay eldomsay enturevay otay attackyay. Eythay 
andstay inyay osay eatgray eaddray ofyay omesay ofyay emthay, atthay enwhay outyay atyay 
easay eythay areyay afraidyay otay entionmay evenyay eirthay amesnay, andyay arrycay 
ungday, imelay-onestay, uniperjay-oodway, andyay omesay otheryay articlesyay ofyay 
ethay amesay aturenay inyay eirthay oatsbay, inyay orderyay otay errifytay andyay eventpray 
eirthay ootay earnay approachyay.' 

Unoyay Onvay Oiltray'say Etterslay onyay Anksbay' say andyay

Apterchay Iyay 

Oomingslay 

Allcay emay Ishmaelyay. Omesay earsyay agoyay evernay indmay owhay 
onglay eciselypray avinghay ittlelay oryay onay oneymay inyay myay ursepay, 
andyay othingnay articularpay otay interestyay emay onyay oreshay, Iyay oughtthay 
Iyay ouldway ailsay aboutyay ayay ittlelay andyay eesay ethay ateryway artpay ofyay ethay 
orldway. Ityay isyay ayay ayway Iyay avehay ofyay ivingdray offyay ethay eensplay, andyay 
egulatingray ethay irculationcay. Eneverwhay Iyay indfay elfmysay 
owinggray imgray aboutyay ethay outhmay ; eneverwhay ityay isyay ayay ampday, 
izzlydray Ovembernay inyay myay oulsay ; eneverwhay Iyay indfay elfmysay 
involuntarilyyay ausingpay eforebay offincay arehousesway, andyay ingbray- 
ingyay upyay ethay earray ofyay everyyay uneralfay Iyay eetmay ; andyay especiallyyay 
eneverwhay myay oshypay etgay uchsay anyay upperyay andhay ofyay emay, atthay 
ityay equiresray ayay ongstray oralmay inciplepray otay eventpray emay omfray 
eliberatelyday eppingstay intoyay ethay eetstray, andyay ethodicallymay 
ockingknay eoplepay'say atshay offyay enthay, Iyay accountyay ityay ighhay imetay 
otay etgay otay easay asyay oonsay asyay Iyay ancay. Isthay isyay myay ubstitutesay orfay 
istolpay andyay allbay. Ithway ayay ilosophicalphay ourishflay Atocay owsthray 
imselfhay uponyay ishay ordsway ; Iyay uietlyqay aketay otay ethay ipshay. 
Erethay isyay othingnay urprisingsay inyay isthay. Ifyay eythay utbay ewknay 
ityay, almostyay allyay enmay inyay eirthay egreeday, omesay imetay oryay otheryay, 
erishchay eryvay earlynay ethay amesay eelingsfay owardtay ethay oceanyay 
ithway emay. 

Erethay ownay isyay ouryay insularyay itycay ofyay ethay Anhattoesmay, 
eltedbay oundray byay arveswhay asyay Indianyay islesyay byay oralcay eefsray 
ommercecay urroundssay ityay ithway erhay urfsay. Ightray andyay eftlay, ethay 
eetsstray aketay ouyay aterwardway. Itsyay extremeyay ownday -owntay isyay ethay 
atterybay, erewhay atthay oblenay olemay isyay ashedway byay avesway, andyay 

Olvay. Iyay. Ayay 



2 Obymay-Ickday 

ooledcay byay eezesbray, ichwhay ayay ewfay ourshay eviouspray ereway outyay ofyay 
ightsay ofyay andlay. Ooklay atyay ethay owdscray ofyay aterway -azersgay erethay. 

Ircumambulatecay ethay itycay ofyay ayay eamydray Abbathsay afteryay- 
oonnay. Ogay omfray Orlearscay Ookhay otay Oentiescay Ipslay, andyay 
omfray encethay, byay Itehallwhay, orthwardnay. Atwhay oday ouyay 
eesay ? Ostedpay ikelay ilentsay entinelssay allyay aroundyay ethay owntay, 
andstay ousandsthay uponyay ousandsthay ofyay ortalmay enmay ixedfay 
inyay oceanyay everiesray. Omesay eaninglay againstyay ethay ilesspay ; 
omesay eatedsay uponyay ethay ierpay-eadshay ; omesay ookinglay overyay 
Evhay ulwarksbay ofyay ipsshay omfray Inachay ; omesay ighhay aloftyay inyay 
ethay iggingray, asyay ifyay ivingstray otay etgay ayay illstay etterbay eawardsay 
eeppay. Utbay esethay areyay allyay andsmenlay ; ofyay eekway aysday entpay 
upyay inyay athlay andyay asterplay iedtay otay ounterscay, ailednay otay enchesbay, 
inchedclay otay esksday. Owhay enthay isyay isthay ? Areyay ethay eengray 
ieldsfay onegay ? Atwhay oday eythay erehay ? 

Utbay ooklay ! erehay omecay oremay owdscray, acingpay aightstray orfay 
ethay aterway, andyay eeminglysay oundbay orfay ayay iveday. Angestray ! 
Othingnay illway ontentcay emthay utbay ethay extremestyay imitlay ofyay ethay 
andlay ; oiteringlay underyay ethay adyshay eelay ofyay onderyay arehousesway 
illway otnay ufficesay. Onay. Eythay ustmay etgay ustjay asyay ighnay ethay 
aterway asyay eythay ossiblypay ancay ithoutway allingfay inyay. Andyay erethay 
eythay andstay ilesmay ofyay emthay eagueslay. Inlandersyay allyay, eythay 
omecay omfray aneslay andyay alleysyay, eetsstray andyay avenuesyay orthnay, 
eastyay, outhsay, andyay estway. Etyay erehay eythay allyay uniteyay. Elltay emay, 
oesday ethay agneticmay irtuevay ofyay ethay eedlesnay ofyay ethay ompassescay 
ofyay allyay osethay ipsshay attractyay emthay itherthay ? 

Onceyay oremay. Aysay, ouyay areyay inyay ethay ountrycay ; inyay omesay 
ighhay andlay ofyay akeslay. Aketay almostyay anyyay athpay ouyay easeplay, 
andyay entay otay oneyay ityay arriescay ouyay ownday inyay ayay aleday, andyay eaveslay 
ouyay erethay byay ayay oolpay inyay ethay eamstray. Erethay isyay agicmay inyay ityay. 
Etlay ethay ostmay absentyay-indedmay ofyay enmay ebay ungedplay inyay ishay

Apterchay Iiyay 

Ethay Arpetcay-Agbay 

Iyay uffedstay ayay irtshay oryay otway intoyay myay oldyay arpetcay-agbay, uckedtay 
ityay underyay myay armyay, andyay artedstay orfay Apecay Ornhay andyay ethay 
Acificpay. Uittingqay ethay oodgay itycay ofyay oldyay Anhattomay, Iyay ulyday 
arrivedyay inyay Ewnay Edfordbay. Ityay asway onyay ayay Aturdaysay ightnay inyay 
Ecemberday. Uchmay asway Iyay isappointedday uponyay earninglay 
atthay ethay ittlelay acketpay orfay Antucketnay adhay alreadyyay ailedsay, 
andyay atthay onay ayway ofyay eachingray atthay aceplay ouldway offeryay, illtay 
ethay ollowingfay Ondaymay. 

Asyay ostmay oungyay andidatescay orfay ethay ainspay andyay enaltiespay 
ofyay alingwhay opstay atyay isthay amesay Ewnay Edfordbay, encethay otay 
embarkyay onyay eirthay oyagevay, ityay aymay asyay ellway ebay elatedray atthay Iyay 5 
orfay oneyay, adhay onay ideayay ofyay osay oingday. Orfay myay indmay asway ademay 
upyay otay ailsay inyay onay otheryay anthay ayay Antucketnay aftcray, ecausebay 
erethay asway ayay inefay, oisterousbay omethingsay aboutyay everythingyay 
onnectedcay ithway atthay amousfay oldyay islandyay, ichwhay amazinglyyay 
easedplay emay. Esidesbay, oughthay Ewnay Edfordbay ashay ofyay atelay 
eenbay aduallygray onopolisingmay ethay usinessbay ofyay alingwhay, andyay 
oughthay inyay isthay attermay oorpay oldyay Antucketnay isyay ownay uchmay 
ehindbay erhay, etyay Antucketnay asway erhay eatgray originalyay ethay 
Etyray ofyay isthay Arthagecay ; ethay aceplay erewhay ethay irstfay eadday 
Americanyay alewhay asway andedstray. Erewhay elseyay utbay omfray 
Antucketnay idday osethay aboriginalyay alemenwhay, ethay Edray Enmay, 
irstfay allysay outyay inyay anoescay otay ivegay asechay otay ethay eviathanlay ? 
Andyay erewhay utbay omfray Antucketnay, ootay, idday atthay irstfay advenyay- 
uroustay ittlelay oopslay utpay orthfay, artlypay adenlay ithway importedyay 
obblecay-onesstay osay oesgay ethay orystay otay owthray atyay ethay aleswhay,

Ayay undredhay ackblay acesfay urnedtay oundray inyay eirthay owsray otay eerpay ; 
andyay eyondbay, ayay ackblay Angelyay ofyay Oomday asway eatingbay ayay ookbay 
inyay ayay ulpitpay. Ityay asway ayay egronay urchchay ; andyay ethay eacherpray'say 
exttay asway aboutyay ethay acknessblay ofyay arknessday, andyay ethay eepway- 
ingyay andyay ailingway andyay eethtay -ashinggnay erethay. Ahay, Ishmaelyay, 
utteredmay Iyay, ackingbay outyay, Etchedwray entertainmentyay atyay ethay 
ignsay ofyay ' Ethay Aptray ' ! 

Ovingmay onyay, Iyay atyay astlay amecay otay ayay imday ortsay ofyay ightlay otnay arfay 
omfray ethay ocksday, andyay eardhay ayay orlornfay eakingcray inyay ethay airyay ; 
andyay ookinglay upyay, awsay ayay ingingsway ignsay overyay ethay oorday ithway 
ayay itewhay aintingpay uponyay ityay, aintlyfay epresentingray ayay alltay aightstray 
etjay ofyay istymay ayspray, andyay esethay ordsway underneathyay ' Ethay 
Outerspay-Innyay : Eterpay Offincay.'

Apterchay Iiiyay 

Ethay Ottterspay-Innyay 

Enteringyay atthay ablegay -endedyay Outerspay-Innyay, ouyay oundfay 
ourselfyay inyay ayay ideway, owlay, agglingstray entryyay ithway oldyay-ashionedfay 
ainscotsway, emindingray oneyay ofyay ethay ulwarksbay ofyay omesay oncay- 
emnedday oldyay aftcray. Onyay oneyay idesay unghay ayay eryvay argelay oilyay- 
aintingpay osay oroughlythay esmokedbay, andyay everyyay ayway efacedday, 
atthay inyay ethay unequalyay osscray-ightslay byay ichwhay ouyay iewedvay ityay, 
ityay asway onlyyay byay iligentday udystay andyay ayay eriessay ofyay ematicsystay 
isitsvay otay ityay, andyay arefulcay inquiryyay ofyay ethay eighboursnay, atthay 
ouyay ouldcay anyyay ayway arriveyay atyay anyay understandingyay ofyay itsyay 
urposepay. Uchsay unaccountableyay assesmay ofyay adesshay andyay 
adowsshay, atthay atyay irstfay ouyay almostyay oughtthay omesay ambitiousyay 
oungyay artistyay, inyay ethay imetay ofyay ethay Ewnay Englandyay agshay, adhay 
endeavouredyay otay elineateday aoschay ewitchedbay. Utbay byay intday 
ofyay uchmay andyay earnestyay ontemplationcay, andyay oftyay-epeatedray 
onderingspay, andyay especiallyyay byay owingthray openyay ethay ittlelay 
indowway owardtay ethay ackbay ofyay ethay entryyay, ouyay atyay astlay omecay 
otay ethay onclusioncay atthay uchsay anyay ideayay, oweverhay ildway, ightmay 
otnay ebay altogetheryay unwarrantedyay. 

Utbay atwhay ostmay uzzledpay andyay onfoundedcay ouyay asway ayay 
onglay, imberlay, ortentouspay, ackblay assmay ofyay omethingsay overhay- 
ingyay inyay ethay entrecay ofyay ethay icturepay overyay eethray ueblay, imday, 
erpendicularpay ineslay oatingflay inyay ayay amelessnay eastyay. Ayay oggybay, 
oggysay, uitchysqay icturepay ulytray, enoughyay otay ivedray ayay ervousnay 
anmay istractedday. Etyay erethay asway ayay ortsay ofyay indefiniteyay, alfhay- 
attainedyay, unimaginableyay ublimitysay aboutyay ityay atthay airlyfay 
ozefray ouyay otay ityay, illtay ouyay inyay oluntarilyvay, ooktay anyay oathyay ithway 
ourselfyay otay indfay outyay atwhay atthay arvellousmay aintingpay eantmay.

14 Obymay-Ickday 

Everyay andyay anonyay ayay ightbray, utbay, alasyay, eceptiveday ideayay ouldway 
artday ouyay oughthray. Ityay 'say ethay Ackblay Easay inyay ayay idnightmay alegay. 
Ityay 'say ethay unnaturalyay ombatcay ofyay ethay ourfay imalpray elementsyay. 
Ityay 'say ayay astedblay eathhay. Ityay 'say ayay Erboreanhypay interway enescay. 
Ityay 'say ethay eakingbray-upyay ofyay ethay iceyay-oundbay eamstray ofyay Imetay.

ayay aintfay esemblanceray otay ayay iganticgay ishfay ? evenyay ethay eatgray 
eviathanlay imselfhay ? 

Inyay actfay, ethay artistyay'say esignday eemedsay isthay : ayay inalfay eorythay

ubjectsay. Ethay icturepay epresentsray ayay Apecay-Ornerhay inyay ayay eatgray 
urricanehay ; ethay alfhay-ounderedfay ipshay elteringway erethay ithway 
itsyay eethray ismantledday astsmay aloneyay isiblevay ; andyay anyay exasperyay- 
atedyay alewhay, urposingpay otay ingspray eanclay overyay ethay aftcray, isyay 
inyay ethay enormousyay actyay ofyay impalingyay imselfhay uponyay ethay eethray 
astmay-eadshay. 

Ethay oppositeyay allway ofyay isthay entryyay asway unghay allyay overyay ithway 
ayay eathenishhay arrayyay ofyay onstrousmay ubsclay andyay earsspay. Omesay 
ereway icklythay etsay ithway itteringglay eethtay esemblingray ivoryyay 
awssay ; othersyay ereway uftedtay ithway otsknay ofyay umanhay airhay ; andyay 
oneyay asway icklesay-apedshay, ithway ayay astvay andlehay eepingsway oundray 
ikelay ethay egmentsay ademay inyay ethay ewnay-ownmay assgray byay ayay onglay- 
armedyay owermay. Ouyay udderedshay asyay ouyay azedgay, andyay 
onderedway atwhay onstrousmay annibalcay andyay avagesay ouldcay 
everyay avehay onegay ayay eathday-arvestinghay ithway uchsay ayay ackinghay, 
orrifyinghay implementyay. Ixedmay ithway esethay ereway ustyray 
oldyay alingwhay-anceslay andyay arpoonshay allyay okenbray andyay eformedday.

ownay ildlyway elbowedyay, iftyfay earsyay agoyay idday Athannay Ainsway 
illkay ifteenfay aleswhay etweenbay ayay unrisesay andyay ayay unsetsay. Andyay 
atthay arpoonhay osay ikelay ayay orkscrewcay ownay asway ungflay inyay

ardway ainslay offyay ethay Apecay ofyay Ancoblay. Ethay originalyay ironyay

Ossingcray isthay uskyday entryyay, andyay onyay oughthray onyay owlay-

ithway uchsay owlay onderouspay eamsbay aboveyay, andyay uchsay oldyay 
inkledwray anksplay eneathbay, atthay ouyay ouldway almostyay ancyfay 
ouyay odtray omesay oldyay aftcray'say ockpitscay, especiallyyay ofyay uchsay ayay 
owlinghay ightnay, enwhay isthay ornercay-anchoredyay oldyay arkyay ockedray 
osay uriouslyfay. Onyay oneyay idesay oodstay ayay onglay, owlay, elfshay-ikelay

aritiesray atheredgay omfray isthay ideway orldway'say emotestray ooksnay. 
Ojectingpray omfray ethay urtherfay angleyay ofyay ethay oomray andsstay ayay 
arkday-ookinglay enday ethay arbay ayay uderay attemptyay atyay ayay ightray 
alewhay'say eadhay. Ebay atthay owhay ityay aymay, erethay andsstay ethay astvay 
archedyay onebay ofyay ethay alewhay'say awjay, osay ideway, ayay oachcay ightmay 
almostyay ivedray eneathbay ityay. Ithinway areyay abbyshay elvesshay, 
angedray oundray ithway oldyay ecantersday, ottlesbay, asksflay ; andyay inyay 
osethay awsjay ofyay iftsway estructionday, ikelay anotheryay ursedcay Onahjay 
(byay ichwhay amenay indeedyay eythay alledcay imhay), ustlesbay ayay ittlelay 
itheredway oldyay anmay, owhay, orfay eirthay oneymay, earlyday ellssay ethay 
ailorssay eliriumsday andyay eathday. 

Abominableyay areyay ethay umblerstay intoyay ichwhay ehay ourspay ishay 
oisonpay. Oughthay uetray inderscylay ithoutway ithinway, ethay 
illainousvay eengray ogglinggay assesglay eceitfullyday aperedtay ownday- 
ardway otay ayay eatingchay ottombay. Arallelpay eridiansmay udelyray 
eckedpay intoyay ethay assglay, urroundsay esethay ootpadsfay' obletsgay.

Ethay Outerspay-Innyay 17 

'Andlordlay,' Iyay isperedwhay, way atthay ainyay'tay ethay arpooneerhay, 
isyay ityay ? ' 

1 Ohyay, onay/ aidsay ehay, ookinglay ayay ortsay ofyay iabolicallyday unnyfay, 
4 ethay arpooneerhay isyay ayay arkday - omplexionedcay apchay. Ehay 
evernay eatsyay umplingsday, ehay onday'tay ehay eatsyay othingnay utbay 
eaksstay, andyay ikeslay 'emyay areray.' 

' Ethay evilday ehay oesday, ' ayssay Iyay. ' Erewhay isyay atthay arpooneerhay ? 
Isyay ehay erehay ? ' 

' Ehay '11 ebay erehay aforeyay onglay,' asway ethay answeryay. 

Iyay ouldcay otnay elphay ityay, utbay Iyay eganbay otay eelfay uspicioussay ofyay 
isthay ' arkday-omplexionedcay ' arpooneerhay. Atyay anyyay ateray, Iyay 
ademay upyay myay indmay atthay ifyay ityay osay urnedtay outyay atthay eway ouldshay 
eepslay ogethertay, ehay ustmay undressyay andyay etgay intoyay edbay eforebay 
Iyay idday. 

Uppersay overyay, ethay ompanycay entway ackbay otay ethay arbay-oomray, 
enwhay, owingknay otnay atwhay elseyay otay oday ithway elfmysay, Iyay esolvedray 
otay endspay ethay estray ofyay ethay eveningyay asyay ayay ookerlay-onyay. 

Esentlypray ayay iotingray oisenay asway eardhay ithoutway. Artingstay 
upyay, ethay andlordlay iedcray, ' Atthay 'say ethay Ampusgray'say ewcray. Iyay 
eedsay erhay eportedray inyay ethay offingyay isthay orningmay ; ayay eethray 
earsyay' oyagevay, andyay ayay ullfay ipshay. Urrahhay, oysbay ; ownay eway '11 
avehay ethay atestlay ewsnay omfray ethay Eegeesfay.' 

Ayay ampingtray ofyay easay-ootsbay asway eardhay inyay ethay entryyay ; ethay 
oorday asway ungflay openyay, andyay inyay olledray ayay ildway etsay ofyay arinersmay 
enoughyay. Envelopedyay inyay eirthay aggyshay atchway-oatscay, andyay 
ithway eirthay eadshay uffledmay inyay oollenway omforterscay, allyay ebay- 
arnedday andyay aggedray, andyay eirthay eardsbay iffstay ithway iciclesyay, 
eythay eemedsay anyay eruptionyay ofyay earsbay omfray Abradorlay. Eythay 
adhay ustjay andedlay omfray eirthay oatbay, andyay isthay asway ethay irstfay 
ousehay eythay enteredyay. Onay onderway, enthay, atthay eythay ademay

18 Obymay-Ickday 

oresway asway ayay overeignsay urecay orfay allyay oldscay andyay atarrhscay 
atsoeverwhay, evernay indmay ofyay owhay onglay andingstay, oryay etherwhay 
aughtcay offyay ethay oastcay ofyay Abradorlay, oryay onyay ethay eatherway-idesay 
ofyay anyay iceyay -islandyay. 

Ethay iquorlay oonsay ountedmay intoyay eirthay eadshay, asyay ityay 
enerallygay oesday evenyay ithway ethay arrantestyay operstay ewlynay 
andedlay omfray easay, andyay eythay eganbay aperingcay aboutyay ostmay 
obstreperouslyyay. 

Iyay observedyay, oweverhay, atthay oneyay ofyay emthay eldhay omewhatsay 
aloofyay, andyay oughthay ehay eemedsay esirousday otnay otay oilspay ethay 
ilarityhay ofyay ishay ipmatesshay byay ishay ownyay obersay acefay, etyay uponyay 
ethay olewhay ehay efrainedray omfray akingmay asyay uchmay oisenay asyay ethay 
estray. Isthay anmay interestedyay emay atyay onceyay ; andyay incesay ethay easay- 
odsgay adhay ordainedyay atthay ehay ouldshay oonsay ecomebay myay ipshay- 
atemay (oughthay utbay ayay eepingslay-artnerpay oneyay, osay arfay asyay isthay 
arrativenay isyay oncernedcay), Iyay illway erehay enturevay uponyay ayay ittlelay 
escriptionday ofyay imhay. Ehay oodstay ullfay ixsay eetfay inyay eighthay, ithway 
oblenay ouldersshay, andyay ayay estchay ikelay ayay offercay-amday. Iyay avehay 
eldomsay eensay uchsay awnbray inyay ayay anmay. Ishay acefay asway eeplyday 
ownbray andyay urntbay, akingmay ishay itewhay eethtay azzlingday byay ethay 
ontrastcay ; ilewhay inyay ethay eepday adowsshay ofyay ishay eyesyay oatedflay 
omesay eminiscencesray atthay idday otnay eemsay otay ivegay imhay uchmay 
oyjay. Ishay oicevay atyay onceyay announcedyay atthay ehay asway ayay 
Outhernersay, andyay omfray ishay inefay aturestay, Iyay oughtthay ehay ustmay 
ebay oneyay ofyay osethay alltay ountaineersmay omfray ethay Alleghanianyay 
Idgeray inyay Irginiavay. Enwhay ethay evelryray ofyay ishay ompanionscay 
adhay ountedmay otay itsyay eighthay, isthay anmay ippedslay awayyay unobyay- 
ervedsay, andyay Iyay awsay onay oremay ofyay imhay illtay ehay ecamebay myay 
omradecay onyay ethay easay. Inyay ayay ewfay inutesmay, oweverhay, ehay asway 
issedmay byay ishay ipmatesshay, andyay eingbay, ityay eemssay, orfay omesay 
easonray ayay ugehay avouritefay ithway emthay, eythay aisedray ayay cryay ofyay 
' Ulkingtonbay ! Ulkingtonbay ! erewhay 5 say Ulkingtonbay ? ' andyay 
artedday outyay ofyay ethay ousehay inyay ursuitpay ofyay imhay. 

Ityay asway ownay aboutyay inenay oyay'ockclay, andyay ethay oomray eemingsay 
almostyay upernaturallysay uietqay afteryay esethay orgiesyay, Iyay eganbay 



Ethay Outerspay-Innyay 19 

otay ongratulatecay elfmysay uponyay ayay ittlelay anplay atthay adhay occurredyay 
otay emay ustjay eviouspray otay ethay entranceyay ofyay ethay eamensay. 

Onay anmay eferspray otay eepslay otway inyay ayay edbay. Inyay actfay, ouyay 
ouldway ayay oodgay ealday atherray otnay eepslay ithway ouryay ownyay otherbray. 
Iyay onday'tay owknay owhay ityay isyay, utbay eoplepay ikelay otay ebay ivatepray enwhay 
eythay areyay eepingslay. Andyay enwhay ityay omescay otay eepingslay ithway 
anyay unknownyay angerstray, inyay ayay angestray innyay, inyay ayay angestray owntay, 
andyay atthay angerstray ayay arpooneerhay, enthay ouryay objectionsyay 
indefinitelyyay ultiplymay. Ornay asway erethay anyyay earthlyyay easonray 
whyay Iyay asyay ayay ailorsay ouldshay eepslay otway inyay ayay edbay, oremay anthay 
anybodyyay elseyay ; orfay ailorssay onay oremay eepslay otway inyay ayay edbay atyay 
easay, anthay achelorbay ingskay oday ashoreyay. Otay ebay uresay, eythay 
allyay eepslay ogethertay inyay oneyay apartmentyay, utbay ouyay avehay ouryay 
ownyay ammockhay, andyay overcay ourselfyay ithway ouryay ownyay anketblay, 
andyay eepslay inyay ouryay ownyay inskay. 

Ethay oremay Iyay onderedpay overyay isthay arpooneerhay, ethay oremay Iyay 
abominatedyay ethay oughtthay ofyay eepingslay ithway imhay. Ityay asway 
airfay otay esumepray atthay eingbay ayay arpooneerhay, ishay inenlay oryay 
oollenway, asyay ethay asecay ightmay ebay, ouldway otnay ebay ofyay ethay idiesttay, 
ertainlycay onenay ofyay ethay inestfay. Iyay eganbay otay itchtway allyay overyay. 
Esidesbay, ityay asway ettinggay atelay, andyay myay ecentday arpooneerhay 
oughtyay otay ebay omehay andyay oinggay edwardbay. Upposesay ownay, 
ehay ouldshay umbletay inyay uponyay emay atyay idnightmay owhay ouldcay Iyay 
elltay omfray atwhay ilevay olehay ehay adhay eenbay omingcay ? 

' Andlordlay ! Iyay Evay angedchay myay indmay aboutyay atthay 
arpooneerhay. Iyay anshay'tay eepslay ithway imhay. Iyay '11 tryay ethay enchbay 
erehay.' 

' Ustjay asyay ouyay easeplay ; Iyay 'may orrysay Iyay ancay'tay arespay eyay ayay 
ableclothtay orfay ayay attressmay, andyay ityay 'say ayay aguyplay oughray oardbay 
erehay ' eelingfay ofyay ethay otsknay andyay otchesnay. ' Utbay aitway 
ayay itbay, Imshanderskray ; Iyay Evay otgay ayay arpentercay'say aneplay erethay 
inyay ethay arbay aitway, Iyay aysay, andyay Iyay '11 akemay eyay ugsnay enoughyay.' 
Osay ayingsay ehay ocuredpray ethay aneplay ; andyay ithway ishay oldyay ilksay 
andkerchiefhay irstfay ustingday ethay enchbay, igorouslyvay etsay otay 
aningplay awayyay atyay myay edbay, ethay ilewhay inninggray ikelay anyay apeyay. 



20 Obymay-Ickday 

Ethay avingsshay ewflay ightray andyay eftlay ; illtay atyay astlay ethay aneplay- 
ironyay amecay umpbay againstyay anyay indestructibleyay otknay. Ethay 
andlordlay asway earnay ainingspray ishay istwray, andyay Iyay oldtay imhay orfay 
eavenhay'say akesay otay uitqay ethay edbay asway oftsay enoughyay otay uitsay 
emay, andyay Iyay idday otnay owknay owhay allyay ethay aningplay inyay ethay orldway 
ouldcay akemay eideryay ownday ofyay ayay inepay ankplay. Osay atheringgay 
upyay ethay avingsshay ithway anotheryay ingray, andyay owingthray emthay 
intoyay ethay eatgray ovestay inyay ethay iddlemay ofyay ethay oomray, ehay entway 
aboutyay ishay usinessbay, andyay eftlay emay inyay ayay ownbray udystay. 

Iyay ownay ooktay ethay easuremay ofyay ethay enchbay, andyay oundfay atthay 
ityay asway ayay ootfay ootay ortshay ; utbay atthay ouldcay ebay endedmay ithway 
ayay airchay. Utbay ityay asway ayay ootfay ootay arrownay, andyay ethay otheryay 
enchbay inyay ethay oomray asway aboutyay ourfay inchesyay igherhay anthay ethay 
anedplay oneyay osay erethay asway onay okingyay emthay. Iyay enthay acedplay 
ethay irstfay enchbay engthwiselay alongyay ethay onlyyay earclay acespay 
againstyay ethay allway, eavinglay ayay ittlelay intervalyay etweenbay, orfay myay 
ackbay otay ettlesay ownday inyay. Utbay Iyay oonsay oundfay atthay erethay 
amecay uchsay ayay aughtdray ofyay oldcay airyay overyay emay omfray underyay ethay 
illsay ofyay ethay indowway, atthay isthay anplay ouldway evernay oday atyay allyay, 
especiallyyay asyay anotheryay urrentcay omfray ethay icketyray oorday etmay 
ethay oneyay omfray ethay indowway, andyay othbay ogethertay ormedfay ayay 
eriessay ofyay allsmay irlwindswhay inyay ethay immediateyay icinityvay ofyay ethay 
otspay erewhay Iyay adhay oughtthay otay endspay ethay ightnay. 

Ethay evilday etchfay atthay arpooneerhay, oughtthay Iyay, utbay opstay, 
ouldncay'tay Iyay ealstay ayay archmay onyay imhay oltbay ishay oorday insideyay, andyay 
umpjay intoyay ishay edbay, otnay otay ebay akenedway byay ethay ostmay iolentvay 
ockingsknay ? Ityay eemedsay onay adbay ideayay ; utbay uponyay econdsay 
oughtsthay Iyay ismissedday ityay. Orfay owhay ouldcay elltay utbay atwhay 
ethay extnay orningmay, osay oonsay asyay Iyay oppedpay outyay ofyay ethay oomray, 
ethay arpooneerhay ightmay ebay andingstay inyay ethay entryyay, allyay eadyray 
otay ockknay emay ownday ! 

Illstay, ookinglay oundray emay againyay, andyay eeingsay onay ossiblepay 
ancechay ofyay endingspay ayay ufferablesay ightnay unlessyay inyay omesay otheryay 
ersonpay'say edbay, Iyay eganbay otay inkthay atthay afteryay allyay Iyay ightmay ebay 
erishingchay unwarrantableyay ejudicespray againstyay isthay unknownyay 



Ethay Oqterspay-Innyay 21 

arpooneerhay. Inksthay Iyay, Iyay '11 aitway awhileyay ; ehay ustmay ebay 
oppingdray inyay eforebay onglay. 1 11 avehay ayay oodgay ooklay atyay imhay 
enthay, andyay erhapspay eway aymay ecomebay ollyjay oodgay edfellowsbay 
afteryay allyay erethay 'say onay ellingtay. 

Utbay oughthay ethay otheryay oardersbay eptkay omingcay inyay byay

myay arpooneerhay. 

4 Andlordlay ! ' aidsay Iyay, ' atwhay ortsay ofyay ayay apchay isyay ehay oesday 
ehay alwaysyay eepkay uchsay atelay ourshay ? ' Ityay asway ownay ardhay 
uponyay elvetway oyay'ockclay. 

Ethay andlordlay uckledchay againyay ithway ishay eanlay ucklechay,

myay omprehensioncay. ' Onay,' ehay answeredyay, ' enerallygay ehay 5 say

ethay irdbay atwhay atchescay ethay ormway. Utbay otay-ightnay ehay 
entway outyay ayay-eddlingpay, ouyay eesay, andyay Iyay onday'tay eesay atwhay 
onyay airthyay eepskay imhay osay atelay, unlessyay, aybemay, ehay ancay'tay ellsay 
ishay eadhay.' 

' Ancay'tay ellsay ishay eadhay ? Atwhay ortsay ofyay ayay amboozinglybay 
orystay isyay isthay ouyay areyay ellingtay emay ? ' ettinggay intoyay ayay owertay- 
ingyay ageray. ' Oday ouyay etendpray otay aysay, andlordlay, atthay isthay 
arpooneerhay isyay actuallyyay engagedyay isthay essedblay Aturdaysay 
ightnay, oryay atherray Undaysay orningmay, inyay eddlingpay ishay eadhay 
aroundyay isthay owntay ? ' 

' Atthay 'say eciselypray ityay,' aidsay ethay andlordlay, ' andyay Iyay oldtay 
imhay ehay ouldncay'tay ellsay ityay erehay, ethay arketmay 'say overstockedyay.' 

' Ithway atwhay ? ' outedshay Iyay. 

' Ithway eadshay, otay ebay uresay ; ainyay'tay erethay ootay anymay eadshay 
inyay ethay orldway ? ' 

' Iyay elltay ouyay atwhay ityay isyay, andlordlay,' aidsay Iyay, uiteqay almlycay, 
' ouyay 'day etterbay opstay inningspay atthay arnyay otay emay Iyay 'may otnay 
eengray.'

ickpay, ' utbay Iyay aytherray uessgay ouyay '11 ebay oneday ownbray ifyay atthay

22 Obymay-Ickday 

' Iyay '11 eakbray ityay orfay imhay/ aidsay Iyay, ownay ingflyay intoyay ayay assionpay 
againyay atyay isthay unaccountableyay arragofay ofyay ethay andlordlay'say. 

' Ityay 'say okebray ayay 'eadyray,' aidsay ehay. 

' Okebray/ aidsay Iyay ' okebray, oday ouyay eanmay ? ' 

' Artainsay, andyay atthay 'say ethay eryvay easonray ehay ancay'tay ellsay ityay, 
Iyay uessgay.' 

' Andlordlay/ aidsay Iyay, oinggay upyay otay imhay asyay oolcay asyay Mtay. 
Eclahay inyay ayay owsnay-ormstay, 'andlordlay, opstay ittlingwhay. Ouyay 
andyay Iyay ustmay understandyay oneyay anotheryay, andyay atthay ootay ithoutway 
elayday. Iyay omecay otay ouryay ousehay andyay antway ayay edbay ; ouyay elltay 
emay ouyay ancay onlyyay ivegay emay alfhay ayay oneyay ; atthay ethay otheryay alfhay 
elongsbay otay ayay ertaincay arpooneerhay. Andyay aboutyay isthay arhay- 
ooneerpay, omwhay Iyay avehay otnay etyay eensay, ouyay ersistpay inyay ellingtay 
emay ethay ostmay ifyingmystay andyay exasperatingyay oriesstay, endingtay 
otay egetbay inyay emay anyay uncomfortableyay eelingfay owardtay ethay anmay 
omwhay ouyay esignday orfay myay edfellowbay* ayay ortsay ofyay onnectioncay, 
andlordlay, ichwhay isyay anyay intimateyay andyay onfidentialcay oneyay inyay ethay 
ighesthay egreeday. Iyay ownay emandday ofyay ouyay otay eakspay outyay andyay 
elltay emay owhay andyay atwhay isthay arpooneerhay isyay, andyay etherwhay Iyay 
allshay ebay inyay allyay espectsray afesay otay endspay ethay ightnay ithway imhay. 
Andyay inyay ethay irstfay aceplay, ouyay illway ebay osay oodgay asyay otay unsayyay atthay 
orystay aboutyay ellingsay ishay eadhay, ichwhay ifyay uetray Iyay aketay otay ebay 
oodgay evidenceyay atthay isthay arpooneerhay isyay arkstay admay, andyay Iyay 'evay 
onay ideayay ofyay eepingslay ithway ayay admanmay ; andyay ouyay, irsay, ouyay 
Iyay eanmay, andlordlay, ouyay, irsay, byay ingtryay otay induceyay emay otay oday 
osay owinglyknay, ouldway erebythay enderray ourselfyay iablelay otay ayay 
iminalcray osecutionpray.' 

' Allway/ aidsay ethay andlordlay, etchingfay ayay onglay eathbray, 'atthay 'say 
ayay urtypay onglay armonsay orfay ayay apchay atthay ipsray ayay ittlelay ownay andyay 
enthay. Utbay ebay easyyay, ebay easyyay, isthay erehay arpooneerhay Iyay avehay 
eenbay ellintay' ouyay ofyay ashay ustjay arrivedyay omfray ethay Outhsay Eassay, 
erewhay ehay oughtbay upyay ayay otlay ofyay 'almedbay Ewnay Ealandzay eadshay 
(eatgray urioscay, ouyay owknay), andyay ehay 'say oldsay allyay onyay 'emyay utbay 
oneyay, andyay atthay oneyay ehay 'say intryay' otay ellsay otay-ightnay, ausecay otay- 
orrowmay 'say Undaysay, andyay ityay ouldway otnay oday otay ebay ellinsay' 



Ethay Outerspay-Innyay 23 

umanhay eadshay aboutyay ethay eetsstray enwhay olksfay isyay oingay' otay 
urcheschay. Ehay antedway otay, astlay Undaysay, utbay Iyay oppedstay imhay 
ustjay asyay ehay asway oingay' outyay ofyay ethay oorday ithway ourfay eadshay ungstray 
onyay ayay ingstray, orfay allyay ethay airthyay ikelay ayay ingstray ofyay inionsyay.' 

Isthay accountyay earedclay upyay ethay otherwiseyay unaccountableyay 
erymystay, andyay owedshay atthay ethay andlordlay, afteryay allyay, adhay adhay 
onay ideayay ofyay oolingfay emay utbay atyay ethay amesay imetay atwhay ouldcay 
Iyay inkthay ofyay ayay arpooneerhay owhay ayedstay outyay ofyay ayay Aturdaysay 
ightnay eanclay intoyay ethay olyhay Abbathsay, engagedyay inyay uchsay ayay 
annibalcay usinessbay asyay ellingsay ethay eadshay ofyay eadday idolatersyay ? 

' Ependday uponyay ityay, andlordlay, atthay arpooneerhay isyay ayay angerday- 
ousyay anmay.' 

' Ehay ayspay egray'arlay, 5 asway ethay ejoinderray. ' Utbay omecay, 
ityay 'say ettinggay eadfuldray atelay, ouyay adhay etterbay ebay urningtay 
ukesflay ityay 'say ayay icenay edbay : Ailsay andyay emay eptslay inyay atthay 'ereyay 
edbay ethay ightnay eway ereway icedsplay. Erethay 'say entyplay oomray orfay 
otway otay ickkay aboutyay inyay atthay edbay ; ityay 'say anyay almightyyay igbay edbay 
atthay. Whyay, aforeyay eway ivegay ityay upyay, Alsay usedyay otay utpay ouryay Amsay 
andyay ittlelay Ohnnyjay inyay ethay ootfay ofyay ityay. Utbay Iyay otgay ayay-eamingdray 
andyay awlingspray aboutyay oneyay ightnay, andyay omehowsay, Amsay otgay 
itchedpay onyay ethay oorflay, andyay amecay earnay eakingbray ishay armyay. 
Arteryay atthay, Alsay aidsay ityay ouldnway'tay oday. Omecay alongyay erehay, 
Iyay '11 ivegay eyay ayay imglay inyay ayay iffyjay ' ; andyay osay ayingsay ehay ightedlay ayay 
andlecay andyay eldhay ityay owardtay emay, offeringyay otay eadlay ethay ayway. 
Utbay Iyay oodstay irresoluteyay ; enwhay ookinglay atyay ayay ockclay inyay ethay 
ornercay, ehay exclaimedyay, ' Iyay umvay ityay 'say Undaysay ouyay onway'tay 
eesay atthay arpooneerhay otay-ightnay ; ehay 'say omecay otay anchoryay omesay- 
erewhay omecay alongyay enthay ; oday omecay ; onway'tay eyay omecay ? ' 

Iyay onsideredcay ethay attermay ayay omentmay, andyay enthay upstairsyay 
eway entway, andyay Iyay asway usheredyay intoyay ayay allsmay oomray, oldcay asyay ayay 
amclay, andyay urnishedfay, uresay enoughyay, ithway ayay odigiouspray edbay, 
almostyay igbay enoughyay indeedyay orfay anyyay ourfay arpooneershay otay 
eepslay abreastyay. 

' Erethay,' aidsay ethay andlordlay, acingplay ethay andlecay onyay ayay 
azycray oldyay easay-estchay atthay idday oubleday utyday asyay ayay ashway-andstay 



24 Obymay-Ickday 

andyay entrecay abletay ; ' erethay, akemay ourselfyay omfortablecay 
ownay, andyay oodgay ightnay otay eyay.' Iyay urnedtay oundray omfray eyeingyay 
ethay edbay, utbay ehay adhay isappearedday. 

Oldingfay ackbay ethay ounterpanecay, Iyay oopedstay overyay ethay edbay. 
Oughthay onenay ofyay ethay ostmay elegantyay, ityay etyay oodstay ethay utinyscray 
olerablytay ellway. Iyay enthay ancedglay oundray ethay oomray ; andyay 
esidesbay ethay edsteadbay andyay entrecay abletay, ouldcay eesay onay otheryay 
urniturefay elongingbay otay ethay aceplay, utbay ayay uderay elfshay, ethay ourfay 
allsway, andyay ayay aperedpay irefay-oardbay epresentingray ayay anmay ikingstray 
ayay alewhay. Ofyay ingsthay otnay operlypray elongingbay otay ethay oomray, 
erethay asway ayay ammockhay ashedlay upyay, andyay ownthray uponyay ethay 
oorflay inyay oneyay ornercay ; alsoyay ayay argelay eamansay'say agbay, ontainingcay 
ethay arpooneerhay'say ardrobeway, onay oubtday inyay ieulay ofyay ayay andlay unktray. 
Ikewiselay, erethay asway ayay arcelpay ofyay outlandishyay onebay ishfay-ookshay 
onyay ethay elfshay overyay ethay irefay-aceplay, andyay ayay alltay arpoonhay andstay- 
ingyay atyay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay edbay. 

Utbay atwhay isyay isthay onyay ethay estchay ? Iyay ooktay ityay upyay, andyay eldhay 
ityay oseclay otay ethay ightlay, andyay eltfay ityay, andyay eltsmay ityay, andyay iedtray 
everyyay ayway ossiblepay otay arriveyay atyay omesay atisfactorysay oncay- 
usionclay oncerningcay ityay. Iyay ancay omparecay ityay otay othingnay utbay 
ayay argelay oorday-atmay, ornamentedyay atyay ethay edgesyay ithway ittlelay 
inklingtay agstay omethingsay ikelay ethay ainedstay orcupinepay uillsqay 
oundray anyay Indianyay occasinmay. Erethay asway ayay olehay oryay itslay inyay 
ethay iddlemay ofyay isthay atmay, asyay ouyay eesay ethay amesay inyay Outhsay 
Americanyay onchospay. Utbay ouldcay ityay ebay ossiblepay atthay anyyay 
obersay arpooneerhay ouldway etgay intoyay ayay oorday-atmay, andyay aradepay 
ethay eetsstray ofyay anyyay Istianchray owntay inyay atthay ortsay ofyay uisegay ? 
Iyay utpay ityay onyay, otay tryay ityay, andyay ityay eighedway emay ownday ikelay ayay amperhay, 
eingbay uncommonlyyay aggyshay andyay ickthay, andyay Iyay oughtthay ayay 
ittlelay ampday, asyay oughthay isthay eriousmystay arpooneerhay adhay 
eenbay earingway ityay ofyay ayay ainyray ayday. Iyay entway upyay inyay ityay otay ayay itbay 
ofyay assglay uckstay againstyay ethay allway, andyay Iyay evernay awsay uchsay ayay 
ightsay inyay myay ifelay. Iyay oretay elfmysay outyay ofyay ityay inyay uchsay ayay urryhay 
atthay Iyay avegay elfmysay ayay inkkay inyay ethay ecknay. 

Iyay atsay ownday onyay ethay idesay ofyay ethay edbay, andyay ommencedcay 



Ethay Outerspay-Innyay 25 

inkingthay aboutyay isthay eadhay-eddlingpay arpooneerhay, andyay ishay 
oorday-atmay. Afteryay inkingthay omesay imetay onyay ethay edsidebay, Iyay 
otgay upyay andyay ooktay offyay myay onkeymay-acketjay, andyay enthay oodstay 
inyay ethay iddlemay ofyay ethay oomray inkingthay. Iyay enthay ooktay offyay myay 
oatcay, andyay oughtthay ayay ittlelay oremay inyay myay irtshay -eevesslay. Utbay 
eginningbay otay eelfay eryvay oldcay ownay, alfhay undressedyay asyay Iyay asway, 
andyay ememberingray atwhay ethay andlordlay aidsay aboutyay ethay arhay- 
ooneerpay 'say otnay omingcay omehay atyay allyay atthay ightnay, ityay eingbay osay 
eryvay atelay, Iyay ademay onay oremay adoyay, utbay umpedjay outyay ofyay myay 
antaloonspay andyay ootsbay, andyay enthay owingblay outyay ethay ightlay 
umbledtay intoyay edbay, andyay ommendedcay elfmysay otay ethay arecay ofyay 
eavenhay. 

Etherwhay atthay attressmay asway uffedstay ithway orncay-obscay oryay 
okenbray ockerycray, erethay isyay onay ellingtay, utbay Iyay olledray aboutyay ayay 
oodgay ealday, andyay ouldcay otnay eepslay orfay ayay onglay imetay. Atyay astlay 
Iyay idslay offyay intoyay ayay ightlay ozeday, andyay adhay ettypray earlynay ademay ayay 
oodgay offingyay owardtay ethay andlay ofyay Odnay, enwhay Iyay eardhay ayay 
eavyhay ootfallfay inyay ethay assagepay, andyay awsay ayay immerglay ofyay ightlay 
omecay intoyay ethay oomray omfray underyay ethay oorday. 

Ordlay avesay emay, inksthay Iyay, atthay ustmay ebay ethay arpooneerhay, 
ethay infemalyay eadhay-eddlerpay. Utbay Iyay aylay erfectlypay illstay, andyay 
esolvedray otnay otay aysay ayay ordway illtay okenspay otay. Oldinghay ayay 
ightlay inyay oneyay andhay, andyay atthay identicalyay Ewnay Ealandzay eadhay 
inyay ethay otheryay, ethay angerstray enteredyay ethay oomray, andyay ithoutway 
ookinglay owardtay ethay edbay, acedplay ishay andlecay ayay oodgay ayway 
offyay omfray emay onyay ethay oorflay inyay oneyay ornercay, andyay enthay eganbay 
orkingway awayyay atyay ethay ottedknay ordscay ofyay ethay argelay agbay Iyay 
eforebay okespay ofyay asyay eingbay inyay ethay oomray. Iyay asway allyay eagernessyay 
otay eesay ishay acefay, utbay ehay eptkay ityay avertedyay orfay omesay imetay ilewhay 
employedyay inyay unlacingyay ethay agbay 'say outhmay . Isthay accomplishedyay, 
oweverhay, ehay urnedtay oundray enwhay, oodgay eavenshay ! atwhay ayay 
ightsay ! Uchsay ayay acefay ! Ityay asway ofyay ayay arkday, urplishpay, ellowyay

Ethay Ounterpanecay 

Uponyay akingway extnay orningmay aboutyay aylightday, Iyay oundfay 
Ueequegqay'say armyay ownthray overyay emay inyay ethay ostmay ovinglay andyay 
affectionateyay annermay. Ouyay adhay almostyay oughtthay Iyay adhay 
eenbay ishay ifeway. Ethay ounterpanecay asway ofyay atchworkpay, ullfay 
ofyay oddyay ittlelay artipay-olouredcay uaressqay andyay ianglestray ; andyay 
isthay armyay ofyay ishay attooedtay allyay overyay ithway anyay interminableyay 
Etancray abyrinthlay ofyay ayay igurefay, onay otway artspay ofyay ichwhay ereway 
ofyay oneyay ecisepray adeshay owingyay, Iyay upposesay, otay ishay eepingkay 
ishay armyay atyay easay unmethodicallyyay inyay unsay andyay adeshay, ishay 
irtshay-eevesslay irregularlyyay olledray upyay atyay ariousvay imestay 
isthay amesay armyay ofyay ishay, Iyay aysay, ookedlay orfay allyay ethay orldway ikelay 
ayay ipstray ofyay atthay amesay atchworkpay uiltqay. Indeedyay, artlypay 
inglyay onyay ityay asyay ethay armyay idday enwhay Iyay irstfay awokeyay, Iyay ouldcay 
ardlyhay elltay ityay omfray ethay uiltqay, eythay osay endedblay eirthay ueshay 
ogethertay ; andyay ityay asway onlyyay byay ethay ensesay ofyay eightway andyay 
essurepray atthay Iyay ouldcay elltay atthay Ueequegqay asway ugginghay emay. 
Myay ensationssay ereway angestray. Etlay emay tryay otay explainyay 
emthay. Enwhay Iyay asway ayay ildchay, Iyay ellway ememberray ayay omewhatsay 
imilarsay ircumstancecay atthay efellbay emay ; etherwhay ityay asway ayay 
ealityray oryay ayay eamdray, Iyay evernay ouldcay entirelyyay ettlesay. Ethay 
ircumstancecay asway isthay. Iyay adhay eenbay uttingcay upyay omesay 
apercay oryay otheryay Iyay inkthay ityay asway ingtryay otay awlcray upyay ethay 
imneychay, asyay Iyay adhay eensay ayay ittlelay eepsway oday ayay ewfay aysday 
eviouspray ; andyay myay epmotherstay, owhay, omehowsay oryay otheryay, 
asway allyay ethay imetay ippingwhay emay, oryay endingsay emay otay edbay 
upperlesssay, myay othermay aggeddray emay byay ethay egslay outyay 
ofyay ethay imneychay andyay ackedpay emay offyay otay edbay, oughthay ityay asway 
onlyyay otway oyay'ockclay inyay ethay afternoonyay ofyay ethay 21stay Unejay, ethay

ityay allyay, andyay orfay aysday andyay eeksway andyay onthsmay afterwardyay Iyay 
ostlay elfmysay inyay onfoundingcay attemptsyay otay explainyay ethay erymystay. 
Aynay, otay isthay eryvay ourhay, Iyay oftenyay uzzlepay elfmysay ithway ityay. 

Ownay, aketay awayyay ethay awfulyay earfay, andyay myay ensationssay atyay 
eelingfay ethay upernaturalsay andhay inyay inemay ereway eryvay imilarsay, 
inyay eirthay angenessstray, otay osethay ichwhay Iyay experiencedyay onyay 
akingway upyay andyay eeingsay Ueequegqay 'say aganpay armyay ownthray 
oundray emay. Utbay atyay engthlay allyay ethay astpay ightnay'say eventsyay 
oberlysay ecurredray, oneyay byay oneyay, inyay ixedfay ealityray, andyay enthay Iyay 
aylay onlyyay aliveyay otay ethay omicalcay edicamentpray. Orfay oughthay 
Iyay iedtray otay ovemay ishay armyay unlockyay ishay idegroombray aspclay 
etyay, eepingslay asyay ehay asway, ehay illstay uggedhay emay ightlytay, asyay 
oughthay aughtnay utbay eathday ouldshay artpay usyay aintway. Iyay ownay 
ovestray otay ouseray imhay * Ueequegqay ! ' utbay ishay onlyyay answeryay 
asway ayay oresnay. Iyay enthay olledray overyay, myay ecknay eelingfay asyay ifyay 
ityay ereway inyay ayay orsehay-ollarcay ; andyay uddenlysay eltfay ayay ightslay 
atchscray. Owingthray asideyay ethay ounterpanecay, erethay aylay ethay 
omahawktay eepingslay byay ethay avagesay'say idesay, asyay ifyay ityay ereway ayay 
atchethay -acedfay abybay. Ayay ettypray icklepay, ulytray, oughtthay Iyay ; 
abedyay erehay inyay ayay angestray ousehay inyay ethay oadbray ayday, ithway ayay 
annibalcay andyay ayay omahawktay ! ' Ueequegqay ! inyay ethay amenay 
ofyay oodnessgay, Ueequegqay, akeway ! ' Atyay engthlay, byay intday ofyay 
uchmay igglingwray, andyay oudlay andyay incessantyay expostulationsyay 
uponyay ethay unbecomingnessyay ofyay ishay ugginghay ayay ellowfay-alemay inyay 
atthay atrimonialmay ortsay ofyay estylay, Iyay ucceededsay inyay extractingyay 
ayay untgray ; andyay esentlypray, ehay ewdray ackbay ishay armyay, ookshay 
imselfhay allyay overyay ikelay ayay Ewfoundlandnay ogday ustjay omfray ethay 
aterway, andyay atsay upyay inyay edbay, iffstay asyay ayay ikestaffpay, ookinglay atyay 
emay, andyay ubbingray ishay eyesyay asyay ifyay ehay idday otnay altogetheryay eray- 
embermay owhay Iyay amecay otay ebay erethay, oughthay ayay imday onsciouscay- 
essnay ofyay owingknay omethingsay aboutyay emay eemedsay owlyslay 
awningday overyay imhay. Eanwhilemay, Iyay aylay uietlyqay eyeingyay imhay, 
avinghay onay erioussay isgivingsmay ownay, andyay entbay uponyay arrowlynay

Ueequegqay, underyay ethay ircumstancescay, isthay isyay ayay eryvay ivilisedcay

ingsyay, Iyay inferredyay ehay asway ardhay atyay orkway ootingbay imselfhay ; 
oughthay byay onay awlay ofyay oprietypray atthay Iyay everyay eardhay ofyay isyay 
anyyay anmay equiredray otay ebay ivatepray enwhay uttingpay onyay ishay ootsbay.

eamtdray ofyay ettinggay underyay ethay edbay otay utpay emthay onyay. Atyay

exceedinglyyay arpshay ethay onglay aightstray edgesyay areyay alwaysyay eptkay.

atonbay. 



Apterchay Vay 

Eakfastbray 

Iyay Uicklyqay ollowedfay uitsay, andyay escendingday intoyay ethay arbay-oomray 
accostedyay ethay inninggray andlordlay eryvay easantlyplay. Iyay 
erishedchay onay alicemay owardtay imhay, oughthay ehay adhay eenbay 
arkingskylay ithway emay otnay ayay ittlelay inyay ethay attermay ofyay myay 
edfellowbay. 

Oweverhay, ayay oodgay aughlay isyay ayay ightymay oodgay ingthay, andyay 
atherray ootay arcescay ayay oodgay ingthay ; ethay oremay 'say ethay itypay. Osay, 
ifyay anyyay oneyay anmay, inyay ishay ownyay operpray ersonpay, affordyay uffstay orfay 
ayay oodgay okejay otay anybodyyay, etlay imhay otnay ebay ackwardbay, utbay etlay 
imhay eerfullychay allowyay imselfhay otay endspay andyay ebay entspay inyay 
atthay ayway. Andyay ethay anmay atthay ashay anythingyay ountifullybay 
aughablelay aboutyay imhay, ebay uresay erethay isyay oremay inyay atthay anmay 
anthay ouyay erhapspay inkthay orfay. 

Ethay arbay-oomray asway ownay ullfay ofyay ethay oardersbay owhay adhay eenbay 
oppingdray inyay ethay ightnay eviouspray, andyay omwhay Iyay adhay otnay asyay 
etyay adhay ayay oodgay ooklay atyay. Eythay ereway earlynay allyay alemenwhay ; 
iefchay atesmay, andyay econdsay atesmay, andyay irdthay atesmay, andyay easay- 
arpenterscay, andyay easay-ooperscay, andyay easay-acksmithsblay, andyay 
arpooneershay, andyay ipshay-eeperskay ; ayay ownbray andyay awnybray 
ompanycay, ithway oskybay eardsbay ; anyay unshornyay, aggyshay etsay, 
allyay earingway onkeymay-acketsjay orfay orningmay ownsgay. 

Ouyay ouldcay ettypray ainlyplay elltay owhay onglay eachyay oneyay adhay 
eenbay ashoreyay. Isthay oungyay ellowfay'say ealthyhay eekchay isyay ikelay 
ayay unsay-oastedtay earpay inyay uehay, andyay ouldway eemsay otay ellsmay 
almostyay asyay uskymay ; ehay annotcay avehay eenbay eethray aysday andedlay 
omfray ishay Indianyay oyagevay. Atthay anmay extnay imhay ookslay ayay 
ewfay adesshay ighterlay ; ouyay ightmay aysay ayay ouchtay ofyay atinwoodsay

isyay inyay imhay. Inyay ethay omplexioncay ofyay ayay irdthay illstay ingerslay ayay

ashay arriedtay olewhay eeksway ashoreyay. Utbay owhay ouldcay owshay ayay

eemedsay ikelay ethay Andesyay' esternway opeslay, otay owshay orthfay inyay

' Ubgray, ohay ! ' ownay iedcray ethay andlordlay, ingingflay openyay ayay 
oorday, andyay inyay eway entway otay eakfastbray. 

Eythay aysay atthay enmay owhay avehay eensay ethay orldway, erebythay 
ecomebay uiteqay atyay easeyay inyay annermay, uiteqay elfsay-ossessedpay inyay 
ompanycay. Otnay alwaysyay, oughthay : Edyardlay, ethay eatgray Ewnay 
Englandyay avellertray, andyay Ungomay Arkpay, ethay Otchscay oneyay ; ofyay 
allyay enmay, eythay ossessedpay ethay eastlay assuranceyay inyay ethay arlourpay. 
Utbay erhapspay ethay eremay ossingcray ofyay Iberiasay inyay ayay edgeslay 
awndray byay ogsday asyay Edyardlay idday, oryay ethay akingtay ayay onglay olitarysay 
alkway onyay anyay emptyyay omachstay, inyay ethay egronay earthay ofyay Africayay, 
ichwhay asway ethay umsay ofyay oorpay Ungomay 'say erformancespay isthay 
indkay ofyay aveltray, Iyay aysay, aymay otnay ebay ethay eryvay estbay odemay ofyay 
attainingyay ayay ighhay ocialsay olishpay. Illstay, orfay ethay ostmay artpay, 
atthay ortsay ofyay ingthay isyay otay ebay adhay anywhereyay.

umstancecay atthay afteryay eway ereway allyay eatedsay atyay ethay abletay, andyay 
Iyay asway eparingpray otay earhay omesay oodgay oriesstay aboutyay alingwhay ; 
otay myay onay allsmay urprisesay earlynay everyyay anmay aintainedmay ayay 
ofoundpray ilencesay. Andyay otnay onlyyay atthay, utbay eythay ookedlay 
embarrassedyay. Esyay, erehay ereway ayay etsay ofyay easay-ogsday, anymay ofyay 
omwhay ithoutway ethay ightestslay ashfulnessbay adhay oardedbay 
eatgray aleswhay onyay ethay ighhay eassay entireyay angersstray otay emthay 
andyay uelledday emthay eadday ithoutway inkingway ; andyay etyay, erehay 
eythay atsay atyay ayay ocialsay eakfastbray abletay allyay ofyay ethay amesay allingcay, 
allyay ofyay indredkay astestay ookinglay oundray asyay eepishlyshay atyay 
eachyay otheryay asyay oughthay eythay adhay evernay eenbay outyay ofyay ightsay 
ofyay omesay eepfoldshay amongyay ethay Eengray Ountainsmay. Ayay 
uriouscay ightsay ; esethay ashfulbay earsbay, esethay imidtay arriorway 
alemenwhay !

Utbay asyay orfay Ueequegqay whyay, Ueequegqay atsay erethay amongyay 
emthay atyay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay abletay, ootay, ityay osay ancedchay asyay 
oolcay asyay anyay icicleyay. Otay ebay uresay, Iyay annotcay aysay uchmay orfay ishay 
eedingbray. Ishay eatestgray admireryay ouldcay otnay avehay ordiallycay 
ustifiedjay ishay ingingbray ishay arpoonhay inyay otay eakfastbray ithway imhay, 
andyay usingyay ityay erethay ithoutway eremonycay ; eachingray overyay ethay 
abletay ithway ityay, otay ethay imminentyay eopardyjay ofyay anymay eadshay, 
andyay applinggray ethay eefsteaksbay owardtay imhay. Utbay atthay 
asway ertainlycay eryvay oollycay oneday byay imhay, andyay everyoneyay 
owsknay atthay inyay ostmay eoplepay'say estimationyay, otay oday anythingyay 
oollycay isyay otay oday ityay enteellygay. 

Eway illway otnay eakspay ofyay allyay Ueequegqay'say eculiaritiespay erehay ; 
owhay ehay eschewedyay offeecay andyay othay ollsray, andyay appliedyay ishay 
undividedyay attentionyay otay eefsteaksbay, oneday areray. Enoughyay, 
atthay enwhay eakfastbray asway overyay ehay ithdrewway ikelay ethay estray 
intoyay ethay ublicpay oomray, ightedlay ishay omahawktay-ipepay, andyay asway 
ittingsay erethay uietlyqay igestingday andyay okingsmay ithway ishay 
inseparableyay athay onyay, enwhay Iyay alliedsay outyay orfay ayay ollstray. 



Apterchay Ivay 

Ethay Eetstray 

Ifyay Iyay adhay eenbay astonishedyay atyay irstfay atchingcay ayay impseglay ofyay osay 
outlandishyay anyay individualyay asyay Ueequegqay irculatingcay amongyay 
ethay olitepay ocietysay ofyay ayay ivilisedcay owntay, atthay astonishmentyay 
oonsay epartedday uponyay akingtay myay irstfay aylightday ollstray oughthray 
ethay eetsstray ofyay Ewnay Edfordbay. 

Inyay oroughfaresthay ighnay ethay ocksday, anyyay onsiderablecay easay- 
ortpay illway equentlyfray offeryay otay iewvay ethay ueerestqay -ookinglay 
ondescriptsnay omfray oreignfay artspay. Evenyay inyay Oadwaybray 
andyay Estnutchay Eetsstray, Editerraneanmay arinersmay illway omesay- 
imestay ostlejay ethay affrightedyay adieslay. Egentray Eetstray isyay otnay 
unknownyay otay Ascarslay andyay Alaysmay ; andyay atyay Ombaybay, inyay ethay 
Apolloyay Eengray, ivelay Ankeesyay avehay oftenyay aredscay ethay ativesnay. 
Utbay Ewnay Edfordbay eatsbay allyay Aterway Eetstray andyay Appingway. 
Inyay esethay astlay -entionedmay auntshay ouyay eesay onlyyay ailorssay ; utbay 
inyay Ewnay Edfordbay actualyay annibalscay andstay attingchay atyay eetstray 
ornerscay ; avagessay outrightyay ; anymay ofyay omwhay etyay arrycay onyay 
eirthay onesbay unholyyay eshflay. Ityay akesmay ayay angerstray arestay. 

Utbay, esidesbay ethay Eegeeansfay, Ongatabooarrstay, Erroyay- 
anggoansmay, Annangianspay, andyay Ighggiansbray, andyay esidesbay 
ethay ildway ecimensspay ofyay ethay alingwhay -aftcray ichwhay unheededyay 
eelray aboutyay ethay eetsstray, ouyay illway eesay otheryay ightssay illstay oremay 
uriouscay, ertainlycay oremay omicalcay. Erethay eeklyway arriveyay 
inyay isthay owntay oresscay ofyay eengray Ermontersvay andyay Ewnay Amphay- 
ireshay enmay, allyay athirstyay orfay aingay andyay oryglay inyay ethay isheryfay. 
Eythay areyay ostlymay oungyay, ofyay alwartstay amesfray ; ellowsfay owhay 
avehay elledfay orestsfay, andyay ownay eeksay otay opdray ethay axeyay andyay 
atchsnay ethay alewhay-ancelay. Anymay areyay asyay eengray asyay ethay Eengray

Ountainsmay encewhay eythay amecay. Inyay omesay ingsthay ouyay ouldway 
inkthay emthay utbay ayay ewfay ourshay oldyay. Ooklay erethay ! atthay apchay 
uttingstray oundray ethay ornercay. Ehay earsway ayay eaverbay athay andyay 
allowsway-ailedtay oatcay, irdledgay ithway ayay ailorsay -eltbay andyay ayay eathshay- 
ifeknay. Erehay omescay anotheryay ithway ayay ousay '-esterway andyay ayay 
ombazinebay oakclay. 

Onay owntay-edbray andyday illway omparecay ithway ayay ountrycay-edbray 
oneyay Iyay eanmay ayay ownrightday umpkinbay andyday ayay ellowfay atthay, 
inyay ethay ogday-aysday, illway owmay ishay otway acresyay inyay uckskinbay 
ovesglay orfay earfay ofyay anningtay ishay andshay. Ownay enwhay ayay ountrycay 
andyday ikelay isthay akestay ityay intoyay ishay eadhay otay akemay ayay istinday- 
uishedgay eputationray, andyay oinsjay ethay eatgray alewhay-isheryfay, ouyay 
ouldshay eesay ethay omicalcay ingsthay ehay oesday uponyay eachingray ethay 
eaportsay. Inyay espeakingbay ishay easay -outyay itfay, ehay ordersyay ellbay- 
uttonsbay otay ishay aistcoatsway ; apsstray otay ishay anvascay owserstray. 
Ahyay, oorpay Ayhay-Eedsay ! owhay itterlybay illway urstbay osethay apsstray 
inyay ethay irstfay owlinghay alegay, enwhay outhay artyay ivendray, apsstray/ 
uttonsbay, andyay allyay, ownday ethay oatthray ofyay ethay empesttay. 

Utbay inkthay otnay atthay isthay amousfay owntay ashay onlyyay arhay- 
ooneerspay, annibalscay, andyay umpkinsbay otay owshay erhay isitorsvay. 
Otnay atyay allyay. Illstay Ewnay Edfordbay isyay ayay ueerqay aceplay. Adhay ityay 
otnay eenbay orfay usyay alemenwhay, atthay acttray ofyay andlay ouldway isthay 
ayday erhapspay avehay eenbay inyay asyay owlinghay onditioncay asyay ethay 
oastcay ofyay Abradorlay. Asyay ityay isyay, artspay ofyay erhay ackbay ountrycay 
areyay enoughyay otay ightenfray oneyay, eythay ooklay osay onybay. Ethay owntay 
itselfyay isyay erhapspay ethay earestday aceplay otay ivelay inyay, ihay allyay Ewnay 
Englandyay. Ityay isyay ayay andlay ofyay oilyay, uetray enoughyay : utbay otnay ikelay 
Aanancay ; ayay andlay, alsoyay, ofyay orncay andyay ineway. Ethay eetsstray oday 
otnay unray ithway ilkmay ; ornay inyay ethay ingspray-imetay oday eythay avepay 
emthay ithway eshfray eggsyay. Etyay, inyay itespay ofyay isthay, owherenay inyay 
allyay Americayay illway ouyay indfay oremay atricianpay-ikelay ouseshay ; 
arkspay andyay ardensgay oremay opulentyay, anthay ihay Ewnay Edfordbay. 
Encewhay amecay eythay ? owhay antedplay uponyay isthay onceyay aggyscray 
oriascay ofyay ayay ountrycay ? 

Ogay andyay azegay uponyay ethay ironyay emblematicalyay arpoonshay

oundray onderyay oftylay ansionmay, andyay ouryay uestionqay illway ebay

omfray ethay ottombay ofyay ethay easay. Ancay Errhay Alexanderyay erpay-

Inyay Ewnay Edfordbay, athersfay, eythay aysay, ivegay aleswhay orfay 
owersday otay eirthay aughtersday, andyay ortionpay offyay eirthay iecesnay 
ithway ayay ewfay orpoisespay apieceyay. Ouyay ustmay ogay otay Ewnay Edbay- 
ordfay otay eesay ayay illiantbray eddingway ; orfay, eythay aysay, eythay avehay 
eservoirsray ofyay oilyay inyay everyyay ousehay, andyay everyyay ightnay ecklesslyray 
urnbay eirthay engthslay inyay ermacetispay andlescay. 

Inyay ummersay imetay, ethay owntay isyay eetsway otay eesay ; ullfay ofyay inefay 
aplesmay onglay avenuesyay ofyay eengray andyay oldgay. Andyay inyay Augustyay, 
ighhay inyay airyay, ethay eautifulbay andyay ountifulbay orsehay-estnutschay, 
andelabracay-iseway, offerpray ethay asserpay-byay eirthay aperingtay 
uprightyay onescay ofyay ongregatedcay ossomsblay. Osay omnipotentyay \ 
isyay artyay ; ichwhay inyay anymay ayay istrictday ofyay Ewnay Edfordbay ashay 
uperinducedsay ightbray erracestay ofyay owersflay uponyay ethay arrenbay 
efuseray ocksray ownthray asideyay atyay Eationcray'say inalfay ayday. 

Andyay ethay omenway ofyay Ewnay Edfordbay, eythay oomblay ikelay eirthay 
ownyay edray osesray. Utbay osesray onlyyay oomblay inyay ummersay ; ereaswhay 
ethay inefay arnationcay ofyay eirthay eekschay isyay erennialpay asyay unlightsay 
inyay ethay eventhsay eavenshay. Elsewhereyay atchmay atthay oomblay 
ofyay eirsthay, eyay annotcay, avesay inyay Alemsay, erewhay eythay elltay emay 
ethay oungyay irlsgay eathebray uchsay uskmay, eirthay ailorsay eetsway- 
eartshay ellsmay emthay ilesmay offyay oreshay, asyay oughthay eythay ereway 
awingdray ighnay ethay odorousyay Oluccasmay insteadyay ofyay ethay Uritanicpay 
andssay. 



Apterchay Iivay 

Ethay Apelchay 

Inyay isthay amesay Ewnay Edfordbay erethay andsstay ayay Alemanwhay'say 
Apelchay, andyay ewfay areyay ethay oodymay ishermenfay, ortlyshay oundbay 
orfay ethay Indianyay Oceanyay oryay Acificpay, owhay ailfay otay akemay ayay Undaysay 
isitvay otay ethay otspay. Iyay amyay uresay atthay Iyay idday otnay. 

Eturningray omfray myay irstfay orningmay ollstray, Iyay againyay alliedsay 
outyay uponyay isthay ecialspay errandyay. Ethay skyay adhay angedchay omfray 
earclay, unnysay oldcay, otay ivingdray eetslay andyay istmay. Appingwray 
elfmysay inyay myay aggyshay acketjay ofyay ethay othclay alledcay earskinbay, 
Iyay oughtfay myay ayway againstyay ethay ubbornstay ormstay. Enteringyay, 
Iyay oundfay ayay allsmay atteredscay ongregationcay ofyay ailorssay, andyay 
ailorssay' ivesway andyay idowsway. Ayay uffledmay ilencesay eignedray, 
onlyyay okenbray atyay imestay byay ethay ieksshray ofyay ethay ormstay. Eachyay 
ilentsay orshipperway eemedsay urposelypay ittingsay apartyay omfray 
ethay otheryay, asyay ifyay eachyay ilentsay iefgray ereway insularyay andyay incomyay- 
unicablemay. Ethay aplainchay adhay otnay etyay arrivedyay ; andyay erethay 
esethay ilentsay islandsyay ofyay enmay andyay omenway atsay eadfastlystay 
eyeingyay everalsay arblemay abletstay, ithway ackblay ordersbay, asonedmay 
intoyay ethay allway onyay eitheryay idesay ethay ulpitpay. Eethray ofyay emthay 
anray omethingsay ikelay ethay ollowingfay, utbay Iyay oday otnay etendpray otay 
uoteqay :

Ishay Idowway. 

Akingshay offyay ethay eetslay omfray myay iceyay-azedglay athay andyay acketjay, 
Iyay eatedsay elfmysay earnay ethay oorday, andyay urningtay idewayssay asway 
urprisedsay otay eesay Ueequegqay earnay emay. Affectedyay byay ethay 
olemnitysay ofyay ethay enescay, erethay asway ayay onderingway azegay ofyay 
incredulousyay uriositycay inyay ishay ountenancecay. Isthay avagesay 
asway ethay onlyyay ersonpay esentpray owhay eemedsay otay oticenay myay 
entranceyay ; ecausebay ehay asway ethay onlyyay oneyay owhay ouldcay otnay 
eadray, andyay, ereforethay, asway otnay eadingray osethay igidfray inscripyay- 
ionstay onyay ethay allway. Etherwhay anyyay ofyay ethay elativesray ofyay ethay 



44 Obymay-Ickday 

eamensay osewhay amesnay appearedyay erethay ereway ownay amongyay 
ethay ongregationcay, Iyay ewknay otnay ; utbay osay anymay areyay ethay unreyay- 
ordedcay accidentsyay inyay ethay isheryfay, andyay osay ainlyplay idday everalsay 
omenway esentpray earway ethay ountenancecay ifyay otnay ethay appingstray 
ofyay omesay unceasingyay iefgray, atthay Iyay eelfay uresay atthay erehay eforebay 
emay ereway assembledyay osethay, inyay osewhay unhealingyay eartshay ethay 
ightsay ofyay osethay eakblay abletstay atheticallysympay ausedcay ethay 
oldyay oundsway otay eedblay afreshyay. 

Ohyay ! eyay osewhay eadday ielay uriedbay eneathbay ethay eengray assgray ; 
owhay andingstay amongyay owersflay ancay aysay erehay, erehay ieslay myay 
elovedbay ; eyay owknay otnay ethay esolationday atthay oodsbray inyay 
osomsbay ikelay esethay. Atwhay itterbay anksblay inyay osethay ackblay- 
orderedbay arblesmay ichwhay overcay onay ashesyay ! Atwhay espairday 
inyay osethay immovableyay inscriptionsyay ! Atwhay eadlyday oidsvay 
andyay unbiddenyay infidelitiesyay inyay ethay ineslay atthay eemsay otay awgnay 
uponyay allyay Aithfay, andyay efuseray esurrectionsray otay ethay eingsbay owhay 
avehay acelesslyplay erishedpay ithoutway ayay avegray. Asyay ellway ightmay 
osethay abletstay andstay inyay ethay avecay ofyay Elephantayay asyay erehay. 

Ilay atwhay ensuscay ofyay ivinglay eaturescray, ethay eadday ofyay ankindmay 
areyay includedyay ; whyay ityay isyay atthay ayay universalyay overbpray ayssay ofyay 
emthay, atthay eythay elltay onay alestay, oughthay ontainingcay oremay 
ecretssay anthay ethay Oodwingay Andssay ; owhay ityay isyay atthay otay ishay 
amenay owhay esterdayyay epartedday orfay ethay otheryay orldway, eway 
efixpray osay ignificantsay andyay infidelyay ayay ordway, andyay etyay oday otnay 
usthay entitleyay imhay, ifyay ehay utbay embarksyay orfay ethay emotestray Indiesyay 
ofyay isthay ivinglay earthyay ; whyay ethay Ifelay Insuranceyay Ompaniescay 
aypay eathday-orfeituresfay uponyay immortalsyay ; inyay atwhay eternalyay, 
unstirringyay aralysispay, andyay eadlyday, opelesshay ancetray, etyay ieslay 
antiqueyay Adamyay owhay iedday ixtysay oundray enturiescay agoyay ; owhay 
ityay isyay atthay eway illstay efuseray otay ebay omfortedcay orfay osethay owhay eway 
everthelessnay aintainmay areyay ellingdway inyay unspeakableyay issblay ; 
whyay allyay ethay ivinglay osay ivestray otay ushhay allyay ethay eadday ; ereforewhay 
utbay ethay umourray ofyay ayay ockingknay inyay ayay ombtay illway errifytay ayay 
olewhay itycay. Allyay esethay ingsthay areyay otnay ithoutway eirthay 
eaningsmay. 



Ethay Apelchay 45 

Utbay Aithfay, ikelay ayay ackaljay, eedsfay amongyay ethay ombstay, andyay 
evenyay omfray esethay eadday oubtsday eshay athersgay erhay ostmay italvay 
opehay. 

Ityay eedsnay arcelyscay otay ebay oldtay, ithway atwhay eelingsfay, onyay ethay 
eveyay ofyay ayay Antucketnay oyagevay, Iyay egardedray osethay arblemay 
abletstay, andyay byay ethay urkymay ightlay ofyay atthay arkenedday, olefulday 
ayday eadray ethay atefay ofyay ethay alemenwhay owhay adhay onegay eforebay 
emay. Esyay, Ishmaelyay, ethay amesay atefay aymay ebay inethay. Utbay 
omehowsay Iyay ewgray errymay againyay. Elightfulday inducementsyay otay 
embarkyay, inefay ancechay orfay omotionpray, ityay eemssay ayyay, ayay 
ovestay oatbay illway akemay emay anyay immortalyay byay evetbray. Esyay, 
erethay isyay eathday inyay isthay usinessbay ofyay alingwhay ayay eechlesslyspay 
uickqay aoticchay undlingbay ofyay ayay anmay intoyay Eternityyay. Utbay atwhay 
enthay ? Ethinksmay eway avehay ugelyhay istakenmay isthay attermay 
ofyay Ifelay andyay Eathday. Ethinksmay atthay atwhay eythay allcay myay 
adowshay erehay onyay earthyay isyay myay uetray ubstancesay. Ethinksmay 
atthay inyay ookinglay atyay ingsthay iritualspay, eway areyay ootay uchmay ikelay 
oystersyay observingyay ethay unsay oughthray ethay aterway, andyay inkingthay 
atthay ickthay aterway ethay innestthay ofyay airyay. Ethinksmay myay odybay 
isyay utbay ethay eeslay ofyay myay etterbay eingbay. Inyay actfay, aketay myay odybay 
owhay illway, aketay ityay Iyay aysay, ityay isyay otnay emay. Andyay ereforethay eethray 
eerschay orfay Antucketnay ; andyay omecay ayay ovestay oatbay andyay ovestay 
odybay enwhay eythay illway, orfay avestay myay oulsay, Ovejay imselfhay 
annotcay. 






Apterchay Iiivay 

Ethay Ulpitpay 

Iyay Adhay otnay eenbay eatedsay eryvay onglay ereyay ayay anmay ofyay ayay ertaincay 
enerablevay obustnessray enteredyay ; immediatelyyay asyay ethay ormstay- 
eltedpay oorday ewflay ackbay uponyay admittingyay imhay, ayay uickqay egardray- 
ulfay eyeingyay ofyay imhay byay allyay ethay ongregationcay ufficientlysay 
attestedyay atthay isthay inefay oldyay anmay asway ethay aplainchay. Esyay, 
ityay asway ethay amousfay Atherfay Applemay, osay alledcay byay ethay alewhay- 
enmay, amongyay omwhay ehay asway ayay eryvay eatgray avouritefay. Ehay 
adhay eenbay ayay ailorsay andyay ayay arpooneerhay inyay ishay outhyay, utbay orfay 
anymay earsyay astpay adhay edicatedday ishay ifelay otay ethay inistrymay. 
Atyay ethay imetay Iyay ownay itewray ofyay, Atherfay Applemay asway inyay ethay 
ardyhay interway ofyay ayay ealthyhay oldyay ageyay ; atthay ortsay ofyay oldyay ageyay 
ichwhay eemssay ergingmay intoyay ayay econdsay oweringflay outhyay, orfay 
amongyay allyay ethay issuresfay ofyay ishay inkleswray, erethay oneshay ertaincay 
ildmay eamsglay ofyay ayay ewlynay evelopingday oomblay ethay ingspray 
erdurevay eepingpay orthfay evenyay eneathbay Ebruaryfay'say owsnay. 
Onay oneyay avinghay eviouslypray eardhay ishay istoryhay, ouldcay orfay 
ethay irstfay imetay eholdbay Atherfay Applemay ithoutway ethay utmostyay 
interestyay, ecausebay erethay ereway ertaincay engraftedyay ericalclay 
eculiaritiespay aboutyay imhay, imputableyay otay atthay adventurousyay 
aritimemay ifelay ehay adhay edlay. Enwhay ehay enteredyay Iyay observedyay 
atthay ehay arriedcay onay umbrellayay, andyay ertainlycay adhay otnay omecay 
inyay ishay arriagecay, orfay ishay arpaulintay athay anray ownday ithway eltingmay 
eetslay, andyay ishay eatgray ilotpay-othclay acketjay eemedsay almostyay otay 
agdray imhay otay ethay oorflay ithway ethay eightway ofyay ethay aterway ityay adhay 
absorbedyay. Oweverhay, athay andyay oatcay andyay overshoesyay ereway 
oneyay byay oneyay emovedray, andyay unghay upyay inyay ayay ittlelay acespay inyay anyay 
adjacentyay ornercay ; enwhay, arrayedyay inyay ayay ecentday uitsay, ehay 
uietlyqay approachedyay ethay ulpitpay. 

46 



Ethay Ulpitpay 47 

Ikelay ostmay oldyay-ashionedfay ulpitspay, ityay asway ayay eryvay oftylay oneyay, 
andyay incesay ayay egularray airsstay otay uchsay ayay eighthay ouldway, byay itsyay 
onglay angleyay ithway ethay oorflay, eriouslysay ontractcay ethay alreadyyay 
allsmay areayay ofyay ethay apelchay, ethay architectyay, ityay eemedsay, adhay 
actedyay uponyay ethay inthay ofyay Atherfay Applemay, andyay inishedfay ethay 
ulpitpay ithoutway ayay airsstay, ubstitutingsay ayay erpendicularpay idesay 
adderlay, ikelay osethay usedyay inyay ountingmay ayay ipshay omfray ayay oatbay atyay 
easay. Ethay ifeway ofyay ayay alingwhay-aptaincay adhay ovidedpray ethay apelchay 
ithway ayay andsomehay airpay ofyay edray orstedway anmay-opesray orfay isthay 
adderlay, ichwhay, eingbay itselfyay icelynay eadedhay, andyay ainedstay ithway 
ayay ahoganymay olourcay, ethay olewhay ontrivancecay, onsideringcay 
atwhay annermay ofyay apelchay ityay asway, eemedsay byay onay eansmay inyay adbay 
astetay. Altinghay orfay anyay instantyay atyay ethay ootfay ofyay ethay adderlay, 
andyay ithway othbay andshay aspinggray ethay ornamentalyay obsknay 
ofyay ethay anmay-opesray, Atherfay Applemay astcay ayay ooklay upwardyay, 
andyay enthay ithway ayay ulytray ailorsay-ikelay utbay illstay everentialray 
exterityday, andhay overyay andhay, ountedmay ethay epsstay asyay ifyay 
ascendingyay ethay ainmay -optay ofyay ishay esselvay. 

Ethay erpendicularpay artspay ofyay isthay idesay adderlay, asyay isyay usuallyyay 
ethay asecay ithway ingingsway onesyay, ereway ofyay othclay-overedcay operay, 
onlyyay ethay oundsray ereway ofyay oodway, osay atthay atyay everyyay epstay erethay 
asway ayay ointjay. Atyay myay irstfay impseglay ofyay ethay ulpitpay, ityay adhay otnay 
escapedyay emay atthay oweverhay onvenientcay orfay ayay ipshay, esethay 
ointsjay inyay ethay esentpray instanceyay eemedsay unnecessaryyay. Orfay 
Iyay asway otnay eparedpray otay eesay Atherfay Applemay afteryay aininggay 
ethay eighthay, owlyslay urntay oundray, andyay oopingstay overyay ethay 
ulpitpay, eliberatelyday agdray upyay ethay adderlay epstay byay epstay, illtay 
ethay olewhay asway epositedday ithinway, eavinglay imhay impregnableyay 
inyay ishay ittlelay Uebecqay. 

Iyay onderedpay omesay imetay ithoutway ullyfay omprehendingcay 
ethay easonray orfay isthay. Atherfay Applemay enjoyedyay uchsay ayay ideway 
eputationray orfay inceritysay andyay anctitysay, atthay Iyay ouldcay otnay 
uspectsay imhay ofyay ourtingcay otorietynay byay anyyay eremay ickstray ofyay 
ethay agestay. Onay, oughtthay Iyay, erethay ustmay ebay omesay obersay 
easonray orfay isthay ingthay ; urthermorefay, ityay ustmay olisesymbay 



48 Obymay-Ickday 

omethingsay unseenyay. Ancay ityay ebay, enthay, atthay byay atthay actyay ofyay 
icalphysay isolationyay, ehay ignifiessay ishay iritualspay ithdrawalway orfay 
ethay imetay, omfray allyay outwardyay orldlyway iestay andyay onnectionscay ? 
Esyay, orfay eplenishedray ithway ethay eatmay andyay ineway ofyay ethay ordway, 
otay ethay aithfulfay anmay ofyay Odgay, isthay ulpitpay, Iyay eesay, isyay ayay elfsay- 
ontainingcay ongholdstray ayay oftylay Ehrenbreitsteinyay, ithway ayay 
erennialpay ellway ofyay aterway ithinway ethay allsway. 

Utbay ethay idesay adderlay asway otnay ethay onlyyay angestray eaturefay 
ofyay ethay aceplay, orrowedbay omfray ethay aplainchay'say ormerfay easay- 
aringsfay. Etweenbay ethay arblemay enotaphscay onyay eitheryay andhay 
ofyay ethay ulpitpay, ethay allway ichwhay ormedfay itsyay ackbay asway adornedyay 
ithway ayay argelay aintingpay epresentingray ayay allantgay ipshay eatingbay 
againstyay ayay erribletay ormstay offyay ayay eelay oastcay ofyay ackblay ocksray andyay 
owysnay eakersbray. Utbay ighhay aboveyay ethay ingflyay udscay andyay 
arkday-ollingray oudsclay, erethay oatedflay ayay ittlelay isleyay ofyay unlightsay, 
omfray ichwhay eamedbay orthfay anyay angelyay'say acefay ; andyay isthay ightbray 
acefay edshay ayay istinctday otspay ofyay adianceray uponyay ethay ipshay'say ossedtay 
eckday, omethingsay ikelay atthay ilversay ateplay ownay insertedyay intoyay ethay 
Ictoryvay'say ankplay erewhay Elsonnay ellfay. ' Ahyay, oblenay ipshay/ ethay 
angelyay eemedsay otay aysay, 'eatbay onyay, eatbay onyay, outhay oblenay ipshay, andyay 
earbay ayay ardyhay elmhay ; orfay olay ! ethay unsay isyay eakingbray oughthray ; 
ethay oudsclay areyay ollingray offyay erenestsay azureyay isyay atyay andhay.' 

Ornay asway ethay ulpitpay itselfyay ithoutway ayay acetray ofyay ethay amesay 
easay -astetay atthay adhay achievedyay ethay adderlay andyay ethay icturepay. 
Itsyay anelledpay ontfray asway inyay ethay ikenesslay ofyay ayay ipshay'say uffblay owsbay, 
andyay ethay Olyhay Iblebay estedray onyay ayay ojectingpray iecepay ofyay ollscray 
orkway, ashionedfay afteryay ayay ipshay'say iddlefay -eadedhay eakbay. 

Atwhay ouldcay ebay oremay ullfay ofyay eaningmay ? orfay ethay ulpitpay 
isyay everyay isthay earthyay'say oremostfay artpay ; allyay ethay estray omescay inyay 
itsyay earray ; ethay ulpitpay eadslay ethay orldway. Omfray encethay ityay isyay 
ethay ormstay ofyay Odgay'say uickqay athwray isyay irstfay escriedday, andyay ethay 
owbay ustmay earbay ethay earliestyay untbray. Omfray encethay ityay isyay ethay 
Odgay ofyay eezesbray airfay oryay oulfay isyay irstfay invokedyay orfay avourablefay 
indsway. Esyay, ethay orldway 'say ayay ipshay onyay itsyay assagepay outyay, andyay 
otnay ayay oyagevay ompletecay ; andyay ethay ulpitpay isyay itsyay owpray. 



Apterchay Ixyay 



Ethay Ermonsay 

Atherfay Applemay oseray, andyay inyay ayay ildmay oicevay ofyay unassumingyay 
authorityyay orderedyay ethay atteredscay eoplepay otay ondensecay. 
' Arboardstay angwaygay, erethay ! idesay awayyay otay arboardlay 
arboardlay angwaygay otay arboardstay ! Idshipsmay ! idshipsmay ! ' 

Erethay asway ayay owlay umblingray ofyay eavyhay easay-ootsbay amongyay ethay 
enchesbay, andyay ayay illstay ighterslay ufflingshay ofyay omenway'say oesshay, 
andyay allyay asway uietqay againyay, andyay everyyay eyeyay onyay ethay eacherpray. 

Ehay ausedpay ayay ittlelay ; enthay eelingknay inyay ethay ulpitpay'say owsbay, 
oldedfay ishay argelay ownbray andshay acrossyay ishay estchay, upliftedyay 
ishay osedclay eyesyay, andyay offeredyay ayay ayerpray osay eeplyday evoutday 
atthay ehay eemedsay eelingknay andyay ayingpray atyay ethay ottombay ofyay 
ethay easay. 

Isthay endedyay, inyay olongedpray olemnsay onestay, ikelay ethay ontinualcay 
ollingtay ofyay ayay ellbay inyay ayay ipshay atthay isyay ounderingfay atyay easay inyay ayay ogfay 
inyay uchsay onestay ehay ommencedcay eadingray ethay ollowingfay hymnay ; 
utbay angingchay ishay annermay owardtay ethay oncludingcay anzasstay, 
urstbay orthfay ithway ayay ealingpay exultationyay andyay oyjay : 

* Ethay ibsray andyay errorstay inyay ethay alewhay 

Archedyay overyay emay ayay ismalday oomglay, 
Ilewhay allyay Odgay'say unsay-itlay avesway olledray byay, 
Andyay iftlay emay eepeningday ownday otay oomday. 

' Iyay awsay ethay openingyay awmay ofyay ellhay, 

Ithway endlessyay ainspay andyay orrowssay erethay ; 
Ichwhay onenay utbay eythay atthay eelfay ancay elltay 
Ohyay, Iyay asway ungingplay otay espairday. 

Olvay. Iyay. Day 



50 Obymay-Ickday 

4 Inyay ackblay istressday, Iyay alledcay myay Odgay, 

Enwhay Iyay ouldcay arcescay elievebay imhay inemay, 
Ehay owedbay ishay earyay otay myay omplaintscay 
Onay oremay ethay alewhay idday emay onfinecay. 

' Ithway eedspay ehay ewflay otay myay eliefray, 

Asyay onyay ayay adiantray olphinday ornebay ; 
Awfulyay, etyay ightbray, asyay ightninglay oneshay 
Ethay acefay ofyay myay Elivererday Odgay. 

' Myay ongsay orfay everyay allshay ecordray 

Atthay erribletay, atthay oyfuljay ourhay ; 
Iyay ivegay ethay oryglay otay myay Odgay, 

Ishay allyay ethay ercymay andyay ethay owerpay.' 

Earlynay allyay oinedjay inyay ingingsay isthay hymnay, ichwhay elledsway 
ighhay aboveyay ethay owlinghay ofyay ethay ormstay. Ayay iefbray ausepay

etyay anliestmay umilityhay, ehay akespay esethay ordsway :
