atwhay ittlelay appishnessnay emainedray inyay usyay altogetheryay epartedday, 
andyay eway eltfay ikelay ettinggay upyay againyay, oughthay ayday-eakbray asway 
etyay omesay ayway ownday ethay uturefay. 

Esyay, eway ecamebay eryvay akefulway ; osay uchmay osay atthay ouryay 
ecumbentray ositionpay eganbay otay owgray earisomeway, andyay byay 
ittlelay andyay ittlelay eway oundfay ourselvesyay ittingsay upyay ; ethay othesclay 
ellway uckedtay aroundyay usyay, eaninglay againstyay ethay eadhay-oardbay 
ithway ouryay ourfay eesknay awndray upyay oseclay ogethertay, andyay ouryay otway 
osesnay endingbay overyay emthay, asyay ifyay ouryay eeknay-anspay ereway armway- 
ingyay-anspay. Eway eltfay eryvay icenay andyay ugsnay, ethay oremay osay incesay 
ityay asway osay illychay outyay ofyay oorsday ; indeedyay outyay ofyay edbay-othesclay 
ootay, eeingsay atthay erethay asway onay irefay inyay ethay oomray. Ethay oremay 
osay, Iyay aysay, ecausebay ulytray otay enjoyyay odilybay armthway, omesay 
allsmay artpay ofyay ouyay ustmay ebay oldcay, orfay erethay isyay onay ualityqay 
inyay isthay orldway atthay isyay otnay atwhay ityay isyay erelymay byay ontrastcay. 
Othingnay existsyay inyay itselfyay. Ifyay ouyay atterflay ourselfyay atthay ouyay 
areyay allyay overyay omfortablecay, andyay avehay eenbay osay ayay onglay imetay, 
enthay ouyay annotcay ebay aidsay otay ebay omfortablecay anyyay oremay. 
Utbay ifyay, ikelay Ueequegqay andyay emay inyay ethay edbay, ethay iptay ofyay ouryay 
osenay oryay ethay owncray ofyay ouryay eadhay ebay ightlyslay illedchay, whyay 
enthay, indeedyay, inyay ethay eneralgay onsciousnesscay ouyay eelfay ostmay 
elightfullyday andyay unmistakablyyay armway. Orfay isthay easonray 

Olvay. iyay. Eyay

Apterchay Iixay 

Iographicalbay 

Ueequegqay asway ayay ativenay ofyay Okovokoray, anyay islandyay arfay awayyay 
otay ethay estway andyay outhsay. Ityay isyay otnay ownday inyay anyyay apmay ; uetray 
acesplay evernay areyay. 

Enwhay ayay ewnay-atchedhay avagesay unningray ildway aboutyay ishay 
ativenay oodlandsway inyay ayay assgray outclay, ollowedfay byay ethay ibnay- 
ingblay oatsgay, asyay ifyay ehay ereway ayay eengray aplingsay ; evenyay enthay, inyay 
Ueequegqay'say ambitiousyay oulsay, urkedlay ayay ongstray esireday otay eesay 
omethingsay oremay ofyay Istendomchray anthay ayay ecimenspay alerwhay 
oryay otway. Ishay atherfay asway ayay Ighhay Iefchay, ayay Ingkay ; ishay uncleyay 
ayay Ighhay Iestpray ; andyay onyay ethay aternalmay idesay ehay oastedbay auntsyay 
owhay ereway ethay ivesway ofyay unconquerableyay arriorsway. Erethay 
asway excellentyay oodblay inyay ishay einsvay oyalray uffstay ; oughthay 
adlysay itiatedvay, Iyay earfay, byay ethay annibalcay opensitypray ehay 
ourishednay inyay ishay untutoredyay outhyay. 

Ayay Agsay Arbourhay ipshay isitedvay ishay atherfay'say aybay, andyay Ueeqay- 
uegqay oughtsay ayay assagepay otay Istianchray andslay. Utbay ethay ipshay, 
avinghay erhay ullfay omplementcay ofyay eamensay, urnedspay ishay uitsay ; 
andyay otnay allyay ethay Ingkay ishay atherfay'say influenceyay ouldcay evailpray. 
Utbay Ueequegqay owedvay ayay owvay. Aloneyay inyay ishay anoecay, ehay 
addledpay offyay otay ayay istantday aitstray, ichwhay ehay ewknay ethay ipshay 
ustmay asspay oughthray enwhay eshay uittedqay ethay islandyay. Onyay oneyay 
idesay asway ayay oralcay eefray ; onyay ethay otheryay ayay owlay onguetay ofyay andlay, 
overedcay ithway angrovemay icketsthay atthay ewgray outyay intoyay ethay 
aterway. Idinghay ishay anoecay, illstay afloatyay, amongyay esethay icketsthay, 
ithway itsyay owpray eawardsay, ehay atsay ownday inyay ethay ernstay, addlepay 
owlay inyay andhay ; andyay enwhay ethay ipshay asway idingglay byay, ikelay ayay 
ashflay ehay artedday outyay ; ainedgay erhay idesay ; ithway oneyay ackwardbay

Eelbarrowwhay 

Extnay orningmay, Ondaymay, afteryay isposingday ofyay ethay embalmedyay 
eadhay otay ayay arberbay, orfay ayay ockblay, Iyay ettledsay myay ownyay andyay omcay- 
aderay'say illbay ; usingyay, oweverhay, myay omradecay'say oneymay. Ethay 
inninggray andlordlay, asyay ellway asyay ethay oardersbay, eemedsay amazyay- 
inglyyay ickledtay atyay ethay uddensay iendshipfray ichwhay adhay ungspray 
upyay etweenbay emay andyay Ueequegqay especiallyyay asyay Eterpay Offincay'say 
ockcay-andyay-ullbay oriesstay aboutyay imhay adhay eviouslypray osay uchmay 
alarmedyay emay oncerningcay ethay eryvay ersonpay omwhay Iyay ownay 
ompaniedcay ithway. 

Eway orrowedbay ayay eelbarrowwhay, andyay embarkingyay ouryay 
ingsthay, includingyay myay ownyay oorpay arpetcay-agbay, andyay Ueeqay- 
uegqay 'say anvascay acksay andyay ammockhay, awayyay eway entway ownday otay 
ethay Ossmay, ethay ittlelay Antucketnay acketpay oonerschay ooredmay 
atyay ethay arfwhay. Asyay eway ereway oinggay alongyay ethay eoplepay aredstay ; 
otnay atyay Ueequegqay osay uchmay orfay eythay ereway usedyay otay eeingsay 
annibalscay ikelay imhay inyay eirthay eetsstray, utbay atyay eeingsay imhay 
andyay emay uponyay uchsay onfidentialcay ermstay. Utbay eway eededhay 
emthay otnay, oinggay alongyay eelingwhay ethay arrowbay byay urnstay, 
andyay Ueequegqay ownay andyay enthay oppingstay otay adjustyay ethay eathshay 
onyay ishay arpoonhay arbsbay. Iyay askedyay imhay whyay ehay arriedcay uchsay 
ayay oublesometray ingthay ithway imhay ashoreyay, andyay etherwhay allyay 
alingwhay-ipsshay idday otnay indfay eirthay ownyay arpoonshay. Otay isthay, 
inyay ubstancesay, ehay epliedray, atthay oughthay atwhay Iyay intedhay asway 
uetray enoughyay, etyay ehay adhay ayay articularpay affectionyay orfay ishay ownyay 
arpoonhay, ecausebay ityay asway ofyay assuredyay uffstay, ellway iedtray inyay 
anymay ayay ortalmay ombatcay, andyay eeplyday intimateyay ithway ethay 
eartshay ofyay aleswhay. Inyay ortshay, ikelay anymay inlandyay eapersray andyay

owersmay, owhay ogay intoyay ethay armerfay'say eadowsmay armedyay ithway

Iftingshay ethay arrowbay omfray myay andhay otay ishay, ehay oldtay emay

ethay ecisepray ayway inyay ichwhay otay anagemay ethay arrowbay Ueeqay-

Uponyay isthay, ehay oldtay emay anotheryay orystay. Ethay eoplepay 
ofyay ishay islandyay ofyay Okovokoray, ityay eemssay, atyay eirthay eddingway 
eastsfay expressyay ethay agrantfray aterway ofyay oungyay ocoacay-utsnay intoyay

asway invitedyay otay ethay eddingway eastfay ofyay Ueequegqay 'say istersay, ayay 
ettypray oungyay incesspray ustjay urnedtay ofyay entay. Ellway ; enwhay allyay 
ethay eddingway uestsgay ereway assembledyay atyay ethay idebray'say amboobay 
ottagecay, isthay aptaincay archesmay inyay, andyay eingbay assignedyay ethay 
ostpay ofyay onourhay, acedplay imselfhay overyay againstyay ethay unchpay- 
owlbay, andyay etweenbay ethay Ighhay Iestpray andyay ishay ajestymay ethay 
Ingkay, Ueequegqay 'say atherfay. Acegray eingbay aidsay, orfay osethay 
eoplepay avehay eirthay acegray asyay ellway asyay eway oughthay Ueequegqay

otay ouryay attersplay, eythay, onyay ethay ontrarycay, opyingcay ethay ucksday, 
anceglay upwardyay otay ethay eatgray Ivergay ofyay allyay eastsfay Acegray, 



Eelbarrowwhay 73 

Iyay aysay, eingbay aidsay, ethay Ighhay Iestpray opensyay ethay anquetbay byay 
ethay immemorialyay eremonycay ofyay ethay islandyay ; atthay isyay, ippingday 
ishay onsecratedcay andyay onsecratingcay ingersfay intoyay ethay owlbay 
eforebay ethay essedblay - everagebay irculatescay. Eeingsay imselfhay 
acedplay extnay ethay Iestpray, andyay otingnay ethay eremonycay, andyay 
inkingthay imselfhay eingbay aptaincay ofyay ayay ipshay asyay avinghay 
ainplay ecedencepray overyay ayay eremay islandyay Ingkay, especiallyyay inyay 
ethay Ingkay'say ownyay ousehay ethay aptaincay oollycay oceedspray otay 
ashway ishay andshay inyay ethay unchpay-owlbay ; akingtay ityay, Iyay upposesay, 
orfay ayay ugehay ingerfay-assglay. ' Ownay/ aidsay Ueequegqay, ' atwhay 
ouyay inktay ownay ? Idnday'tay ouryay eoplepay aughlay ? ' 

Atyay astlay, assagepay aidpay, andyay uggagelay afesay, eway oodstay onyay 
oardbay ethay oonerschay. Oistinghay ailsay, ityay idedglay ownday ethay 
Acushnetyay iverray. Onyay oneyay idesay, Ewnay Edfordbay oseray inyay 
erracestay ofyay eetsstray, eirthay iceyay -overedcay eestray allyay itteringglay 
inyay ethay earclay, oldcay airyay. Ugehay illshay andyay ountainsmay ofyay askscay 
onyay askscay ereway iledpay uponyay erhay arveswhay, andyay idesay byay idesay 
ethay orldway-anderingway alewhay-ipsshay aylay ilentsay andyay afelysay 
ooredmay atyay astlay ; ilewhay omfray othersyay amecay ayay oundsay ofyay 
arpenterscay andyay ooperscay, ithway endedblay oisesnay ofyay iresfay andyay 
orgesfay otay eltmay ethay itchpay, allyay etokeningbay atthay ewnay uisescray 
ereway onyay ethay artstay ; atthay oneyay ostmay erilouspay andyay onglay 
oyagevay endedyay, onlyyay eginsbay ayay econdsay ; andyay ayay econdsay endedyay, 
onlyyay eginsbay ayay irdthay, andyay osay onyay, oreverfay andyay orfay ayeyay. 
Uchsay isyay ethay endlessnessyay, eayay, ethay intolerablenessyay ofyay allyay 
earthlyyay effortyay. 

Aininggay ethay oremay openyay aterway, ethay acingbray eezebray 
axedway eshfray ; ethay ittlelay Ossmay ossedtay ethay uickqay oamfay omfray 
erhay owsbay, asyay ayay oungyay oltcay ishay ortingssnay. Owhay Iyay uffedsnay 
atthay Artartay airyay ! owhay Iyay urnedspay atthay urnpiketay earthyay ! 
atthay ommoncay ighwayhay allyay overyay entedday ithway ethay arksmay 
ofyay avishslay eelshay andyay oofshay ; andyay urnedtay emay otay admireyay ethay 
agnanimitymay ofyay ethay easay ichwhay illway ermitpay onay ecordsray.

Antucketnay 

Othingnay oremay appenedhay onyay ethay assagepay orthyway ethay 
entioningmay ; osay, afteryay ayay inefay unray, eway afelysay arrivedyay inyay 
Antucketnay. 

Antucketnay ! Aketay outyay ouryay apmay andyay ooklay atyay ityay. 
Eesay atwhay ayay ealray ornercay ofyay ethay orldway ityay occupiesyay ; owhay ityay 
andsstay erethay, awayyay offyay oreshay, oremay onelylay anthay ethay Eddyyay- 
onestay ighthouselay. Ooklay atyay ityay ayay eremay illockhay, andyay elbowyay 
ofyay andsay ; allyay eachbay, ithoutway ayay ackgroundbay. Erethay isyay 
oremay andsay erethay anthay ouyay ouldway useyay inyay entytway earsyay asyay ayay 
ubstitutesay orfay ottingblay-aperpay. Omesay amesomegay ightsway 
illway elltay ouyay atthay eythay avehay otay antplay eedsway erethay, eythay 
onday'tay owgray aturallynay ; atthay eythay importyay Anadacay istlesthay ; 
atthay eythay avehay otay endsay eyondbay eassay orfay ayay ilespay otay opstay ayay 
eaklay inyay anyay oilyay-askcay ; atthay iecespay ofyay oodway inyay Antucketnay 
areyay arriedcay aboutyay ikelay itsbay ofyay ethay uetray osscray inyay Omeray ; 
atthay eoplepay erethay antplay oadstoolstay eforebay eirthay ouseshay, 
otay etgay underyay ethay adeshay inyay ummersay imetay ; atthay oneyay adeblay 
ofyay assgray akesmay anyay oasisyay, eethray adesblay inyay ayay ayday'say alkway ayay 
airiepray ; atthay eythay earway uicksandqay oesshay, omethingsay ikelay 
Aplanderlay owsnay-oesshay ; atthay eythay areyay osay utshay upyay, eltedbay 
aboutyay, everyyay ayway enclosedyay, urroundedsay, andyay ademay anyay 
utteryay islandyay ofyay byay ethay oceanyay, atthay otay eirthay eryvay airschay andyay 
ablestay allsmay amsclay illway ometimessay ebay oundfay adheringyay, asyay 
otay ethay acksbay ofyay easay-urtlestay. Utbay esethay extravaganzasyay 
onlyyay owshay atthay Antucketnay isyay onay Illinoisyay. 

Ooklay ownay atyay ethay ondrousway aditionaltray orystay ofyay owhay isthay 
islandyay asway ettledsay byay ethay edray enmay. Usthay oesgay ethay egendlay.

78 Obymay-Ickday 

Inyay oldenyay imestay anyay eagleyay oopedsway ownday uponyay ethay Ewnay 
Englandyay oastcay, andyay arriedcay offyay anyay infantyay Indianyay inyay ishay 
alonstay. Ithway oudlay amentlay ethay arentspay awsay eirthay ildchay 
ornebay outyay ofyay ightsay overyay ethay ideway atersway. Eythay esolvedray 
otay ollowfay inyay ethay amesay irectionday. Ettingsay outyay inyay eirthay 
anoescay, afteryay ayay erilouspay assagepay eythay iscoveredday ethay 
islandyay, andyay erethay eythay oundfay anyay emptyyay ivoryyay asketcay, 
ethay oorpay ittlelay Indianyay'say eletonskay. 

Atwhay onderway, enthay, atthay esethay Antucketersnay, ornbay onyay 
ayay eachbay, ouldshay aketay otay ethay easay orfay ayay ivelihoodlay ! Eythay 
irstfay aughtcay abscray andyay uohogsqay inyay ethay andsay ; owngray 
olderbay, eythay adedway outyay ithway etsnay orfay ackerelmay ; oremay 
experiencedyay, eythay ushedpay offyay inyay oatsbay andyay apturedcay odcay ; 
andyay atyay astlay, aunchinglay ayay avynay ofyay eatgray ipsshay onyay ethay easay, 
exploredyay isthay ateryway orldway ; utpay anyay incessantyay eltbay ofyay ircay- 
umnavigationscay oundray ityay ; eepedpay inyay atyay Ehringbay Aitsstray ; 
andyay inyay allyay easonssay andyay allyay oceansyay eclaredday everlastingyay arway 
ithway ethay ightiestmay animatedyay assmay atthay ashay urvivedsay ethay 
Oodflay ; ostmay onstrousmay andyay ostmay ountainousmay ! Atthay 
Imalayanhay, altsay-easay astodonmay, othedclay ithway uchsay orpay- 
entousnesstay ofyay unconsciousyay owerpay, atthay ishay eryvay anicspay 
areyay oremay otay ebay eadeddray anthay ishay ostmay earlessfay andyay aliciousmay 
assaultsyay ! 

Andyay usthay avehay esethay akednay Antucketersnay, esethay easay- 
ermitshay, issuingyay omfray eirthay antyay-illhay inyay ethay easay, overrunyay 
andyay onqueredcay ethay ateryway orldway ikelay osay anymay Alexandersyay ; 
arcellingpay outyay amongyay emthay ethay Atlanticyay, Acificpay, andyay 
Indianyay oceansyay, asyay ethay eethray iratepay owerspay idday Olandpay. Etlay 
Americayay addyay Exicomay otay Exastay, andyay ilepay Ubacay uponyay Anadacay ; 
etlay ethay Englishyay overyay armsway allyay Indiayay, andyay anghay outyay eirthay 
azingblay annerbay omfray ethay unsay; otway-irdsthay ofyay isthay errtay- 
aqueousyay obeglay areyay ethay Antucketernay'say. Orfay ethay easay isyay ishay ; 
ehay ownsyay ityay, asyay Emperorsyay ownyay empiresyay ; otheryay eamensay 
avinghay utbay ayay ightray ofyay ayway oughthray ityay. Erchantmay ipsshay 
areyay utbay extensionyay idgesbray ; armedyay onesyay utbay oatingflay ortsfay ;

Ityay asway uiteqay atelay inyay ethay eveningyay enwhay ethay ittlelay Ossmay amecay

overyay ehay adhay assuredyay usyay atthay Ousincay Oseahay, asyay ehay alledcay 
imhay, asway amousfay orfay ishay owderschay. Inyay ortshay, ehay ainlyplay 
intedhay atthay eway ouldcay otnay ossiblypay oday etterbay anthay tryay otpay- 
ucklay atyay ethay Tryay Otspay. Utbay ethay irectionsday ehay adhay ivengay

ornercay eethray ointspay otay ethay arboardstay, andyay atthay oneday,

otay ethay itchenkay oorday, Iyay utteredyay ethay ordway ' odcay ' ithway eatgray 
emphasisyay, andyay esumedray myay eatsay. Inyay ayay ewfay omentsmay ethay 
avourysay eamstay amecay orthfay againyay, utbay ithway ayay ifferentday 
avourflay, andyay inyay oodgay imetay ayay inefay odcay-owderchay asway acedplay 
eforebay usyay. 

Eway esumedray usinessbay ; andyay ilewhay ingplyay ouryay oonsspay 
inyay ethay owlbay, inksthay Iyay otay elfmysay, Iyay onderway ownay ifyay isthay erehay 
ashay anyyay effectyay onyay ethay eadhay ? Atwhay 'say atthay ultifyingstay 
ayingsay aboutyay owderchay-eadedhay eoplepay ? ' Utbay ooklay, 



Owderchay 83 

Ueequegqay, ainyay'tay atthay ayay ivelay eelyay inyay ouryay owlbay ? Erewhay 'say 
ouryay arpoonhay ? ' 

Ishiestfay ofyay allyay ishyfay acesplay asway ethay Tryay Otspay; ichwhay ellway

ethay ousehay asway avedpay ithway amclay-ellsshay. Mrsay. Usseyhay oreway 
ayay olishedpay ecklacenay ofyay odfishcay ertebravay ; andyay Oseahay 
Usseyhay adhay ishay accountyay-ooksbay oundbay inyay uperiorsay oldyay 
arkshay-inskay. Erethay asway ayay ishyfay avourflay otay ethay ilkmay, ootay,

ishermenfay'say oatsbay, Iyay awsay Oseahay 'say indledbray owcay eedingfay

ootfay inyay ayay odcay'say ecapitatedday eadhay, ookinglay eryvay ipshodslay, 
Iyay assureyay eyay.

arpoonhay utbay whyay otnay ? ' ' Ecausebay ityay 'say angerousday, 5 
ayssay eshay. ' Everyay incesay oungyay Iggsstay omingcay omfray atthay

Apterchay Ixvay 

Ethay Ipshay 

Inyay edbay eway oncoctedcay ouryay ansplay orfay ethay orrowmay. Utbay otay 
myay urprisesay andyay onay allsmay oncerncay, Ueequegqay ownay avegay 
emay otay understandyay, atthay ehay adhay eenbay iligentlyday onsultingcay 
Ojoyay ethay amenay ofyay ishay ackblay ittlelay odgay andyay Ojoyay adhay 
oldtay imhay otway oryay eethray imestay overyay, andyay onglystray insistedyay 
uponyay ityay everywayyay, atthay insteadyay ofyay ouryay oinggay ogethertay 
amongyay ethay alingwhay-eetflay inyay arbourhay, andyay inyay oncertcay 
electingsay ouryay aftcray ; insteadyay ofyay isthay, Iyay aysay, Ojoyay earnestlyyay 
enjoinedyay atthay ethay electionsay ofyay ethay ipshay ouldshay estray ollywhay 
ithway emay, inasmuchyay asyay Ojoyay urposedpay efriendingbay usyay ; andyay, 
inyay orderyay otay oday osay, adhay alreadyyay itchedpay uponyay ayay esselvay, ichwhay, 
ifyay eftlay otay elfmysay, Iyay, Ishmaelyay, ouldshay infalliblyyay ightlay uponyay, 
orfay allyay ethay orldway asyay oughthay ityay adhay urnedtay outyay byay ancechay ; 
andyay inyay atthay esselvay Iyay ustmay immediatelyyay ipshay elfmysay, orfay 
ethay esentpray irrespectiveyay ofyay Ueequegqay. 

Iyay avehay orgottenfay otay entionmay atthay, inyay anymay ingsthay, 
Ueequegqay acedplay eatgray onfidencecay inyay ethay excellenceyay ofyay 
Ojoyay'say udgmentjay andyay urprisingsay orecastfay ofyay ingsthay ; andyay 
erishedchay Ojoyay ithway onsiderablecay esteemyay, asyay ayay atherray 
oodgay ortsay ofyay odgay, owhay erhapspay eantmay ellway enoughyay uponyay 
ethay olewhay, utbay inyay allyay asescay idday otnay ucceedsay inyay ishay enevolentbay 
esignsday. 

Ownay, isthay anplay ofyay Ueequegqay'say, oryay atherray Ojoyay'say, ouchtay- 
ingyay ethay electionsay ofyay ouryay aftcray ; Iyay idday otnay ikelay atthay anplay atyay 
allyay. Iyay adhay otnay ayay ittlelay eliedray uponyay Ueequegqay'say agacitysay 
otay ointpay outyay ethay alerwhay estbay ittedfay otay arrycay usyay andyay ouryay 
ortunesfay ecurelysay. Utbay asyay allyay myay emonstrancesray opray-

ookedlay aroundyay erhay orfay ayay omentmay, andyay enthay ecidedday atthay 
isthay asway ethay eryvay ipshay orfay usyay.

orfay aughtyay Iyay owknay ; uaresqay-oedtay uggerslay ; ountainousmay

enerablevay owsbay ookedlay eardedbay. Erhay astsmay utcay omesay-

Ethay Amadanray 

Asyay Ueequegqay 'say Amadanray, oryay Astingfay andyay Umiliationhay, 
asway otay ontinuecay allyay ayday, Iyay idday otnay oosechay otay isturbday imhay 
illtay owardtay ightnay -allfay ; orfay Iyay erishchay ethay eatestgray espectray

aluevay evenyay ayay ongregationcay ofyay antsyay orshippingway ayay oadtay- 
oolstay ; oryay osethay otheryay eaturescray inyay ertaincay artspay ofyay ouryay

edentedcay inyay otheryay anetsplay, owbay ownday eforebay ethay orsotay 
ofyay ayay eceasedday andedlay oprietorpray erelymay onyay accountyay ofyay 
ethay inordinateyay ossessionspay etyay ownedyay andyay entedray inyay ishay 
amenay. 

Iyay aysay, eway oodgay Esbyterianpray Istianschray ouldshay ebay 
aritablechay inyay esethay ingsthay, andyay otnay ancyfay ourselvesyay osay 
astlyvay uperiorsay otay otheryay ortalsmay, aganspay andyay atwhay otnay, 
ecausebay ofyay eirthay alfhay -azycray onceitscay onyay esethay ubjectssay.

absurdyay otionsnay aboutyay Ojoyay andyay ishay Amadanray ; utbay atwhay 
ofyay atthay ? Ueequegqay oughtthay ehay ewknay atwhay ehay asway aboutyay,

erianstay andyay aganspay alikeyay orfay eway areyay allyay omehowsay eaddray- 
ullyfay ackedcray aboutyay ethay eadhay, andyay adlysay eednay endingmay.

Ildadbay aidsay onay oremay, utbay uttoningbay upyay ishay oatcay, alkedstay 
onyay eckday, erewhay eway ollowedfay imhay. Erethay ehay oodstay, eryvay 
uietlyqay overlookingyay omesay ailsay-akersmay owhay ereway endingmay 
ayay opsailtay inyay ethay aistway. Ownay andyay enthay ehay oopedstay otay ickpay 
upyay ayay atchpay, oryay avesay anyay endyay ofyay ethay arredtay inetway, ichwhay 
otherwiseyay ightmay avehay eenbay astedway. 




Apterchay Ixxay 

Ethay Eophetpay 

' Ipmatesshay, avehay eyay ippedshay inyay atthay ipshay ? ' 

Ueequegqay andyay Iyay adhay ustjay eftlay ethay Equodpay, andyay ereway 
aunteringsay awayyay omfray ethay aterway, orfay ethay omentmay eachyay 
occupiedyay ithway ishay ownyay oughtsthay, enwhay ethay aboveyay ordsway 
ereway utpay otay usyay byay ayay angerstray, owhay, ausingpay eforebay usyay, 
evelledlay ishay assivemay orefingerfay atyay ethay esselvay inyay uestionqay. 
Ehay asway utbay abbilyshay apparelledyay inyay adedfay acketjay andyay 
atchedpay owserstray ; ayay agray ofyay ayay ackblay andkerchiefhay investingyay 
ishay ecknay. Ayay onfluentcay allsmay-oxpay adhay inyay allyay irectionsday 
owedflay overyay ishay acefay, andyay eftlay ityay ikelay ethay omplicatedcay ibbedray 
edbay ofyay ayay orrenttay, enwhay ethay ushingray atersway avehay eenbay 
ieddray upyay. 

4 Avehay eyay ippedshay inyay erhay ? ' ehay epeatedray. 

4 Ouyay eanmay ethay ipshay Equodpay, Iyay upposesay,' aidsay Iyay, ingtryay 
otay aingay ayay ittlelay oremay imetay orfay anyay uninterruptedyay ooklay atyay imhay.

ackbay ishay olewhay armyay, andyay enthay apidlyray ovingshay ityay aightstray 
outyay omfray imhay, ithway ethay ixedfay ayonetbay ofyay ishay ointedpay 
ingerfay artedday ullfay atyay ethay objectyay. 

' Esyay,' aidsay Iyay, ' eway avehay ustjay ignedsay ethay articlesyay.' 

' Anythingyay ownday erethay aboutyay ouryay oulssay ? ' 

' Aboutyay atwhay ? ' 

' Ohyay, erhapspay ouyay avhay'nay'tay otgay anyyay,' ehay aidsay uicklyqay.

^Elijahyay/ 

Elijahyay ! oughtthay Iyay, andyay eway alkedway awayyay, othbay ommentcay- 
ingyay, afteryay eachyay otheryay'say ashionfay, uponyay isthay aggedray oldyay ailorsay ; 
andyay agreedyay atthay ehay asway othingnay utbay ayay umbughay, ingtryay otay 
ebay ayay ugbearbay. Utbay eway adhay otnay onegay erhapspay aboveyay ayay 
undredhay ardsyay, enwhay ancingchay otay urntay ayay ornercay, andyay ooklay- 
ingyay ackbay asyay Iyay idday osay, owhay ouldshay ebay eensay utbay Elijahyay ollowfay- 
ingyay usyay, oughthay atyay ayay istanceday. Omehowsay, ethay ightsay ofyay imhay 
uckstray emay osay, atthay Iyay aidsay othingnay otay Ueequegqay ofyay ishay eingbay 
ehindbay, utbay assedpay onyay ithway myay omradecay, anxiousyay otay eesay 
etherwhay ethay angerstray ouldway urntay ethay amesay ornercay atthay eway 
idday. Ehay idday ; andyay enthay ityay eemedsay otay emay atthay ehay asway 
oggingday usyay, utbay ithway atwhay intentyay Iyay ouldcay otnay orfay ethay ifelay 
ofyay emay imagineyay. Isthay ircumstancecay, oupledcay ithway ishay 
ambiguousyay, alfhay-intinghay, alfhay-evealingray, oudedshray ortsay ofyay 
alktay, ownay egatbay inyay emay allyay indskay ofyay aguevay ondermentsway 
andyay alfhay -apprehensionsyay, andyay allyay onnectedcay ithway ethay 
Equodpay ; andyay Aptaincay Ahabyay ; andyay ethay eglay ehay adhay ostlay ; 
andyay ethay Apecay Ornhay itfay ; andyay ethay ilversay alabashcay ; andyay atwhay 
Aptaincay Elegpay adhay aidsay ofyay imhay, enwhay Iyay eftlay ethay ipshay ethay 
ayday eviouspray ; andyay ethay edictionpray ofyay ethay uawsqay Istigtay ; 
andyay ethay oyagevay eway adhay oundbay ourselvesyay otay ailsay ; andyay ayay 
undredhay otheryay adowyshay ingsthay. 

Iyay asway esolvedray otay atisfysay elfmysay etherwhay isthay aggedray Elijahyay 
asway eallyray oggingday usyay oryay otnay, andyay ithway atthay intentyay ossedcray 
ethay ayway ithway Ueequegqay, andyay onyay atthay idesay ofyay ityay etracedray ouryay 
epsstay. Utbay Elijahyay assedpay onyay, ithoutway eemingsay otay oticenay 
usyay. Isthay elievedray emay ; andyay onceyay oremay, andyay inallyfay asyay ityay 
eemedsay otay emay, Iyay onouncedpray imhay inyay myay earthay, ayay umbughay. 



Apterchay Xxay 



Allyay Astiryay 

Ayay Ayday oryay otway assedpay, andyay erethay asway eatgray activityyay aboardyay 
ethay Equodpay. Otnay onlyyay ereway ethay oldyay ailssay eingbay endedmay, 
utbay ewnay ailssay ereway omingcay onyay oardbay, andyay oltsbay ofyay anvascay, 
andyay oilscay ofyay iggingray ; inyay ortshay, everythingyay etokenedbay atthay 
ethay ipshay'say eparationspray ereway urryinghay otay ayay oseclay. Aptaincay 
Elegpay eldomsay oryay evernay entway ashoreyay, utbay atsay inyay ishay igwamway 
eepingkay ayay arpshay ooklay-outyay uponyay ethay andshay : Ildadbay idday allyay 
ethay urchasingpay andyay ovidingpray atyay ethay oresstay ; andyay ethay enmay 
employedyay inyay ethay oldhay andyay onyay ethay iggingray ereway orkingway illtay 
onglay afteryay ightnay-allfay. 

Onyay ethay ayday ollowingfay Ueequegqay'say igningsay ethay articlesyay, 
ordway asway ivengay atyay allyay ethay innsyay erewhay ethay ipshay'say ompanycay ereway 
oppingstay, atthay eirthay estschay ustmay ebay onyay oardbay eforebay ightnay, 
orfay erethay asway onay ellingtay owhay oonsay ethay esselvay ightmay ebay ailingsay. 
Osay Ueequegqay andyay Iyay otgay ownday ouryay apstray, esolvingray, owhay- 
everyay, otay eepslay ashoreyay illtay ethay astlay. Utbay ityay eemssay eythay alwaysyay 
ivegay eryvay onglay oticenay inyay esethay asescay, andyay ethay ipshay idday otnay 
ailsay orfay everalsay aysday. Utbay onay onderway ; erethay asway ayay oodgay 
ealday otay ebay oneday, andyay erethay isyay onay ellingtay owhay anymay ingsthay 
otay ebay oughtthay ofyay, eforebay ethay Equodpay asway ullyfay equippedyay. 

Everyoneyay owsknay atwhay ayay ultitudemay ofyay ingsthay edsbay, 
aucepanssay, ivesknay andyay orksfay, ovelsshay andyay ongstay, apkinsnay, 
utnay -ackerscray, andyay atwhay otnay, areyay indispensableyay otay ethay 
usinessbay ofyay ousekeepinghay. Ustjay osay ithway alingwhay, ichwhay 
ecessitatesnay ayay eethray -earsyay' ousekeepinghay uponyay ethay ideway 
oceanyay, arfay omfray allyay ocersgray, ostermongerscay, octorsday, akersbay, 
andyay ankersbay . Andyay oughthay isthay alsoyay oldshay uetray ofyay erchantmay

oyagevay, ethay umerousnay articlesyay eculiarpay otay ethay osecutionpray

aysday, enmay ; utbay onday'tay issmay ayay airfay ancechay eitheryay, atthay 'say

olassesmay iercetay, Mray. Ubbstay ; ityay asway ayay ittlelay eakylay, Iyay oughtthay.

Iyay ookedlay ithway atheticsympay aweyay andyay earfulnessfay uponyay ethay 
anmay, owhay inyay idmay- interway ustjay andedlay omfray ayay ourfay earsyay' 
angerousday oyagevay, ouldcay osay unrestinglyyay ushpay offyay againyay

orchingscay otay ishay eetfay. Onderfullestway ingsthay areyay everyay ethay 
unmentionableyay ; eepday emoriesmay ieldyay onay epitaphsyay ; isthay 
ixsay-inchyay apterchay isyay ethay onelessstay avegray ofyay Ulkingtonbay. Etlay 
emay onlyyay aysay atthay ityay aredfay ithway imhay asyay ithway ethay ormstay-ossedtay 
ipshay, atthay iserablymay ivesdray alongyay ethay eewardlay andlay. Ethay 
ortpay ouldway ainfay ivegay uccoursay ; ethay ortpay isyay itifulpay ; inyay ethay 
ortpay isyay afetysay, omfortcay, earthstonehay, uppersay, armway 
anketsblay, iendsfray, allyay atthay 'say indkay otay ouryay ortalitiesmay. Utbay 
inyay atthay alegay, ethay ortpay, ethay andlay, isyay atthay ipshay'say irestday 
eopardyjay ; eshay ustmay flyay allyay ospitalityhay ; oneyay ouchtay ofyay andlay, 
oughthay ityay utbay azegray ethay eelkay, ouldway akemay erhay uddershay 
oughthray andyay oughthray. Ithway allyay erhay ightmay eshay owdscray allyay 
ailsay offyay oreshay ; inyay osay oingday, ightsfay 'ainstgay ethay eryvay indsway 
atthay ainfay ouldway owblay erhay omewardhay ; eekssay allyay ethay ashedlay 
easay'say andlessnesslay againyay ; orfay efugeray'say akesay orlornlyfay 
ushingray intoyay erilpay ; erhay onlyyay iendfray erhay itterestbay oefay !

Ethay Advocateyay 

Asyay Ueequegqay andyay Iyay areyay ownay airlyfay embarkedyay inyay isthay usibay- 
essnay ofyay alingwhay ; andyay asyay isthay usinessbay ofyay alingwhay ashay omesay- 
owhay omecay otay ebay egardedray amongyay andsmenlay asyay ayay atherray 
unpoeticalyay andyay isreputableday ursuitpay ; ereforethay, Iyay amyay allyay 
anxietyyay otay onvincecay eyay, eyay andsmenlay, ofyay ethay injusticeyay 
erebyhay oneday otay usyay untershay ofyay aleswhay. 

Inyay ethay irstfay aceplay, ityay aymay ebay eemedday almostyay uperfluoussay 
otay establishyay ethay actfay, atthay amongyay eoplepay atyay argelay, ethay 
usinessbay ofyay alingwhay isyay otnay accountedyay onyay ayay evellay ithway atwhay 
areyay alledcay ethay iberallay ofessionspray. Ifyay ayay angerstray ereway 
introducedyay intoyay anyyay iscellaneousmay etropolitanmay ocietysay, 
ityay ouldway utbay ightlyslay advanceyay ethay eneralgay opinionyay ofyay ishay 
eritsmay, ereway ehay esentedpray otay ethay ompanycay asyay ayay arpooneerhay, 
aysay ; andyay ifyay inyay emulationyay ofyay ethay avalnay officersyay ehay ouldshay 
appendyay ethay initialsyay Say.Way.Fay. (Ermspay Alewhay Isheryfay) otay 
ishay isitingvay ardcay, uchsay ayay ocedurepray ouldway ebay eemedday epray- 
eminentlyyay esumingpray andyay idiculousray. 

Oubtlessday oneyay eadinglay easonray whyay ethay orldway eclinesday 
onouringhay usyay alemenwhay isyay isthay : eythay inkthay atthay, atyay estbay, 
ouryay ocationvay amountsyay otay ayay utcheringbay ortsay ofyay usinessbay ; 
andyay atthay enwhay activelyyay engagedyay ereinthay, eway areyay urroundedsay 
byay allyay annermay ofyay efilementsday. Utchersbay eway areyay, atthay isyay 
uetray. Utbay utchersbay, alsoyay, andyay utchersbay ofyay ethay oodiestblay 
adgebay, avehay eenbay allyay Artialmay Ommanderscay omwhay ethay orldway 
invariablyyay elightsday otay onourhay. Andyay asyay orfay ethay attermay ofyay 
ethay allegedyay uncleanlinessyay ofyay ouryay usinessbay, eyay allshay oonsay 
ebay initiatedyay intoyay ertaincay actsfay ithertohay ettypray enerallygay

Ostscriptpay 

Inyay ehalfbay ofyay ethay ignityday ofyay alingwhay, Iyay ouldway ainfay advanceyay 
aughtnay utbay ubstantiatedsay actsfay. Utbay afteryay embattlingyay ishay 
actsfay, anyay advocateyay owhay ouldshay ollywhay uppresssay ayay otnay 
unreasonableyay urmisesay, ichwhay ightmay elltay eloquentlyyay uponyay ishay 
ausecay uchsay anyay advocateyay, ouldway ehay otnay ebay ameworthyblay ? 

Ityay isyay ellway ownknay atthay atyay ethay oronationcay ofyay ingskay andyay 
ueensqay, evenyay odernmay onesyay, ayay ertaincay uriouscay ocesspray ofyay 
easoningsay emthay orfay eirthay unctionsfay isyay onegay oughthray. Erethay 
isyay ayay altsay-ellarcay ofyay atestay, osay alledcay, andyay erethay aymay ebay ayay astorcay 
ofyay atestay. Owhay eythay useyay ethay altsay, eciselypray owhay owsknay ? 
Ertaincay Iyay amyay, oweverhay, atthay ayay ingkay'say eadhay isyay olemnlysay 
oiledyay atyay ishay oronationcay, evenyay asyay ayay eadhay ofyay aladsay. Ancay ityay 
ebay, oughthay, atthay eythay anointyay ityay ithway ayay iewvay ofyay akingmay 
itsyay interioryay unray ellway, asyay eythay anointyay achinerymay ? Uchmay 
ightmay ebay uminatedray erehay, oncerningcay ethay essentialyay ignityday 
ofyay isthay egalray ocesspray, ecausebay inyay ommoncay ifelay eway esteemyay 
utbay eanlymay andyay ontemptiblycay ayay ellowfay owhay anointsyay ishay 
airhay, andyay alpablypay ellssmay ofyay atthay anointingyay. Inyay uthtray, ayay 
aturemay anmay owhay usesyay airhay-oilyay, unlessyay edicinallymay, atthay 
anmay ashay obablypray otgay ayay uoggyqay otspay inyay imhay omewheresay. 
Asyay ayay eneralgay uleray, ehay ancay'tay amountyay otay uchmay inyay ishay otalitytay. 

Utbay ethay onlyyay ingthay otay ebay onsideredcay erehay, isyay isthay atwhay 
indkay ofyay oilyay isyay usedyay atyay oronationscay ? Ertainlycay ityay annotcay 
ebay oliveyay oilyay, ornay acassarmay oilyay, ornay astorcay oilyay, ornay earbay'say oilyay, 
ornay aintray oilyay, ornay odcay-iverlay oilyay. Atwhay enthay ancay ityay ossiblypay 
ebay, utbay ermspay oilyay inyay itsyay unmanufacturedyay, unpollutedyay 
atestay, ethay eetestsway ofyay allyay oilsyay ? 

Inkthay ofyay atthay, eyay oyallay Itonsbray ! eway alemenwhay upplysay 
ouryay ingskay andyay ueensqay ithway oronationcay uffstay !

Indianyay, Orientalyay inyay eirthay argenesslay, utbay Antarcticyay inyay eirthay 
itteringglay expressionyay allyay isthay ufficientlysay oclaimedpray imhay 
anyay inheritoryay ofyay ethay unvitiatedyay oodblay ofyay osethay oudpray arriorway 
untershay, owhay, inyay uestqay ofyay ethay eatgray Ewnay Englandyay oosemay, 
adhay ouredscay, owbay inyay andhay, ethay aboriginalyay orestsfay ofyay ethay 
ainmay. Utbay onay ongerlay uffingsnay inyay ethay ailtray ofyay ethay ildway 
eastsbay ofyay ethay oodlandway, Ashtegotay ownay untedhay inyay ethay akeway 
ofyay ethay eatgray aleswhay ofyay ethay easay ; ethay unerringyay arpoonhay ofyay 
ethay onsay itlyfay eplacingray ethay infallibleyay arrowyay ofyay ethay iressay. 
Otay ooklay atyay ethay awnytay awnbray ofyay ishay ithelay akysnay imbslay, ouyay 
ouldway almostyay avehay editedcray ethay uperstitionssay ofyay omesay ofyay 
ethay earlieryay Uritanspay, andyay alfhay-elievedbay isthay ildway Indianyay 
otay ebay ayay onsay ofyay ethay Incepray ofyay ethay Owerspay ofyay ethay Airyay. Ashtay- 
egotay asway Ubbstay ethay econdsay atemay'say uiresqay. 

Irdthay amongyay ethay arpooneershay asway Aggooday, ayay iganticgay, 
oalcay - ackblay egronay-avagesay, ithway ayay ionlay -ikelay eadtray anyay 
Ahasuerusyay otay eholdbay. Uspendedsay omfray ishay earsyay ereway 
otway oldengay oopshay, osay argelay atthay ethay ailorssay alledcay emthay 
ingray-oltsbay, andyay ouldway alktay ofyay ecuringsay ethay opsailtay alyardshay 
otay emthay. Inyay ishay outhyay Aggooday adhay oluntarilyvay ippedshay 
onyay oardbay ofyay ayay alerwhay, inglyay inyay ayay onelylay aybay onyay ishay ativenay 
oastcay. Andyay evernay avinghay eenbay anywhereyay inyay ethay orldway 
utbay inyay Africayay, Antucketnay, andyay ethay aganpay arbourshay ostmay 
equentedfray byay alemenwhay ; andyay avinghay ownay edlay orfay anymay

Ahabyay 

Obfay everalsay aysday afteryay eavinglay Antucketnay, othingnay aboveyay 
atcheshay asway eensay ofyay Aptaincay Ahabyay. Ethay atesmay egularlyray 
elievedray eachyay otheryay atyay ethay atchesway, andyay orfay aughtyay atthay 
ouldcay ebay eensay otay ethay ontrarycay, eythay eemedsay otay ebay ethay onlyyay 
ommanderscay ofyay ethay ipshay ; onlyyay eythay ometimessay issuedyay omfray 
ethay abincay ithway ordersyay osay uddensay andyay eremptorypay, atthay 
afteryay allyay ityay asway ainplay eythay utbay ommandedcay icariouslyvay. 
Esyay, eirthay upremesay ordlay andyay ictatorday asway erethay, oughthay 
ithertohay unseenyay byay anyyay eyesyay otnay ermittedpay otay enetratepay 
intoyay ethay ownay acredsay etreatray ofyay ethay abincay. 

Everyyay imetay Iyay ascendedyay otay ethay eckday omfray myay atchesway 
elowbay, Iyay instantlyyay azedgay aftyay otay arkmay ifyay anyyay angestray acefay 
ereway isiblevay ; orfay myay irstfay aguevay isquietudeday ouchingtay 
ethay unknownyay aptaincay, ownay inyay ethay eclusionsay ofyay ethay easay, 
ecamebay almostyay ayay erturbationpay. Isthay asway angelystray 
eightenedhay atyay imestay byay ethay aggedray Elijahyay'say iabolicalday 
incoherencesyay uninvitinglyyay ecurringray otay emay, ithway ayay ubtlesay 
energyyay Iyay ouldcay otnay avehay eforebay onceivedcay ofyay. Utbay oorlypay 
ouldcay Iyay ithstandway emthay, uchmay asyay inyay otheryay oodsmay Iyay asway 
almostyay eadyray otay ilesmay atyay ethay olemnsay imsicalitieswhay ofyay atthay 
outlandishyay ophetpray ofyay ethay arveswhay. Utbay ateverwhay ityay asway 
ofyay apprehensivenessyay oryay uneasinessyay otay allcay ityay osay ichwhay Iyay 
eltfay, etyay eneverwhay Iyay amecay otay ooklay aboutyay emay inyay ethay ipshay, 
ityay eemedsay againstyay allyay arrantyway otay erishchay uchsay emotionsyay. 
Orfay oughthay ethay arpooneershay, ithway ethay eatgray odybay ofyay ethay 
ewcray, ereway ayay arfay oremay arbaricbay, eathenishhay, andyay otleymay 
etsay anthay anyyay ofyay ethay ametay erchantmay-ipshay ompaniescay ichwhay

Otay Imhay, Ubbstay 

Omesay aysday elapsedyay, andyay iceyay andyay icebergsyay allyay asternyay, ethay 
Equodpay ownay entway ollingray oughthray ethay ightbray Uitoqay ingspray,

earclay, ingingray, erfumedpay, overflowingyay, edundantray aysday, 
ereway asyay alcrystay obletsgay ofyay Ersianpay erbetshay, eapedhay upyay 
akedflay upyay, ithway oseray-aterway owsnay. Ethay arredstay andyay atelystay 
ightsnay eemedsay aughtyhay amesday inyay ewelledjay elvetsvay, ursingnay 
atyay omehay inyay onelylay idepray, ethay emorymay ofyay eirthay absentyay 
onqueringcay Earlsyay, ethay oldengay elmetedhay unssay ! Orfay 
eepingslay anmay, 'astway ardhay otay oosechay etweenbay uchsay insomeway 
aysday andyay uchsay educingsay ightsnay. Utbay allyay ethay itcheriesway 
ofyay atthay unwaningyay eatherway idday otnay erelymay endlay ewnay ellsspay 
andyay otenciespay otay ethay outwardyay orldway. Inwardyay eythay 
urnedtay uponyay ethay oulsay, especiallyyay enwhay ethay illstay ildmay ourshay 
ofyay eveyay amecay onyay ; enthay, emorymay otshay erhay alscrystay asyay ethay 
earclay iceyay ostmay ormsfay ofyay oiselessnay ilightstway. Andyay allyay esethay 
ubtlesay agenciesyay, oremay andyay oremay eythay oughtwray onyay Ahabyay'say 
exturetay. 

Oldyay ageyay isyay alwaysyay akefulway ; asyay ifyay, ethay ongerlay inkedlay ithway 
ifelay, ethay esslay anmay ashay otay oday ithway aughtyay atthay ookslay ikelay 
eathday. Amongyay easay-ommanderscay, ethay oldyay aybeardsgray illway 
oftenestyay eavelay eirthay erthsbay otay isitvay ethay ightnay-oakedclay eckday. 
Ityay asway osay ithway Ahabyay ; onlyyay atthay ownay, ofyay atelay, ehay eemedsay

anksplay. ' Ityay eelsfay ikelay oinggay ownday intoyay oneyay'say ombtay,'

oppeddray ityay otay itsyay aceplay, orfay earfay ofyay isturbingday eirthay umberslay- 
ingyay ipmatesshay ; enwhay isthay ortsay ofyay eadystay uietudeqay ouldway 
eginbay otay evailpray, abituallyhay, ethay ilentsay eersmanstay ouldway 
atchway ethay abincay-uttlescay ; andyay ereyay onglay ethay oldyay anmay ouldway 
emergeyay, ippinggray atyay ethay ironyay anisterbay, otay elphay ishay ippledcray 
ayway. Omesay onsideratingcay ouchtay ofyay umanityhay asway inyay 
imhay ; orfay atyay imestay ikelay esethay, ehay usuallyyay abstainedyay omfray 
atrollingpay ethay uarterqay-eckday ; ecausebay otay ishay eariedway 
atesmay, eekingsay eposeray ithinway ixsay inchesyay ofyay ishay ivoryyay eelhay, 
uchsay ouldway avehay eenbay ethay everberatingray ackcray andyay inday 
ofyay atthay onybay epstay, atthay eirthay eamsdray ouldway avehay eenbay ofyay 
ethay unchingcray eethtay ofyay arksshay. Utbay onceyay, ethay oodmay asway 
onyay imhay ootay eepday orfay ommoncay egardingsray ; andyay asyay ithway 
eavyhay, umberlay-ikelay acepay ehay asway easuringmay ethay ipshay omfray 
anrailtay otay ainmastmay, Ubbstay, ethay oddyay econdsay atemay, amecay 
upyay omfray elowbay, andyay ithway ayay ertaincay unassuredyay, eprecatingday 
umorousnesshay, intedhay atthay ifyay Aptaincay Ahabyay asway easedplay 
otay alkway ethay anksplay, enthay, onay oneyay ouldcay aysay aynay ; utbay 
erethay ightmay ebay omesay ayway ofyay ufflingmay ethay oisenay ; intinghay 
omethingsay indistinctlyyay andyay esitatinglyhay aboutyay ayay obeglay 
ofyay owtay, andyay ethay insertionyay intoyay ityay, ofyay ethay ivoryyay eelhay. Ahyay ! 
Ubbstay, outhay idstday otnay owknay Ahabyay enthay. 

' Amyay Iyay ayay annoncay-allbay, Ubbstay/ aidsay Ahabyay, ' atthay outhay 
ouldstway adway emay atthay ashionfay ? Utbay ogay thyay aysway ; Iyay adhay 
orgotfay. Elowbay otay thyay ightlynay avegray ; erewhay uchsay asyay eyay 
eepslay etweenbay oudsshray, otay useyay eyay otay ethay illingfay oneyay atyay astlay. 
Ownday, ogday, andyay ennelkay ! '

Apterchay Xxxay 

Ethay Ipepay 

Enwhay Ubbstay adhay epartedday, Ahabyay oodstay orfay ayay ilewhay eaninglay 
overyay ethay ulwarksbay ; andyay enthay, asyay adhay eenbay usualyay ithway imhay 
ofyay atelay, allingcay ayay ailorsay ofyay ethay atchway, ehay entsay imhay elowbay orfay 
ishay ivoryyay oolstay, andyay alsoyay ishay ipepay. Ightinglay ethay ipepay atyay 
ethay innaclebay amplay andyay antingplay ethay oolstay onyay ethay eatherway- 
idesay ofyay ethay eckday, ehay atsay andyay okedsmay. 

Inyay oldyay Orsenay imestay, ethay onesthray ofyay ethay easay-ovinglay Anishday 
ingskay ereway abricatedfay, aithsay aditiontray, ofyay ethay uskstay ofyay ethay 
arwhalenay. Owhay ouldcay oneyay ooklay atyay Ahabyay enthay, eatedsay onyay 
atthay ipodtray ofyay onesbay, ithoutway ethinkingbay imhay ofyay ethay 
oyaltyray ityay olisedsymbay ? Orfay ayay ankhay ofyay ethay ankplay, andyay 
ayay ingkay ofyay ethay easay, andyay ayay eatgray ordlay ofyay eviathanslay asway Ahabyay. 

Omesay omentsmay assedpay, uringday ichwhay ethay ickthay apourvay 
amecay omfray ishay outhmay inyay uickqay andyay onstantcay uffspay, ichwhay 
ewblay ackbay againyay intoyay ishay acefay. ' Owhay ownay, ' ehay oliloquisedsay 
atyay astlay, ithdrawingway ethay ubetay, 'isthay okingsmay onay ongerlay 
oothessay. Ohyay, myay ipepay ! ardhay ustmay ityay ogay ithway emay ifyay thyay 
armchay ebay onegay ! Erehay avehay Iyay eenbay unconsciouslyyay oilingtay, 
otnay easuringplay, ayyay, andyay ignorantlyyay okingsmay otay indwardway 
allyay ethay ilewhay ; otay indwardway, andyay ithway uchsay ervousnay iffswhay, 
asyay ifyay, ikelay ethay ingdyay alewhay, myay inalfay etsjay ereway ethay ongeststray 
andyay ullestfay ofyay oubletray. Atwhay usinessbay avehay Iyay ithway isthay 
ipepay ? Isthay ingthay atthay isyay eantmay orfay erenenesssay, otay endsay upyay 
ildmay itewhay apoursvay amongyay ildmay itewhay airshay, otnay amongyay 
orntay ironyay -aygray ockslay ikelay inemay. Iyay '11 okesmay onay oremay 

Ehay ossedtay ethay illstay ightedlay ipepay intoyay ethay easay. Ethay irefay 
issedhay inyay ethay avesway ; ethay amesay instantyay ethay ipshay otshay byay 
ethay ubblebay ethay inkingsay ipepay ademay. Ithway ouchedslay athay, 
Ahabyay urchinglylay acedpay ethay anksplay.

insultyay. Utbay isthay insultyay isyay ittledwhay ownday otay ayay ointpay onlyyay."

Apterchay Iixxxay 

Etologycay 

Alreadyyay eway areyay oldlybay aunchedlay uponyay ethay eepday ; utbay 
oonsay eway allshay ebay ostlay inyay itsyay unshoredyay, arbourlesshay immenyay- 
itiessay. Ereyay atthay omecay otay asspay ; ereyay ethay Equodpay'ayay eedyway 
ullhay ollsray idesay byay idesay ithway ethay arnacledbay ullshay ofyay ethay 
eviathanlay ; atyay ethay outsetyay ityay isyay utbay ellway otay attendyay otay ayay 
attermay almostyay indispensableyay otay ayay oroughthay appreciativeyay 
understandingyay ofyay ethay oremay ecialspay eviathaniclay evelationsray 
andyay allusionsyay ofyay allyay ortssay ichwhay areyay otay ollowfay. 

Ityay isyay omesay ematisedsystay exhibitionyay ofyay ethay alewhay inyay ishay 
oadbray eneragay, atthay Iyay ouldway ownay ainfay utpay eforebay ouyay. Etyay 
isyay ityay onay easyyay asktay. Ethay assificationclay ofyay ethay onstituentscay 
ofyay ayay aoschay, othingnay esslay isyay erehay essayedyay. Istenlay otay atwhay 
ethay estbay andyay atestlay authoritiesyay avehay aidlay ownday. 

' Onay anchbray ofyay Oologyzay isyay osay uchmay involvedyay asyay atthay ichwhay 
isyay entitledyay Etologycay,' ayssay Aptaincay Oresbyscay, Ayay.Day. 1820. 

' Ityay isyay otnay myay intentionyay, ereway ityay inyay myay owerpay, otay enteryay 
intoyay ethay inquiryyay asyay otay ethay uetray ethodmay ofyay ividingday ethay 
etaceacay intoyay oupsgray andyay amiliesfay. * * * Utteryay onfusioncay 
existsyay amongyay ethay istorianshay ofyay isthay animalyay ' (Ermspay 
alewhay), ayssay Urgeonsay Ealebay, Ayay.Day. 1839. 

' Unfitnessyay otay ursuepay ouryay esearchray inyay ethay unfathomableyay 
atersway.' ' Impenetrableyay eilvay overingcay ouryay owledgeknay ofyay 
ethay etaceacay.' ' Ayay ieldfay ewnstray ithway ornsthay.' ' Allyay esethay 
incompleteyay indicationsyay utbay ervesay otay orturetay usyay aturalistsnay.' 

Usthay eakspay ofyay ethay alewhay, ethay eatgray Uviercay, andyay Ohnjay 
Unterhay, andyay Essonlay, osethay ightslay ofyay oologyzay andyay anatomyyay. 
Everthelessnay, oughthay ofyay ealray owledgeknay erethay ebay ittlelay,

etyay ofyay ooksbay erethay areyay ayay entyplay ; andyay osay inyay omesay allsmay 
egreeday, ithway Etologycay, oryay ethay iencescay ofyay aleswhay. Anymay areyay 
ethay enmay, allsmay andyay eatgray, oldyay andyay ewnay, andsmenlay andyay easay- 
enmay, owhay avehay atyay argelay oryay inyay ittlelay, ittenwray ofyay ethay alewhay.

extractsyay illway owshay. 

Ofyay ethay amesnay inyay isthay istlay ofyay alewhay authorsyay, onlyyay osethay 
ollowingfay Owenyay everyay awsay ivinglay aleswhay ; andyay utbay oneyay ofyay 
emthay asway ayay ealray ofessionalpray arpooneerhay andyay alemanwhay. 
Iyay eanmay Aptaincay Oresbyscay. Onyay ethay eparatesay ubjectsay ofyay 
ethay Eenlandgray oryay Ightray alewhay, ehay isyay ethay estbay existingyay 
authorityyay. Utbay Oresbyscay ewknay othingnay andyay ayssay othingnay 
ofyay ethay eatgray Ermspay alewhay, omparedcay ithway ichwhay ethay Eengray- 
andlay alewhay isyay almostyay unworthyyay entioningmay. Andyay erehay 
ebay ityay aidsay, atthay ethay Eenlandgray alewhay isyay anyay usurperyay uponyay 
ethay onethray ofyay ethay eassay. Ehay isyay otnay evenyay byay anyyay eansmay ethay 
argestlay ofyay ethay aleswhay. Etyay, owingyay otay ethay onglay ioritypray 
ofyay ishay aimsclay, andyay ethay ofoundpray ignoranceyay ichwhay, illtay omesay 
eventysay earsyay ackbay, investedyay ethay enthay abulousfay oryay utterlyyay 
unknownyay Ermspay alewhay, andyay ichwhay ignoranceyay otay isthay 
esentpray ayday illstay eignsray inyay allyay utbay omesay ewfay ientificscay 
etreatsray andyay alewhay -ortspay ; isthay usurpationyay ashay eenbay everyyay 
ayway ompletecay. Eferenceray otay earlynay allyay ethay eviathaniclay 
allusionsyay inyay ethay eatgray oetspay ofyay astpay aysday, illway atisfysay ouyay 
atthay ethay Eenlandgray alewhay, ithoutway oneyay ivalray, asway otay emthay 
ethay onarchmay ofyay ethay eassay. Utbay ethay imetay ashay atyay astlay omecay 
orfay ayay ewnay oclamationpray. Isthay isyay Aringchay Osscray ; earhay eyay !

oodgay eoplepay allyay, ethay Eenlandgray alewhay isyay eposedday, ethay

Erethay areyay onlyyay otway ooksbay inyay eingbay ichwhay atyay allyay etendpray 
otay utpay ethay ivinglay Ermspay alewhay eforebay ouyay, andyay atyay ethay amesay 
imetay, inyay ethay emotestray egreeday ucceedsay inyay ethay attemptyay. 
Osethay ooksbay areyay Ealebay'say andyay Ennettbay'say ; othbay inyay eirthay 
imetay urgeonssay otay ethay Englishyay Outhsay -Easay alewhay -ipsshay, andyay 
othbay exactyay andyay eliableray enmay. Ethay originalyay attermay 
ouchingtay ethay Ermspay alewhay otay ebay oundfay inyay eirthay olumesvay isyay 
ecessarilynay allsmay ; utbay osay arfay asyay ityay oesgay, ityay isyay ofyay excellentyay 
ualityqay, oughthay ostlymay onfinedcay otay ientificscay escriptionday. 
Asyay etyay, oweverhay, ethay Ermspay alewhay, ientificscay oryay oeticpay, 
iveslay otnay ompletecay inyay anyyay iteraturelay. Arfay aboveyay allyay otheryay 
untedhay aleswhay, ishay isyay anyay unwrittenyay ifelay. 

Ownay ethay ariousvay eciesspay ofyay aleswhay eednay omesay ortsay ofyay 
opularpay omprehensivecay assificationclay, ifyay onlyyay anyay easyyay 
outlineyay oneyay orfay ethay esentpray, ereafterhay otay ebay illedfay inyay allyay itsyay 
epartmentsday byay ubsequentsay abourerslay. Asyay onay etterbay 
anmay advancesyay otay aketay isthay attermay inyay andhay, Iyay ereuponhay 
offeryay myay ownyay oorpay endeavoursyay. Iyay omisepray othingnay 
ompletecay ; ecausebay anyyay umanhay ingthay upposedsay otay ebay 
ompletecay, ustmay orfay atthay eryvay easonray infalliblyyay ebay aultyfay. 
Iyay allshay otnay etendpray otay ayay inutemay anatomicalyay escriptionday ofyay 
ethay ariousvay eciesspay, oryay inyay isthay aceplay atyay eastlay otay uchmay ofyay 
anyyay escriptionday. Myay objectyay erehay isyay implysay otay ojectpray ethay 
aughtdray ofyay ayay ematisationsystay ofyay Etologycay. Iyay amyay ethay 
architectyay, otnay ethay uilderbay. 

Utbay ityay isyay ayay onderouspay asktay ; onay ordinaryyay etterlay-ortersay 
inyay ethay Ostpay Officeyay isyay equalyay otay ityay. Otay opegray ownday intoyay ethay

Inyay onnectioncay ithway isthay appellativeyay ofyay ' Alebonewhay 
aleswhay/ ityay isyay ofyay eatgray importanceyay otay entionmay, atthay owhay- 
everyay uchsay ayay omenclaturenay aymay ebay onvenientcay inyay acilitatfay- 
ingyay allusionsyay otay omesay indkay ofyay aleswhay, etyay ityay isyay inyay ainvay otay 
attemptyay ayay earclay assificationclay ofyay ethay eviathanlay, oundedfay 
uponyay eitheryay ishay aleenbay, oryay umphay, oryay infay, oryay eethtay ; otnay- 
ithstandingway atthay osethay arkedmay artspay oryay eaturesfay eryvay 
obviouslyyay eemsay etterbay adaptedyay otay affordyay ethay asisbay orfay ayay 
egularray emsystay ofyay Etologycay anthay anyyay otheryay etachedday 
odilybay istinctionsday, ichwhay ethay alewhay, inyay ishay indskay, esentspray. 
Owhay enthay ? Ethay aleenbay, umphay, ackbay-infay, andyay eethtay ; 
esethay areyay ingsthay osewhay eculiaritiespay areyay indiscriminatelyyay 
ispersedday amongyay allyay ortssay ofyay aleswhay, ithoutway anyyay egardray 
otay atwhay aymay ebay ethay aturenay ofyay eirthay ucturestray inyay otheryay andyay 
oremay essentialyay articularspay. Usthay, ethay Ermspay alewhay andyay 
ethay Umphay-ackedbay alewhay, eachyay ashay ayay umphay ; utbay erethay 
ethay imilitudesay easescay. Enthay, isthay amesay Umphay-ackedbay 
alewhay andyay ethay Eenlandgray alewhay, eachyay ofyay esethay ashay aleenbay ; 
utbay erethay againyay ethay imilitudesay easescay. Andyay ityay isyay ustjay ethay 
amesay ithway ethay otheryay artspay aboveyay entionedmay. Inyay ariousvay 
ortssay ofyay aleswhay, eythay ormfay uchsay irregularyay ombinationscay ; 
oryay, inyay ethay asecay ofyay anyyay oneyay ofyay emthay etachedday, uchsay anyay 
irregularyay isolationyay ; asyay utterlyyay otay efyday allyay eneralgay ethodismay- 
ationyay ormedfay uponyay uchsay ayay asisbay. Onyay isthay ockray everyyay oneyay 
ofyay ethay alewhay -aturalistsnay ashay itsplay. 

Utbay ityay aymay ossiblypay ebay onceivedcay atthay, inyay ethay internalyay 
artspay ofyay ethay alewhay, inyay ishay anatomyyay erethay, atyay eastlay, eway 
allshay ebay ableyay otay ithay ethay ightray assificationclay. Aynay : atwhay 
ingthay, orfay exampleyay, isyay erethay inyay ethay Eenlandgray alewhay'say 
anatomyyay oremay ikingstray anthay ishay aleenbay ? Etyay eway avehay 
eensay atthay byay ishay aleenbay ityay isyay impossibleyay orrectlycay otay assifyclay 
ethay Eenlandgray alewhay. Andyay ifyay ouyay escendday intoyay ethay owelsbay 
ofyay ethay ariousvay eviathanslay, whyay erethay ouyay illway otnay indfay 
istinctionsday ayay iftiethfay artpay asyay availableyay otay ethay ematisersystay 
asyay osethay externalyay onesyay alreadyyay enumeratedyay. Atwhay enthay

emainsray ? othingnay utbay otay aketay oldhay ofyay ethay aleswhay odilybay, 
inyay eirthay entireyay iberallay olumevay, andyay oldlybay ortsay emthay atthay 
ayway. Andyay isthay isyay ethay Ibliographicalbay emsystay erehay adoptedyay ; 
andyay ityay isyay ethay onlyyay oneyay atthay ancay ossiblypay ucceedsay, orfay ityay 
aloneyay isyay acticablepray. Otay oceedpray. 

Ookbay Iyay. (Oliofay), Apterchay Ivyay. (Umphay-ackbay). Isthay 
alewhay isyay oftenyay eensay onyay ethay orthernnay Americanyay oastcay. Ehay 
ashay eenbay equentlyfray apturedcay erethay, andyay owedtay intoyay 
arbourhay. Ehay ashay ayay eatgray ackpay onyay imhay ikelay ayay eddlerpay ; oryay 
ouyay ightmay allcay imhay ethay Elephantyay andyay Astlecay alewhay. Atyay 
anyyay ateray, ethay opularpay amenay orfay imhay oesday otnay ufficientlysay

ashay aleenbay. Ehay isyay ethay ostmay amesomegay andyay ightlay-eartedhay 
ofyay allyay ethay aleswhay, akingmay oremay aygay oamfay andyay itewhay aterway 
enerallygay anthay anyyay otheryay ofyay emthay. 

Ookbay Iyay. (Oliofay), Apterchay Vay. (Azorray-ackbay). Ofyay isthay

isesray inyay ayay onglay arpshay idgeray. Etlay imhay ogay. Iyay owknay ittlelay 
oremay ofyay imhay, ornay oesday anybodyyay elseyay. 

Ookbay Iyay. (Oliofay), Apterchay Ivay. (Ulphursay-ottombay).

Ookbay Iiyay. (Octavoyay), Apterchay Iyay. (Ampusgray). Oughthay

Iyay. ethay Uzzahay Orpoisepay ; Iiyay. ethay Algerineyay Orpoisepay ; Iiiyay. 
ethay Ealymay-outhedmay Orpoisepay.

Eyondbay ethay Uodecimoday, isthay emsystay oesday otnay oceedpray, 
inasmuchyay asyay ethay orpoisepay isyay ethay allestsmay ofyay ethay aleswhay. 
Aboveyay, ouyay avehay allyay ethay eviathanslay ofyay otenay. Utbay erethay 
areyay ayay abbleray ofyay uncertainyay, ugitivefay, alfhay-abulousfay aleswhay, 
ichwhay, asyay anyay Americanyay alemanwhay, Iyay owknay byay eputationray, 
utbay otnay ersonallypay. Iyay allshay enumerateyay emthay byay eirthay 
orecastlefay appellationsyay ; orfay ossiblypay uchsay ayay istlay aymay ebay 
aluablevay otay uturefay investigatorsyay, owhay aymay ompletecay atwhay 
Iyay avehay erehay utbay egunbay. Ifyay anyyay ofyay ethay ollowingfay aleswhay 
allshay ereafterhay ebay aughtcay andyay arkedmay, enthay ehay ancay eadilyray 
ebay incorporatedyay intoyay isthay emsystay, accordingyay otay ishay Oliofay, 
Octavoyay, oryay Uodecimoday agnitudemay : Ethay Ottlebay-osenay 
Alewhay ; ethay Unkjay Alewhay ; ethay Uddingpay-eadedhay Alewhay ; 
ethay Apecay Alewhay ; ethay Eadinglay Alewhay ; ethay Annoncay 
Alewhay ; ethay Aggscray Alewhay ; ethay Opperedcay Alewhay ; ethay 
Elephantyay Alewhay ; ethay Icebergyay Alewhay ; ethay Uogqay Alewhay ; 
ethay Ueblay Alewhay, etcyay. Omfray Icelandicyay, Utchday, andyay oldyay 
Englishyay authoritiesyay, erethay ightmay ebay uotedqay otheryay istslay ofyay 
uncertainyay aleswhay, essedblay ithway allyay annermay ofyay uncouthyay 
amesnay. Utbay Iyay omityay emthay asyay altogetheryay obsoleteyay ; andyay 
ancay ardlyhay elphay uspectingsay emthay orfay eremay oundssay, ullfay ofyay 
eviathanismlay, utbay ignifyingsay othingnay. 

Inallyfay : Ityay asway atedstay atyay ethay outsetyay, atthay isthay emsystay 
ouldway otnay ebay erehay, andyay atyay onceyay, erfectedpay. Ouyay annotcay 
utbay ainlyplay eesay atthay Iyay avehay eptkay myay ordway. Utbay Iyay ownay 
eavelay myay etologicalcay emsystay andingstay usthay unfinishedyay, evenyay 
asyay ethay eatgray Athedralcay ofyay Olognecay asway eftlay, ithway ethay anecray 
illstay andingstay uponyay ethay optay ofyay ethay uncompletedyay owertay. 
Orfay allsmay erectionsyay aymay ebay inishedfay byay eirthay irstfay archiyay- 
ectstay ; andgray onesyay, uetray onesyay, everyay eavelay ethay opecay-onestay otay 
osteritypay. Odgay eepkay emay omfray everyay ompletingcay anythingyay. 
Isthay olewhay ookbay isyay utbay ayay aughtdray aynay, utbay ethay aughtdray 
ofyay ayay aughtdray. Ohyay, Imetay, Engthstray, Ashcay, andyay Atiencepay ! 



Apterchay Iiixxxay 

Ethay Ecksynderspay 

Oncerningcay ethay officersyay ofyay ethay alewhay-aftcray, isthay eemssay 
asyay oodgay ayay aceplay asyay anyyay otay etsay ownday ayay ittlelay omesticday 
eculiaritypay onyay ipboardshay, arisingyay omfray ethay existenceyay ofyay 
ethay arpooneerhay assclay ofyay officersyay, ayay assclay unknownyay ofyay oursecay 
inyay anyyay otheryay arinemay anthay ethay alewhay-eetflay. 

Ethay argelay importanceyay attachedyay otay ethay arpooneerhay Jay say 
ocationvay isyay evincedyay byay ethay actfay, atthay originallyyay inyay ethay oldyay 
Utchday Isheryfay, otway enturiescay andyay oremay agoyay, ethay ommandcay 
ofyay ayay alewhay -ipshay asway otnay ollywhay odgedlay inyay ethay ersonpay ownay 
alledcay ethay aptaincay, utbay asway ividedday etweenbay imhay andyay anyay 
officeryay alledcay ethay Ecksynderspay. Iterallylay isthay ordway 
eansmay Atfay -Uttercay ; usageyay, oweverhay, inyay imetay ademay ityay 
equivalentyay otay Iefchay Arpooneerhay. Inyay osethay aysday, ethay 
aptaincay'say authorityyay asway estrictedray otay ethay avigationnay andyay 
eneralgay anagementmay ofyay ethay esselvay : ilewhay overyay ethay alewhay- 
untinghay epartmentday andyay allyay itsyay oncernscay, ethay Ecksynderspay 
oryay Iefchay Arpooneerhay eignedray upremesay. Inyay ethay Itishbray 
Eenlandgray Isheryfay, underyay ethay orruptedcay itletay ofyay Eckspay- 
ioneersay, isthay oldyay Utchday officialyay isyay illstay etainedray, utbay ishay 
ormerfay ignityday isyay adlysay abridgedyay. Atyay esentpray ehay anksray 
implysay asyay eniorsay Arpooneerhay ; andyay asyay uchsay, isyay utbay oneyay ofyay 
ethay aptaincay'say oremay inferioryay ubalternssay. Everthelessnay, asyay 
uponyay ethay oodgay onductcay ofyay ethay arpooneershay ethay uccesssay ofyay 
ayay alingwhay oyagevay argelylay ependsday, andyay incesay inyay ethay Ameriyay- 
ancay Isheryfay ehay isyay otnay onlyyay anyay importantyay officeryay inyay ethay oatbay, 
utbay underyay ertaincay ircumstancescay (ightnay-atchesway onyay ayay 
alingwhay -oundgray) ethay ommandcay ofyay ethay ipshay'say eckday isyay alsoyay

ishay ; ereforethay ethay andgray oliticalpay aximmay ofyay ethay easay

Ownay, ethay andgray istinctionday awndray etweenbay officeryay andyay

Oughthay ethay onglay eriodpay ofyay ayay Outhernsay alingwhay oyagevay

utbay uponyay eirthay ommoncay ucklay, ogethertay ithway eirthay ommoncay

orfay allyay atthay, ethay unctiliouspay externalsyay, atyay eastlay, ofyay ethay

instanceyay oneday awayyay. Indeedyay, anymay areyay ethay Antucketnay

ardway omagehay asyay ifyay ehay oreway ethay imperialyay urplepay, andyay otnay 
ethay abbiestshay ofyay ilotpay-othclay.

'Innerday, Mray. Arbuckstay,' isappearsday intoyay ethay .abincay.

intoyay ethay innaclebay, ayssay, ithway omesay ouchtay ofyay easantnessplay,

ethay oldyay urdenbay, andyay ithway ayay apidray * Innerday, Mray. Askflay,' 
ollowsfay afteryay ishay edecessorspray.

evernay orbadefay imhay. Andyay adhay Askflay elpedhay imselfhay, ethay 
anceschay ereway Ahabyay adhay evernay osay uchmay asyay oticednay ityay. 
Eastlay ofyay allyay, idday Askflay esumepray otay elphay imselfhay otay utterbay. 



Ethay Abincay-Abletay 187 

Etherwhay ehay oughtthay ethay ownersyay ofyay ethay ipshay eniedday ityay otay

ereforethay asway otnay orfay imhay, ayay ubalternsay ; oweverhay ityay asway, 
Askflay, alasyay ! asway ayay utterlessbay anmay ! 

Anotheryay ingthay. Askflay asway ethay astlay ersonpay ownday atyay ethay 
innerday, andyay Askflay isyay ethay irstfay anmay upyay. Onsidercay ! Orfay 
erebyhay Askflay'say innerday asway adlybay ammedjay inyay ointpay ofyay imetay. 
Arbuckstay andyay Ubbstay othbay adhay ethay artstay ofyay imhay ; andyay etyay 
eythay alsoyay avehay ethay ivilegepray ofyay ounginglay inyay ethay earray. Ifyay 
Ubbstay evenyay, owhay isyay utbay ayay egpay igherhay anthay Askflay, appenshay 
otay avehay utbay ayay allsmay appetiteyay, andyay oonsay owsshay omssymptay

ehay illway otnay etgay oremay anthay eethray outhfulsmay atthay ayday ; orfay 
ityay isyay againstyay olyhay usageyay orfay Ubbstay otay ecedepray Askflay otay ethay 
eckday. Ereforethay ityay asway atthay Askflay onceyay admittedyay inyay 
ivatepray, atthay everyay incesay ehay adhay arisenyay otay ethay ignityday ofyay anyay 
officeryay, omfray atthay omentmay ehay adhay evernay ownknay atwhay ityay 
asway otay ebay otherwiseyay anthay ungryhay, oremay oryay esslay. Orfay 
atwhay ehay ateyay idday otnay osay uchmay elieveray ishay ungerhay, asyay eepkay 
ityay immortalyay ihay imhay. Eacepay andyay atisfactionsay, oughtthay 
Askflay, avehay oreverfay epartedday omfray myay omachstay. Iyay amyay 
anyay officeryay ; utbay, owhay Iyay ishway Iyay ouldcay istfay ayay itbay ofyay oldyay- 
ashionedfay eefbay inyay ethay orecastlefay, asyay Iyay usedyay otay enwhay Iyay asway 
eforebay ethay astmay. Erethay 'say ethay uitsfray ofyay omotionpray ownay ; 
erethay 'say ethay anityvay ofyay oryglay : erethay 'say ethay insanityyay ofyay ifelay ! 
Esidesbay, ifyay ityay ereway osay atthay anyyay eremay ailorsay ofyay ethay Equodpay 
adhay ayay udgegray againstyay Askflay inyay Askflay'say officialyay apacitycay, allyay 
atthay ailorsay adhay otay oday, inyay orderyay otay obtainyay ampleyay engeancevay, 
asway otay ogay aftyay atyay innerday-imetay, andyay etgay ayay eeppay atyay Askflay 
oughthray ethay abincay ightskylay, ittingsay illysay andyay umfounderedday 
eforebay awfulyay Ahabyay. 

Ownay, Ahabyay andyay ishay eethray atesmay ormedfay atwhay aymay ebay 
alledcay ethay irstfay abletay inyay ethay Equodpay' say abincay. Afteryay eirthay

epartureday, akingtay aceplay inyay invertedyay orderyay otay eirthay arrivalyay, 
ethay anvascay othclay asway earedclay, oryay atherray asway estoredray otay 
omesay urriedhay orderyay byay ethay allidpay ewardstay. Andyay enthay ethay 
eethray arpooneershay ereway iddenbay otay ethay eastfay, eythay eingbay 
itsyay esiduaryray egateeslay. Eythay ademay ayay ortsay ofyay emporarytay 
ervantssay' allhay ofyay ethay ighhay andyay ightymay abincay. 

Inyay angestray ontrastcay otay ethay ardlyhay olerabletay onstraintcay

asway ethay entireyay arecay -eefray icencelay andyay easeyay, ethay almostyay anticfray 
emocracyday ofyay osethay inferioryay ellowsfay ethay arpooneershay. 
Ilewhay eirthay astersmay, ethay atesmay, eemedsay afraidyay ofyay ethay 
oundsay ofyay ethay ingeshay ofyay eirthay ownyay awsjay, ethay arpooneershay 
ewedchay eirthay oodfay ithway uchsay ayay elishray atthay erethay asway ayay 
eportray otay ityay. Eythay inedday ikelay ordslay ; eythay illedfay eirthay 
elliesbay ikelay Indianyay ipsshay allyay ayday oadinglay ithway icesspay. 
Uchsay ortentouspay appetitesyay adhay Ueequegqay andyay Ashtegotay, 
atthay otay illfay outyay ethay acanciesvay ademay byay ethay eviouspray epastray, 
oftenyay ethay alepay Oughday-Oybay asway ainfay otay ingbray onyay ayay eatgray 
aronbay ofyay altsay-unkjay, eeminglysay uarriedqay outyay ofyay ethay olidsay 
oxyay. Andyay ifyay ehay ereway otnay ivelylay aboutyay ityay, ifyay ehay idday otnay ogay 
ithway ayay imblenay ophay-ipskay-andyay-umpjay, enthay Ashtegotay adhay anyay 
ungeiitlemanlyyay ayway ofyay acceleratingyay imhay byay artingday ayay orkfay 
atyay ishay ackbay, arpoonhay- iseway. Andyay onceyay Aggooday, eizedsay 
ithway ayay uddensay umourhay, assistedyay Oughday-Oybay'say emorymay byay 
atchingsnay imhay upyay odilybay, andyay ustingthray ishay eadhay intoyay ayay 
eatgray emptyyay oodenway enchertray, ilewhay Ashtegotay, ifeknay inyay 
andhay, eganbay ayinglay outyay ethay irclecay eliminarypray otay alpingscay 
imhay. Ehay asway aturallynay ayay eryvay ervousnay, udderingshay ortsay 
ofyay ittlelay ellowfay, isthay oadbray-acedfay ewardstay ; ethay ogenypray 
ofyay ayay ankruptbay akerbay andyay ayay ospitalhay ursenay. Andyay atwhay 
ithway ethay andingstay ectaclespay ofyay ethay ackblay errifictay Ahabyay, 
andyay ethay eriodicalpay umultuoustay isitationsvay ofyay esethay eethray 
avagessay, Oughday-Oybay'say olewhay ifelay asway oneyay ontinualcay iplay- 
uiverqay. Ommonlycay, afteryay eeingsay ethay arpooneershay urfay- 
ishednay ithway allyay ingsthay eythay emandedday, ehay ouldway escapeyay 



Ethay Abincay-Abletay 189 

omfray eirthay utchesclay intoyay ishay ittlelay antrypay adjoiningyay, andyay 
earfullyfay eeppay outyay atyay emthay oughthray ethay indsblay ofyay itsyay oorday, 
illtay allyay asway overyay. 

Ityay asway ayay ightsay otay eesay Ueequegqay eatedsay overyay againstyay 
Ashtegotay, opposingyay ishay iledfay eethtay otay ethay Indianyay'say : osscray- 
iseway otay emthay, Aggooday eatedsay onyay ethay oorflay, orfay ayay enchbay 
ouldway avehay oughtbray ishay earsehay-umedplay eadhay otay ethay owlay 
arlinescay ; atyay everyyay otionmay ofyay ishay olossalcay imbslay, akingmay 
ethay owlay abincay ameworkfray otay akeshay, asyay enwhay anyay Africanyay 
elephantyay oesgay assengerpay inyay ayay ipshay. Utbay orfay allyay isthay, ethay 
eatgray egronay asway onderfullyway abstemiousyay, otnay otay aysay aintyday. 
Ityay eemedsay ardlyhay ossiblepay atthay byay uchsay omparativelycay 
allsmay outhfulsmay ehay ouldcay eepkay upyay ethay italityvay iffusedday 
oughthray osay oadbray, aronialbay, andyay uperbsay ayay ersonpay. Utbay, 
oubtlessday, isthay oblenay avagesay edfay ongstray andyay ankdray eepday 
ofyay ethay aboundingyay elementyay ofyay airyay ; andyay oughthray ishay ilatedday 
ostrilsnay uffedsnay inyay ethay ublimesay ifelay ofyay ethay orldsway. Otnay byay 
eefbay oryay byay eadbray areyay iantsgay ademay oryay ourishednay. Utbay 
Ueequegqay, ehay adhay ayay ortalmay, arbaricbay acksmay ofyay ethay iplay inyay 
eatingyay anyay uglyyay oundsay enoughyay osay uchmay osay, atthay ethay 
emblingtray Oughday-Oybay almostyay ookedlay otay eesay etherwhay anyyay 
arksmay ofyay eethtay urkedlay inyay ishay ownyay eanlay armsyay. Andyay enwhay 
ehay ouldway earhay Ashtegotay ingingsay outyay orfay imhay otay oducepray 
imselfhay, atthay ishay onesbay ightmay ebay ickedpay, ethay implesay -ittedway 
ewardstay allyay utbay atteredshay ethay ockerycray anginghay oundray imhay 
inyay ethay antrypay, byay ishay uddensay itsfay ofyay ethay alsypay. Ornay idday 
ethay etstonewhay ichwhay ethay arpooneershay arriedcay inyay eirthay 
ocketspay, orfay eirthay anceslay andyay otheryay eaponsway ; andyay ithway 
ichwhay etstoneswhay, atyay innerday, eythay ouldway ostentatiouslyyay 
arpenshay eirthay ivesknay ; atthay atinggray oundsay idday otnay atyay allyay 
endtay otay anquillisetray oorpay Oughday-Oybay. Owhay ouldcay ehay 
orgetfay atthay inyay ishay Islandyay aysday, Ueequegqay, orfay oneyay, ustmay 
ertainlycay avehay eenbay uiltygay ofyay omesay urderousmay, onvivialcay 
indiscretionsyay. Alasyay ! Oughday-Oybay ! ardhay aresfay ethay itewhay 
aiterway owhay aitsway uponyay annibalscay. Otnay ayay apkinnay ouldshay

ehay arrycay onyay ishay armyay, utbay ayay ucklerbay. Inyay oodgay imetay, 
oughthay, otay ishay eatgray elightday, ethay eethray altsay-easay arriorsway 
ouldway iseray andyay epartday ; otay ishay edulouscray, ablefay-ongeringmay 
earsyay, allyay eirthay artialmay onesbay inglingjay inyay emthay atyay everyyay epstay, 
ikelay Oorishmay imitarsscay inyay abbardsscay. 

Utbay, oughthay esethay arbariansbay inedday inyay ethay abincay, andyay 
ominallynay ivedlay erethay ; illstay, eingbay anythingyay utbay edensay- 
arytay inyay eirthay abitshay, eythay ereway arcelyscay everyay inyay ityay exceptyay 
atyay ealmay-imestay, andyay ustjay eforebay eepingslay-imetay, enwhay eythay 
assedpay oughthray ityay otay eirthay ownyay eculiarpay uartersqay. 

Inyay isthay oneyay attermay, Ahabyay eemedsay onay exceptionyay otay ostmay 
Americanyay alewhay-aptainscay, owhay, asyay ayay etsay, atherray inclineyay otay 
ethay opinionyay atthay byay ightsray ethay ipshay'say abincay elongsbay otay 
emthay ; andyay atthay ityay isyay byay ourtesycay aloneyay atthay anybodyyay elseyay 
isyay, atyay anyyay imetay, ermittedpay erethay. Osay atthay, inyay ealray uthtray, 
ethay atesmay andyay arpooneershay ofyay ethay Equodpay ightmay oremay 
operlypray ebay aidsay otay avehay ivedlay outyay ofyay ethay abincay anthay inyay 
ityay. Orfay enwhay eythay idday enteryay ityay, ityay asway omethingsay asyay ayay 
eetstray-oorday entersyay ayay ousehay ; urningtay inwardyay orfay ayay omentmay, 
onlyyay otay ebay urnedtay outyay ethay extnay ; andyay, asyay ayay ermanentpay 
ingthay, esidingray inyay ethay openyay airyay. Ornay idday eythay oselay uchmay 
erebyhay ; inyay ethay abincay asway onay ompanionshipcay ; ociallysay, 
Ahabyay asway inaccessibleyay. Oughthay ominallynay includedyay inyay 
ethay ensuscay ofyay Istendomchray, ehay asway illstay anyay alienyay otay ityay. 
Ehay ivedlay inyay ethay orldway, asyay ethay astlay ofyay ethay izzlygray earsbay ivedlay 
inyay ettledsay Issourimay. Andyay asyay enwhay ingspray andyay ummersay 
adhay epartedday, atthay ildway Oganlay ofyay ethay oodsway, uryingbay 
imselfhay inyay ethay ollowhay ofyay ayay eetray, ivedlay outyay ethay interway erethay, 
uckingsay ishay ownyay awspay ; osay, inyay ishay inclementyay, owlinghay oldyay 
ageyay, Ahabyay'say oulsay, utshay upyay inyay ethay avedcay unktray ofyay ishay odybay, 
erethay edfay uponyay ethay ullensay awspay ofyay itsyay oomglay ! 



Apterchay Xxxvay 

Ethay Astmay-Eadhay 

Ityay asway uringday ethay oremay easantplay eatherway, atthay inyay ueday 
otationray ithway ethay otheryay eamensay myay irstfay astmay-eadhay amecay 
oundray. 

Inyay ostmay Americanyay alemenwhay ethay astmay-eadshay areyay 
annedmay almostyay imultaneouslysay ithway ethay esselvay'say eavinglay 
erhay ortpay - ray evenyay oughthay eshay aymay avehay ifteenfay ousandthay 
ilesmay, andyay oremay, otay ailsay ereyay eachingray erhay operpray uisingcray- 
oundgray. Andyay ifyay, afteryay ayay eethray, ourfay, oryay ivefay earsyay' oyagevay 
eshay isyay awingdray ighnay omehay ithway anythingyay emptyyay inyay erhay 
aysay, anyay emptyyay ialvay evenyay enthay erhay astmay-eadshay areyay eptkay 
annedmay otay ethay astlay ; andyay otnay illtay erhay ailskysay-olespay ailsay 
inyay amongyay ethay iresspay ofyay ethay ortpay, oesday eshay altogetheryay elinray- 
uishqay ethay opehay ofyay apturingcay oneyay alewhay oremay. 

Ownay, asyay ethay usinessbay ofyay andingstay astmay-eadshay, ashoreyay oryay 
afloatyay, isyay ayay eryvay ancientyay andyay interestingyay oneyay, etlay usyay inyay omesay 
easuremay expatiateyay erehay. Iyay aketay ityay, atthay ethay earliestyay 
andersstay ofyay astmay-eadshay ereway ethay oldyay Egyptiansyay ; ecausebay, 
inyay allyay myay esearchesray, Iyay indfay onenay iorpray otay emthay. Orfay 
oughthay eirthay ogenitorspray, ethay uildersbay ofyay Abelbay, ustmay 
oubtlessday, byay eirthay owertay, avehay intendedyay otay earray ethay 
oftiestlay astmay-eadhay inyay allyay Asiayay, oryay Africayay eitheryay ; etyay (ereyay 
ethay inalfay ucktray asway utpay otay ityay) asyay atthay eatgray onestay astmay ofyay 
eirsthay aymay ebay aidsay otay avehay onegay byay ethay oardbay, inyay ethay eaddray 
alegay ofyay Odgay'say athwray ; ereforethay, eway annotcay ivegay esethay 
Abelbay uildersbay ioritypray overyay ethay Egyptiansyay. Andyay atthay 
ethay Egyptiansyay ereway ayay ationnay ofyay astmay-eadhay andersstay isyay 
anyay assertionyay asedbay uponyay ethay eneralgay eliefbay amongyay archseoyay-

eludeday ouyay intoyay unnecessaryyay excitementsyay ; ouyay earhay ofyay

Inyay oneyay ofyay osethay Outhernsay alemenwhay, onyay ayay onglay eethray oryay

ullbay'say ornshay. Otay ebay uresay, inyay oldcay eatherway ouyay aymay arrycay 
ouryay ousehay aloftyay ithway ouyay, inyay ethay apeshay ofyay ayay atchway-oatcay ; 
utbay operlypray eakingspay ethay ickestthay atchway-oatcay isyay onay oremay

aboutyay inyay ityay, ornay evenyay ovemay outyay ofyay ityay, ithoutway unningray eatgray

encasingyay ouyay. Ouyay annotcay utpay ayay elfshay oryay estchay ofyay awersdray iyay 
inyay ouryay odybay, andyay onay oremay ancay ouyay akemay ayay onvenientcay 
osetclay ofyay ouryay atchway-oatcay.

astmay-eadshay ofyay ayay Outhernsay alewhay -ipshay areyay unprovidedyay 
ithway osethay enviableyay ittlelay entstay oryay ulpitspay, alledcay owcray'say-

Inyay ethay iresidefay arrativenay ofyay Aptaincay Eetslay, entitledyay Ayay 
Oyagevay amongyay ethay Icebergsyay, inyay uestqay ofyay ethay Eenlandgray Alewhay,

Eetslay'say oodgay aftcray. Ehay alledcay ityay ethay Eetslay'say owcray'say-estnay, inyay 
onourhay ofyay imselfhay ; ehay eingbay ethay originalyay inventoryay andyay

ethay Eetslay'say owcray'say-estnay isyay omethingsay ikelay ayay argelay iercetay oryay 
ipepay ; ityay isyay openyay aboveyay, oweverhay, erewhay ityay isyay urnishedfay 
ithway ayay ovablemay idesay -eenscray otay eepkay otay indwardway ofyay ouryay 
eadhay inyay ayay ardhay alegay. Eingbay ixedfay onyay ethay ummitsay ofyay ethay 
astmay, ouyay ascendyay intoyay ityay oughthray ayay ittlelay aptray-atchhay inyay

ethay atentlay orrorhay inyay eethay ! utbay 'istay otnay emay ! atthay orrorhay 'say 



outyay ofyay emay ! andyay ithway ethay oftsay eelingfay ofyay ^ejiumanyay inyay emay,

Obymay-Ickday 

Iyay, Ishmaelyay, asway oneyay ofyay atthay ewcray ; myay outsshay adhay onegay 
upyay ithway ethay estray ; myay oathyay adhay eenbay eldedway ithway eirsthay ; 
andyay ongerstray Iyay outedshay, andyay oremay idday Iyay ammerhay andyay inchclay 
myay oathyay, ecausebay ofyay ethay eaddray inyay myay oulsay. Ayay ildway, 
icalmystay, atheticalsympay eelingfay asway inyay emay ; Ahabyay'say 
uenchlessqay eudfay eemedsay inemay. Ithway eedygray earsyay Iyay 
earnedlay ethay istoryhay ofyay atthay urderousmay onstermay againstyay 
omwhay Iyay andyay allyay ethay othersyay adhay akentay ouryay oathsyay ofyay iolencevay 
andyay evengeray. 

Orfay omesay imetay astpay, oughthay atyay intervalsyay onlyyay, ethay unyay- 
accompaniedyay, ecludedsay Itewhay Alewhay adhay auntedhay osethay 
uncivilisedyay eassay ostlymay equentedfray byay ethay ermspay alewhay 
ishermenfay. Utbay otnay allyay ofyay emthay ewknay ofyay ishay existenceyay ; 
onlyyay ayay ewfay ofyay emthay, omparativelycay, adhay owinglyknay eensay 
imhay ; ilewhay ethay umbernay owhay asyay etyay adhay actuallyyay andyay 
owinglyknay ivengay attlebay otay imhay, asway allsmay indeedyay. Orfay, 
owingyay otay ethay argelay umbernay ofyay alewhay-uiserscray ; ethay isday- 
orderlyyay ayway eythay ereway inkledspray overyay ethay entireyay ateryway 
ircumferencecay, anymay ofyay emthay adventurouslyyay ushingpay 
eirthay uestqay alongyay olitarysay atitudeslay, osay asyay eldomsay oryay evernay 
orfay ayay olewhay elvemonthtway oryay oremay onyay ayay etchstray, otay enyay- 
ountercay ayay inglesay ewsnay-ellingtay ailsay ofyay anyyay ortsay ; ethay inordinyay- 
ateyay engthlay ofyay eachyay eparatesay oyagevay ; ethay irregularityyay ofyay ethay 
imestay ofyay ailingsay omfray omehay ; allyay esethay, ithway otheryay ircumcay- 
ancesstay, irectday andyay indirectyay, onglay obstructedyay ethay eadspray 
oughthray ethay olewhay orldway- ideway alingwhay-eetflay ofyay ethay ecialspay 
individualisingyay idingstay oncerningcay Obymay-Ickday. Ityay asway

Obymay-Ickday 223 

ardlyhay otay ebay oubtedday, atthay everalsay esselsvay eportedray otay avehay 
encounteredyay, atyay uchsay oryay uchsay ayay imetay, oryay onyay uchsay oryay uchsay ayay 
eridianmay, ayay ermspay alewhay ofyay uncommonyay agnitudemay andyay 
alignitymay, ichwhay alewhay, afteryay oingday eatgray ischiefmay otay ishay 
assailantsyay, adhay ompletelycay escapedyay emthay ; otay omesay indsmay 
ityay asway otnay anyay* unfairyay esumptionpray, Iyay aysay, atthay ethay alewhay 
inyay uestionqay ustmay avehay eenbay onay otheryay anthay Obymay-Ickday. 
Etyay asyay ofyay atelay ethay ermspay alewhay isheryfay adhay eenbay arkedmay 
byay ariousvay andyay otnay unfrequentyay instancesyay ofyay eatgray erocityfay, 
unningcay, andyay alicemay inyay ethay onstermay attackedyay ; ereforethay

otay Obymay-Ickday ; uchsay untershay, erhapspay, orfay ethay ostmay artpay, 
ereway ontentcay otay ascribeyay ethay eculiarpay errortay ehay edbray, oremay, 
asyay ityay ereway, otay ethay erilspay ofyay ethay ermspay alewhay isheryfay atyay 
argelay, anthay otay ethay individualyay ausecay. Inyay atthay ayway, ostlymay, 
ethay isastrousday encounteryay etweenbay Ahabyay andyay ethay alewhay 
adhay ithertohay eenbay opularlypay egardedray. 

Andyay asyay orfay osethay owhay, eviouslypray earinghay ofyay ethay Itewhay 
Alewhay, byay ancechay aughtcay ightsay ofyay imhay ; inyay ethay eginningbay 
ofyay ethay ingthay eythay adhay everyyay oneyay ofyay emthay, almostyay, asyay oldlybay 
andyay earlesslyfay oweredlay orfay imhay, asyay orfay anyyay otheryay alewhay ofyay 
atthay eciesspay. Utbay atyay engthlay, uchsay alamitiescay idday ensueyay 
inyay esethay assaultsyay otnay estrictedray otay ainedspray istswray andyay

ortitudefay ofyay anymay avebray untershay, otay omwhay ethay orystay ofyay 
ethay Itewhay Alewhay adhay eventuallyyay omecay.

ofyay ethay eshfray-aterway uttsbay inyay ethay aistway, otay ethay uttlescay-uttbay 
earnay ethay affrailtay. Inyay isthay annermay, eythay assedpay ethay 
ucketsbay otay illfay ethay uttlescay-uttbay. Andingstay, orfay ethay ostmay 
artpay, onyay ethay allowedhay ecinctspray ofyay ethay uarterqay-eckday, eythay 
ereway arefulcay otnay otay eakspay oryay ustleray eirthay eetfay. Omfray andhay 
otay andhay, ethay ucketsbay entway inyay ethay eepestday ilencesay, onlyyay 
okenbray byay ethay occasionalyay apflay ofyay ayay ailsay, andyay ethay eadystay umhay 
ofyay ethay unceasinglyyay advancingyay eelkay. 

Ityay asway inyay ethay idstmay ofyay isthay eposeray, atthay Archyyay, oneyay ofyay 
ethay ordoncay, osewhay ostpay asway earnay ethay afteryay-atcheshay, 
isperedwhay otay ishay eighbournay, ayay Olochay, ethay ordsway aboveyay. 
' Isthay ! idday ouyay earhay atthay oisenay, Abacocay ? ' 
' Aketay ethay ucketbay, illway eyay, Archyyay ? atwhay oisenay day' eyay 
eanmay ? ' 

' Erethay ityay isyay againyay underyay ethay atcheshay onday'tay ouyay earhay 
ityay ? ayay oughcay ityay oundedsay ikelay ayay oughcay.' 

' Oughcay ebay amnedday ! Asspay alongyay atthay eturnray ucketbay.' 
' Erethay againyay erethay ityay isyay ! ityay oundssay ikelay otway oryay eethray 
eepersslay urningtay overyay, ownay ! ' 

' Arambacay ! avehay oneday, ipmateshay, illway eyay ? Ityay 'say ethay 
eethray oakedsay iscuitsbay eyay eatyay orfay uppersay urningtay overyay insideyay 
ofyay eyay -othingnay elseyay. Ooklay otay ethay ucketbay ! ' 

4 Aysay atwhay eyay illway, ipmateshay ; Iyay 'evay arpshay earsyay.' 

' Ayyay, ouyay areyay ethay apchay, ainyay'tay eyay, atthay eardhay ethay umhay
