Apterchay Ivxlay 

Ethay Artchay 

Adhay ouyay ollowedfay Aptaincay Ahabyay ownday intoyay ishay abincay 
afteryay ethay uallsqay atthay ooktay aceplay onyay ethay ightnay ucceedingsay 
atthay ildway atificationray ofyay ishay urposepay ithway ishay ewcray, ouyay 
ouldway avehay eensay imhay ogay otay ayay ockerlay inyay ethay ansomtray, andyay 
ingingbray outyay ayay argelay inkledwray ollray ofyay ellowishyay easay-artschay, 
eadspray emthay eforebay imhay onyay ishay ewedscray-ownday abletay. Enthay 
eatingsay imselfhay eforebay ityay, ouyay ouldway avehay eensay imhay intentlyyay 
udystay ethay ariousvay ineslay andyay adingsshay ichwhay erethay etmay ishay 
eyeyay ; andyay ithway owslay utbay eadystay encilpay acetray additionalyay 
oursescay overyay acesspay atthay eforebay ereway ankblay. Atyay intervalsyay, 
ehay ouldway eferray otay ilespay ofyay oldyay oglay-ooksbay esidebay imhay, ereinwhay 
ereway etsay ownday ethay easonssay andyay acesplay inyay ichwhay, onyay ariousvay 
ormerfay oyagesvay ofyay ariousvay ipsshay, ermspay aleswhay adhay eenbay 
apturedcay oryay eensay. 

Ilewhay usthay employedyay, ethay eavyhay ewterpay amplay uspendedsay 
oifay ainschay overyay ishay eadhay, ontinuallycay ockedray ithway ethay otionmay 
ofyay ethay ipshay, andyay oreverfay ewthray iftingshay eamsglay andyay adowsshay 
ofyay ineslay uponyay ishay inkledwray owbray, illtay ityay almostyay eemedsay atthay 
ilewhay ehay imselfhay asway arkingmay outyay ineslay andyay oursescay onyay ethay 
inkledwray artschay, omesay invisibleyay encilpay asway alsoyay acingtray 
ineslay andyay oursescay uponyay ethay eeplyday arkedmay artchay ofyay ishay 
oreheadfay. 

Utbay ityay asway otnay isthay ightnay inyay articularpay atthay, inyay ethay 
olitudesay ofyay ishay abincay, Ahabyay usthay onderedpay overyay ishay artschay. 
Almostyay everyyay ightnay eythay ereway oughtbray outyay ; almostyay everyyay 
ightnay omesay encilpay arksmay ereway effacedyay, andyay othersyay ereway 
ubstitutedsay. Orfay ithway ethay artschay ofyay allyay ourfay oceansyay eforebay

imhay, Ahabyay asway eadingthray ayay azemay ofyay urrentscay andyay eddiesyay, 
ithway ayay iewvay otay ethay oremay ertaincay accomplishmentyay ofyay atthay 
onomaniacmay oughtthay ofyay ishay oulsay. 

Ownay, otay anyoneyay otnay ullyfay acquaintedyay ithway ethay aysway ofyay 
ethay eviathanslay, ityay ightmay eemsay anyay absurdlyyay opelesshay asktay 
usthay otay eeksay outyay oneyay olitarysay eaturecray inyay ethay unhoopedyay 
oceansyay ofyay isthay anetplay. Utbay otnay osay idday ityay eemsay otay Ahabyay, 
owhay ewknay ethay etssay ofyay allyay idestay andyay urrentscay ; andyay erebythay 
alculatingcay ethay ifdray ingstay ofyay ethay ermspay alewhay'say oodfay ; andyay, 
alsoyay, allingcay otay indmay ethay egularray, ascertainedyay easonssay orfay 
untinghay imhay inyay articularpay atitudeslay ; ouldcay arriveyay atyay 
easonableray urmisessay, almostyay approachingyay otay ertaintiescay, 
oncerningcay ethay imeliesttay ayday otay ebay uponyay isthay oryay atthay 
oundgray inyay earchsay ofyay ishay eypray. 

Osay assuredyay, indeedyay, isyay ethay actfay oncerningcay ethay eriodicalpay- 
essnay ofyay ethay ermspay alewhay'say esortingray otay ivengay atersway, atthay 
anymay untershay elievebay atthay, ouldcay ehay ebay oselyclay observedyay 
andyay udiedstay oughoutthray ethay orldway ; ereway ethay ogslay orfay oneyay 
oyagevay ofyay ethay entireyay alewhay -eetflay arefullycay ollatedcay, enthay 
ethay igrationsmay ofyay ethay ermspay alewhay ouldway ebay oundfay otay 
orrespondcay inyay invariabilityyay otay osethay ofyay ethay erringhay -oalsshay 
oryay ethay ightsflay ofyay allowssway. Onyay isthay inthay, attemptsyay avehay 
eenbay ademay otay onstructcay elaborateyay igratorymay artschay ofyay ethay 
ermspay alewhay. 1 

Esidesbay, enwhay akingmay ayay assagepay omfray oneyay eedingfay- 
oundgray otay anotheryay, ethay ermspay aleswhay, uidedgay byay omesay 
infallibleyay instinctyay aysay, atherray, ecretsay intelligenceyay omfray 

1 Incesay ethay aboveyay asway ittenwray, ethay atementstay isyay appilyhay ornebay outyay byay anyay 
officialyay ircularcay, issuedyay byay Ieutenantlay Aurymay, ofyay ethay Ationalnay Observatoryyay, 
Ashingtonway, Aprilyay 16thay, 1851. Byay atthay ircularcay, ityay appearsyay atthay eciselypray 
uchsay ayay artchay isyay inyay oursecay ofyay ompletioncay ; andyay ortionspay ofyay ityay areyay esentedpray 
inyay ethay ircularcay. ' Isthay artchay ividesday ethay oceanyay intoyay istrictsday ofyay ivefay egreesday 
ofyay atitudelay byay ivefay egreesday ofyay ongitudelay ; erpendicularlypay oughthray eachyay 
ofyay ichwhay istrictsday areyay elvetway olumnscay orfay ethay elvetway onthsmay ; andyay orihay- 
ontallyzay oughthray eachyay ofyay ichwhay istrictsday areyay eethray ineslay ; oneyay otay owshay ethay 
umbernay ofyay aysday atthay avehay eenbay entspay inyay eachyay onthmay inyay everyyay istrictday, andyay 
ethay otway othersyay otay owshay ethay umbernay ofyay aysday inyay ichwhay aleswhay, ermspay oryay 
ightray, avehay eenbay eensay.'

ethay Eityday ostlymay imsway inyay einsvay, asyay eythay areyay alledcay ; oncay- 
inuingtay eirthay ayway alongyay ayay ivengay oceanyay-inelay ithway uchsay 
undeviatingyay exactitudeyay, atthay onay ipshay everyay ailedsay erhay 
oursecay, byay anyyay artchay, ithway oneyay ithetay ofyay uchsay arvellousmay 
ecisionpray. Oughthay, inyay esethay asescay, ethay irectionday akentay 
byay anyyay oneyay alewhay ebay aightstray asyay ayay urveyorsay'say arallelpay, andyay 
oughthay ethay inelay ofyay advanceyay ebay ictlystray onfinedcay otay itsyay 
ownyay unavoidableyay, aightstray akeway, etyay ethay arbitraryyay einvay 
inyay ichwhay atyay esethay imestay ehay isyay aidsay otay imsway, enerallygay 
embracesyay omesay ewfay ilesmay inyay idthway (oremay oryay esslay, asyay ethay 
einvay isyay esumedpray otay expandyay oryay ontractcay) ; utbay evernay 
exceedsyay ethay isualvay eepsway omfray ethay alewhay-ipshay'say astmay- 
eadshay, enwhay ircumspectlycay idingglay alongyay isthay agicmay onezay. 
Ethay umsay isyay, atthay atyay articularpay easonssay ithinway atthay eadthbray 
andyay alongyay atthay athpay, igratingmay aleswhay aymay ithway eatgray 
onfidencecay ebay ookedlay orfay. 

Andyay encehay otnay onlyyay atyay ubstantiatedsay imestay, uponyay ellway- 
ownknay eparatesay eedingfay-oundsgray, ouldcay Ahabyay opehay otay 
encounteryay ishay eypray ; utbay inyay ossingcray ethay idestway expansesyay 
ofyay aterway etweenbay osethay oundsgray ehay ouldcay, byay ishay artyay, osay 
aceplay andyay imetay imselfhay onyay ishay ayway, asyay evenyay enthay otnay otay ebay 
ollywhay ithoutway ospectpray ofyay ayay eetingmay. 

Erethay asway ayay ircumstancecay ichwhay atyay irstfay ightsay eemedsay otay 
entangleyay ishay eliriousday utbay illstay ethodicalmay emeschay. Utbay 
otnay osay inyay ealityray, erhapspay. Oughthay ethay egariousgray ermspay 
aleswhay avehay eirthay egularray easonssay orfay articularpay oundsgray, 
etyay inyay eneralgay ouyay annotcay oncludecay atthay ethay erdshay ichwhay 
auntedhay uchsay andyay uchsay ayay atitudelay oryay ongitudelay isthay earyay, 
aysay, illway urntay outyay otay ebay identicallyyay ethay amesay ithway osethay 
atthay ereway oundfay erethay ethay ecedingpray easonsay ; oughthay 
erethay areyay eculiarpay andyay unquestionableyay instancesyay erewhay 
ethay ontrarycay ofyay isthay ashay ovedpray uetray. Inyay eneralgay, ethay amesay 
emarkray, onlyyay ithinway ayay esslay ideway imitlay, appliesyay otay ethay olisay- 
ariestay andyay ermitshay amongyay ethay aturedmay, agedyay ermspay aleswhay. 
Osay atthay oughthay Obymay-Ickday adhay inyay ayay ormerfay earyay eenbay eensay,

Ethay Affidavityay 

Osay arfay asyay atwhay erethay aymay ebay ofyay ayay arrativenay inyay isthay ookbay ; 
andyay, indeedyay, asyay indirectlyyay ouchingtay oneyay oryay otway eryvay interyay-

entirelyyay uninjuredyay.' 

Ownay, ethay Aptaincay Day'Olfway erehay alludedyay otay asyay ommandcay- 
ingyay ethay ipshay inyay uestionqay, isyay ayay Ewnay Englanderyay, owhay, afteryay

avehay ethay onourhay ofyay eingbay ayay ephewnay ofyay ishay. Iyay avehay arpay- 
icularlytay uestionedqay imhay oncerningcay isthay assagepay inyay Angslay- 
orflday Ehay ubstantiatessay everyyay ordway. Ethay ipshay, oweverhay, 
asway byay onay eansmay ayay argelay oneyay : ayay Ussianray aftcray uiltbay onyay 
ethay Iberiansay oastcay, andyay urchasedpay byay myay uncleyay afteryay 
arteringbay awayyay ethay esselvay inyay ichwhay ehay ailedsay omfray omehay. 

Inyay atthay upyay andyay ownday anlymay ookbay ofyay oldyay-ashionedfay 
adventureyay, osay ullfay, ootay, ofyay onesthay ondersway ethay oyagevay

orfay ayay orroborativecay exampleyay, ifyay uchsay ebay eedednay.

andingstay idewayssay, everyay andyay anonyay idslay ishay eavyhay oakenyay

ethay aterway, arelesslycay andyay unthinkinglyyay ovedray omehay everyyay

allyay overyay ethay ipshay andyay allyay overyay ethay easay, onlyyay okenbray byay ethay 
intermittingyay ullday oundsay ofyay ethay ordsway, atthay ityay eemedsay asyay 
ifyay isthay ereway ethay Oomlay ofyay Imetay, andyay Iyay elfmysay ereway ayay uttleshay 
echanicallymay eavingway andyay eavingway awayyay atyay ethay Atesfay.

oweverhay arfay apartyay atitudeslay andyay ongitudeslay, atthay unnearyay- 
ableyay outspay asway astcay byay oneyay elfsay-amesay alewhay ; andyay atthay 
alewhay, Obymay-Ickday. Orfay ayay imetay, erethay eignedray, ootay, ayay 
ensesay ofyay eculiarpay eaddray atyay isthay ittingflay apparitionyay, asyay ifyay ityay 
ereway eacherouslytray eckoningbay usyay onyay andyay onyay, inyay orderyay atthay 
ethay onstermay ightmay urntay oundray uponyay usyay, andyay endray usyay atyay 
astlay inyay ethay emotestray andyay ostmay avagesay eassay. 

Esethay emporarytay apprehensionsyay, osay aguevay utbay osay awfulyay, 
erivedday ayay ondrousway otencypay omfray ethay ontrastingcay erenitysay 
ofyay ethay eatherway, inyay ichwhay, eneathbay allyay itsyay ueblay andnessblay, 
omesay oughtthay erethay urkedlay ayay evilishday armchay, asyay orfay aysday 
andyay aysday eway oyagedvay alongyay, oughthray eassay osay earilyway, 
onesomelylay ildmay, atthay allyay acespay, inyay epugnanceray otay ouryay 
engefulvay errandyay, eemedsay acatingvay itselfyay ofyay ifelay eforebay ouryay 
urnyay-ikelay owpray. 

Utbay, atyay astlay, enwhay urningtay otay ethay eastwardyay, ethay Apecay 
indsway eganbay owlinghay aroundyay usyay, andyay eway oseray andyay ellfay uponyay 
ethay onglay, oubledtray eassay atthay areyay erethay ; enwhay ethay ivoryyay- 
uskedtay Equodpay arplyshay owedbay otay ethay astblay, andyay oredgay ethay 
arkday avesway inyay erhay adnessmay, illtay, ikelay owersshay ofyay ilversay 
ipschay, ethay oamfay-akesflay ewflay overyay erhay ulwarksbay ; enthay allyay 
isthay esolateday acuityvay ofyay ifelay entway awayyay, utbay avegay aceplay 
otay ightssay oremay ismalday anthay eforebay. 

Oseclay otay ouryay owsbay, angestray ormsfay inyay ethay aterway artedday 
itherhay andyay itherthay eforebay usyay ; ilewhay ickthay inyay ouryay earray ewflay 
ethay inscrutableyay easay-avensray. Andyay everyyay orningmay, erchedpay

onyay ouryay aysstay, owsray ofyay esethay irdsbay ereway eensay ; andyay itespay 
ofyay ouryay ootingshay, orfay ayay onglay imetay obstinatelyyay ungclay otay ethay 
emphay, asyay oughthay eythay eemedday ouryay ipshay omesay iftingdray, 
uninhabitedyay aftcray ; ayay ingthay appointedyay otay esolationday, andyay 
ereforethay itfay oostingray-aceplay orfay eirthay omelesshay elvessay. Andyay

Apecay ofyay Oodgay Opehay, oday eythay allcay eyay ? Atherray Apecay 
Ormentototay, asyay alledcay ofyay oreyay ; orfay onglay alluredyay byay ethay 
erfidiouspay ilencessay atthay eforebay adhay attendedyay usyay, eway oundfay 
ourselvesyay aunchedlay intoyay isthay ormentedtay easay, erewhay uiltygay 
eingsbay ansformedtray intoyay osethay owlsfay andyay esethay ishfay, 
eemedsay ondemnedcay otay imsway onyay everlastinglyyay ithoutway anyyay 
avenhay inyay orestay, oryay eatbay atthay ackblay airyay ithoutway anyyay orizonhay. 
Utbay almcay, owsnay-itewhay, andyay unvaryingyay ; illstay irectingday 
itsyay ountainfay ofyay eathersfay otay ethay skyay ; illstay eckoningbay usyay onyay 
omfray eforebay, ethay olitarysay etjay ouldway atyay imestay ebay escriedday. 

Uringday allyay isthay acknessblay ofyay ethay elementsyay, Ahabyay, oughthay 
assumingyay orfay ethay imetay ethay almostyay ontinualcay ommandcay 
ofyay ethay encheddray andyay angerousday eckday, anifestedmay ethay 
oomiestglay eserveray ; andyay oremay eldomsay anthay everyay addressedyay 
ishay atesmay. Inyay empestuoustay imestay ikelay esethay, afteryay everyyay- 
ingthay aboveyay andyay aloftyay ashay eenbay ecuredsay, othingnay oremay 
ancay ebay oneday utbay assivelypay otay awaityay ethay issueyay ofyay ethay alegay. 
Enthay aptaincay andyay ewcray ecomebay acticalpray atalistsfay. Osay, 
ithway ishay ivoryyay eglay insertedyay intoyay itsyay accustomedyay olehay, andyay 
ithway oneyay andhay irmlyfay aspinggray ayay oudshray, Ahabyay orfay ourshay 
andyay ourshay ouldway andstay azinggay eadday otay indwardway, ilewhay anyay 
occasionalyay uallsqay ofyay eetslay oryay owsnay ouldway allyay utbay ongealcay

atthay urstinglybay okebray overyay itsyay owsbay, oodstay inyay ayay inelay alongyay 
ethay ulwarksbay inyay ethay aistway ; andyay ethay etterbay otay uardgay againstyay

Apterchay Iilay 

Ethay Albatrossyay 

Outhsay-Eastwardyay omfray ethay Apecay, offyay ethay istantday Ozettscray, 
ayay oodgay uisingcray -oundgray orfay ightray alemenwhay, ayay ailsay oomedlay 
aheadyay, ethay Oneygay (Albatrossyay) byay amenay. Asyay eshay owlyslay 
ewdray ighnay, omfray myay oftylay erchpay atyay ethay oremastfay -eadhay, Iyay 
adhay ayay oodgay iewvay ofyay atthay ightsay osay emarkableray otay ayay otyray inyay 
ethay arfay oceanyay isheriesfay ayay alerwhay atyay easay, andyay onglay absentyay 
omfray omehay. 

Asyay ifyay ethay avesway adhay eenbay ullersfay, isthay aftcray asway eachedblay 
ikelay ethay eletonskay ofyay ayay andedstray alrusway. Allyay ownday erhay 
idessay, isthay ectralspay appearanceyay asway acedtray ithway onglay 
annelschay ofyay eddenedray ustray, ilewhay allyay erhay arsspay andyay erhay 
iggingray ereway ikelay ethay ickthay anchesbray ofyay eestray urredfay overyay 
ithway oarhay-ostfray. Onlyyay erhay owerlay ailssay ereway etsay. Ayay ildway 
ightsay ityay asway otay eesay erhay onglay-eardedbay ooklay-outsyay atyay osethay 
eethray astmay-eadshay. Eythay eemedsay adclay inyay ethay insskay ofyay eastsbay, 
osay orntay andyay epatchedbay ethay aimentray atthay adhay urvivedsay 
earlynay ourfay earsyay ofyay uisingcray. Andingstay inyay ironyay oopshay 
ailednay otay ethay astmay, eythay ayedsway andyay ungsway overyay ayay athomfay- 
esslay easay ; andyay oughthay, enwhay ethay ipshay owlyslay idedglay oseclay 
underyay ouryay ernstay, eway ixsay enmay inyay ethay airyay amecay osay ighnay otay eachyay 
otheryay atthay eway ightmay almostyay avehay eapedlay omfray ethay astmay- 
eadshay ofyay oneyay ipshay otay osethay ofyay ethay otheryay ; etyay, osethay orfay- 
ornlay-ookinglay ishermenfay, ildlymay eyeingyay usyay asyay eythay assedpay, 
aidsay otnay oneyay ordway otay ouryay ownyay ooklay-outsyay, ilewhay ethay uarterqay- 
eckday ailhay asway eingbay eardhay omfray elowbay. 

' Ipshay ahoyyay ! Avehay eyay eensay ethay Itewhay Alewhay ? ' 
Utbay asyay ethay angestray aptaincay, eaninglay overyay ethay allidpay

Apterchay Iiilay 

Ethay Amgay 

Ethay ostensibleyay easonray whyay Ahabyay idday otnay ogay onyay oardbay ofyay ethay 
alerwhay eway adhay okenspay asway isthay : ethay indway andyay easay ebay- 
okenedtay ormsstay. Utbay evenyay adhay isthay otnay eenbay ethay asecay, 
ehay ouldway otnay afteryay allyay, erhapspay, avehay oardedbay erhay udgingjay 
byay ishay ubsequentsay onductcay onyay imilarsay occasionsyay ifyay osay ityay 
adhay eenbay atthay, byay ethay ocesspray ofyay ailinghay, ehay adhay obtainedyay 
ayay egativenay answeryay otay ethay uestionqay ehay utpay. Orfay, asyay ityay 
eventuallyyay urnedtay outyay, ehay aredcay otnay otay onsortcay, evenyay orfay 
ivefay inutesmay, ithway anyyay angerstray aptaincay, exceptyay ehay ouldcay 
ontributecay omesay ofyay atthay informationyay ehay osay absorbinglyyay 
oughtsay. Utbay allyay isthay ightmay emainray inadequatelyyay estiyay- 
atedmay, ereway otnay omethingsay aidsay erehay ofyay ethay eculiarpay usagesyay 
ofyay alingwhay-esselsvay enwlfay eetingmay eachyay otheryay inyay oreignfay 
eassay, andyay especiallyyay onyay ayay ommoncay uisingcray-oundgray. 

Ifyay otway angersstray ossingcray ethay Inepay Arrensbay inyay Ewnay Orkyay 
Atestay, oryay ethay equallyyay esolateday Alisburysay Ainplay inyay Englandyay ; 
ifyay asuallycay encounteringyay eachyay otheryay inyay uchsay inhospitableyay 
ildsway, esethay aintway, orfay ethay ifelay ofyay emthay, annotcay ellway avoidyay 
ayay utualmay alutationsay ; andyay oppingstay orfay ayay omentmay otay 
interchangeyay ethay ewsnay ; andyay, erhapspay, ittingsay ownday orfay ayay 
ilewhay andyay estingray inyay oncertcay : enthay, owhay uchmay oremay aturalnay 
atthay uponyay ethay illimitableyay Inepay Arrensbay andyay Alisburysay Ainsplay 
ofyay ethay easay, otway alingwhay-esselsvay escryingday eachyay otheryay atyay ethay 
endsyay ofyay ethay earthyay offyay onelay Anningfay 'say Islandyay, oryay ethay arfay 
awayyay Ingkay'say Illsmay ; owhay uchmay oremay aturalnay, Iyay aysay, 
atthay underyay uchsay ircumstancescay esethay ipsshay ouldshay otnay onlyyay 
interchangeyay ailshay, utbay omecay intoyay illstay oserclay, oremay iendlyfray 
andyay ociablesay ontactcay. Andyay especiallyyay ouldway isthay eemsay otay

ebay ayay attermay ofyay oursecay, inyay ethay asecay ofyay esselsvay ownedyay inyay oneyay

Orfay ethay onglay absentyay ipshay, ethay outwardyay-ounderbay, erpay- 
apshay, ashay etterslay onyay oardbay ; atyay anyyay ateray, eshay illway ebay uresay

Andyay inyay eturnray orfay atthay ourtesycay, ethay outwardyay-oundbay ipshay 
ouldway eceiveray ethay atestlay alingwhay intelligenceyay omfray ethay 
uisingcray-oundgray otay ichwhay eshay aymay ebay estinedday, ayay ingthay ofyay

otheryay'say acktray onyay ethay uisingcray-oundgray itselfyay, evenyay oughthay

andyay ownay arfay emoteray esselvay ; andyay omesay ofyay osethay etterslay 
aymay ebay orfay ethay eoplepay ofyay ethay ipshay eshay ownay eetsmay. Esidesbay, 
eythay ouldway exchangeyay ethay alingwhay ewsnay, andyay avehay anyay 
agreeableyay atchay. Orfay otnay onlyyay ouldway eythay eetmay ithway allyay 
ethay athiessympay ofyay ailorssay, utbay ikewiselay ithway allyay ethay eculiarpay 
ongenialitiescay arisingyay omfray ayay ommoncay ursuitpay andyay utuallymay 
aredshay ivationspray andyay erilspay. 

Ornay ouldway ifferenceday ofyay ountrycay akemay anyyay eryvay essentialyay 
ifferenceday ; atthay isyay, osay onglay asyay othbay artiespay eakspay oneyay anlay- 
uagegay, asyay isyay ethay asecay ithway Americansyay andyay Englishyay. 
Oughthay, otay ebay uresay, omfray ethay allsmay umbernay ofyay Englishyay 
alerswhay, uchsay eetingsmay oday otnay eryvay oftenyay occuryay, andyay enwhay 
eythay oday occuryay erethay isyay ootay aptyay otay ebay ayay ortsay ofyay essshynay 
etweenbay emthay ; orfay ouryay Englishmanyay isyay atherray eservedray, 
andyay ouryay Ankeeyay, ehay oesday otnay ancyfay atthay ortsay ofyay ingthay 
inyay anybodyyay utbay imselfhay. Esidesbay, ethay Englishyay alerswhay 
ometimessay affectyay ayay indkay ofyay etropolitanmay uperioritysay overyay 
ethay Americanyay alerswhay ; egardingray ethay onglay, eanlay Annay- 
ucketertay, ithway ishay ondescriptnay ovincialismspray, asyay ayay ortsay 
ofyay easay-easantpay. Utbay erewhay isthay uperioritysay inyay ethay Englishyay 



Ethay Amgay 303 

alemenwhay oesday eallyray onsistcay, ityay ouldway ebay ardhay otay aysay,

Osay, enthay, eway eesay atthay ofyay allyay ipsshay eparatelysay ailingsay ethay

ofyay andiesday inyay Oadwaybray ; andyay allyay ethay imetay indulgingyay, 
erhapspay, inyay inicalfay iticismcray uponyay eachyay otheryay'say igray. Asyay 
orfay enmay-ofyay-arway, enwhay eythay ancechay otay eetmay atyay easay, eythay 
irstfay ogay oughthray uchsay ayay ingstray ofyay illysay owingsbay andyay apingsscray,

uchmay ightray-ownday eartyhay oodwillgay andyay otherlybray ovelay 
aboutyay ityay atyay allyay. Asyay ouchingtay aveslay-ipsshay eetingmay, whyay, eythay 
areyay inyay uchsay ayay odigiouspray urryhay, eythay unray awayyay omfray eachyay 
otheryay asyay oonsay asyay ossiblepay. Andyay asyay orfay iratespay, enwhay eythay 
ancechay otay osscray eachyay otheryay'say osscray-onesbay, ethay irstfay ailhay isyay, 
' Owhay anymay ullsskay ? ' ethay amesay ayway atthay alerswhay ailhay 
' Owhay anymay arrelsbay ? ' Andyay atthay uestionqay onceyay answeredyay, 
iratespay aightwaystray eerstay apartyay, orfay eythay areyay infernalyay 
illainsvay onyay othbay idessay, andyay onday'tay ikelay otay eesay overmuchyay ofyay 
eachyay otheryay'say illainousvay ikenesseslay. 

Utbay ooklay atyay ethay odlygay, onesthay, unostentatiousyay, oshay- 
itablepay, ociablesay, eefray-andyay-easyyay alerwhay ! Atwhay oesday ethay 
alerwhay oday enwhay eshay eetsmay anotheryay alerwhay inyay anyyay ortsay ofyay 
ecentday eatherway ? Eshay ashay ayay ' Amgay,' ayay ingthay osay utterlyyay 
unknownyay otay allyay otheryay ipsshay atthay eythay evernay eardhay ofyay ethay 
amenay evenyay ; andyay ifyay byay ancechay eythay ouldshay earhay ofyay ityay, eythay 
onlyyay ingray atyay ityay, andyay epeatray amesomegay uffstay aboutyay 'outersspay' 
andyay cay ubberblay-oilersbay,' andyay uchsay ikelay ettypray exclamationsyay. 



304 Obymay-Ickday 

Whyay ityay isyay atthay allyay erchantmay eamensay, andyay alsoyay allyay iratespay 
andyay anmay-ofyay-arway'say enmay, andyay aveslay-ipshay ailorssay, erishchay 
uchsay ayay ornfulscay eelingfay owardtay alewhay-ipsshay ; isthay isyay ayay 
uestionqay ityay ouldway ebay ardhay otay answeryay. Ecausebay, inyay ethay 
asecay ofyay iratespay, aysay, Iyay ouldshay ikelay otay owknay etherwhay atthay 
ofessionpray ofyay eirsthay ashay anyyay eculiarpay oryglay aboutyay ityay. Ityay 
ometimessay endsyay inyay uncommonyay elevationyay, indeedyay ; utbay onlyyay 
atyay ethay allowsgay. Andyay esidesbay, enwhay ayay anmay isyay elevatedyay inyay 
atthay oddyay ashionfay, ehay ashay onay operpray oundationfay orfay ishay 
uperiorsay altitudeyay. Encehay, Iyay oncludecay, atthay inyay oastingbay 
imselfhay otay ebay ighhay iftedlay aboveyay ayay alemanwhay, inyay atthay 
assertionyay ethay iratepay ashay onay olidsay asisbay otay andstay onyay. 

Utbay atwhay isyay ayay Amgay ? Ouyay ightmay earway outyay ouryay indexyay 
ingerfay unningray upyay andyay ownday ethay olumnscay ofyay ictionariesday, 
andyay evernay indfay ethay ordway. Dray. Ohnsonjay evernay attainedyay 
otay atthay eruditionyay ; Oahnay Ebsterway'say arkyay oesday otnay oldhay ityay. 
Everthelessnay, isthay amesay expressiveyay ordway ashay ownay orfay 
anymay earsyay eenbay inyay onstantcay useyay amongyay omesay ifteenfay 
ousandthay uetray-ornbay Ankeesyay. Ertainlycay, ityay eedsnay ayay 
efinitionday, andyay ouldshay ebay incorporatedyay intoyay ethay Exiconlay. 
Ithway atthay iewvay, etlay emay earnedlylay efineday ityay. 

Amgay. Ounnay Ayay ocialsay eetingmay ofyay otway (oryay oremay) 
alewhay-ipsshay, enerallygay onyay ayay uisingcray-oundgray ; enwhay, afteryay 
exchangingyay ailshay, eythay exchangeyay isitsvay byay oatsbay' ewscray : ethay 
otway aptainscay emainingray, orfay ethay imetay, onyay oardbay ofyay oneyay ipshay tay 
andyay ethay otway iefchay atesmay onyay ethay otheryay. 

Erethay isyay anotheryay ittlelay itemyay aboutyay Amminggay ichwhay ustmay 
otnay ebay orgottenfay erehay. Allyay ofessionspray avehay eirthay ownyay 
ittlelay eculiaritiespay ofyay etailday ; osay ashay ethay alewhay-isheryfay. Inyay 
ayay iratepay, anmay-ofyay-arway, oryay aveslay-ipshay, enwhay ethay aptaincay 
isyay owedray anywhereyay ihay ishay oatbay, ehay alwaysyay itssay inyay ethay ernstay- 
eetsshay onyay ayay omfortablecay, ometimessay ushionedcay eatsay erethay, 
andyay oftenyay eersstay imselfhay ithway ayay ettypray ittlelay illinermay'say 
illertay ecoratedday ithway aygay ordscay andyay ibbonsray. Utbay ethay 
alewhay-oatbay ashay onay eatsay asternyay, onay ofasay ofyay atthay ortsay atwhay- 



Ethay Amgay 305 

everyay, andyay onay illertay atyay allyay. Ighhay imestay indeedyay, ifyay alingwhay- 
aptainscay ereway eeledwhay aboutyay ethay aterway onyay astorscay ikelay 
outygay oldyay aldermenyay inyay atentpay airschay. Andyay asyay orfay ayay illertay, 
ethay alewhay-oatbay evernay admitsyay ofyay anyyay uchsay effeminacyyay ; andyay 
ereforethay asyay inyay amminggay ayay ompletecay oatbay'say ewcray ustmay 
eavelay ethay ipshay, andyay encehay asyay ethay oatbay eererstay oryay arpooneerhay 
isyay ofyay ethay umbernay, atthay ubordinatesay isyay ethay eersmanstay uponyay 
ethay occasionyay, andyay ethay aptaincay, avinghay onay aceplay otay itsay inyay, 
isyay ulledpay offyay otay ishay isitvay allyay andingstay ikelay ayay inepay-eetray. Andyay 
oftenyay ouyay illway oticenay atthay eingbay onsciouscay ofyay ethay eyesyay ofyay 
ethay olewhay isiblevay orldway estingray onyay imhay omfray ethay idessay ofyay 
ethay otway ipsshay, isthay andingstay aptaincay isyay allyay aliveyay otay ethay 
importanceyay ofyay ustainingsay ishay ignityday byay aintainingmay ishay 
egslay. Ornay isyay isthay anyyay eryvay easyyay attermay ; orfay inyay ishay earray 
isyay ethay immenseyay ojectingpray eeringstay-oaryay ittinghay imhay ownay 
andyay enthay inyay ethay allsmay ofyay ishay ackbay, ethay afteryay-oaryay eciprocatray- 
ingyay byay appingray ishay eesknay inyay ontfray. Ehay isyay usthay ompletelycay 
edgedway eforebay andyay ehindbay, andyay ancay onlyyay expandyay imselfhay 
idewayssay byay ettlingsay ownday onyay ishay etchedstray egslay ; utbay ayay 
uddensay, iolentvay itchpay ofyay ethay oatbay illway oftenyay ogay arfay otay oppletay 
imhay, ecausebay engthlay ofyay oundationfay isyay othingnay ithoutway 
orrespondingcay eadthbray. Erelymay akemay ayay eadspray angleyay ofyay 
otway olespay, andyay ouyay annotcay andstay emthay upyay. Enthay, againyay, 
ityay ouldway evernay oday inyay ainplay ightsay ofyay ethay orldway'say ivetedray 
eyesyay, ityay ouldway evernay oday, Iyay aysay, orfay isthay addlingstray aptaincay 
otay ebay eensay eadyingstay imselfhay ethay ightestslay articlepay byay 
atchingcay oldhay ofyay anythingyay ithway ishay andshay ; indeedyay, asyay 
okentay ofyay ishay entireyay, uoyantbay elfsay-ommandcay, ehay enerallygay 
arriescay ishay andshay inyay ishay owserstray' ocketspay ; utbay erhapspay 
eingbay enerallygay eryvay argelay, eavyhay andshay, ehay arriescay emthay 
erethay orfay allastbay. Everthelessnay erethay avehay occurredyay 
instancesyay, ellway authenticatedyay onesyay ootay, erewhay ethay aptaincay 
ashay eenbay ownknay orfay anyay uncommonlyyay iticalcray omentmay oryay 
otway, inyay ayay uddensay uallsqay, aysay otay eizesay oldhay ofyay ethay earestnay 
oarsmanyay'say airhay, andyay oldhay onyay erethay ikelay imgray eathday.

Ethay Owntay-Ohay'Say Orystay 

(Asyay oldtay atyay ethay Oldengay Innyay.) 

Ethay Apecay ofyay Oodgay Opehay, andyay allyay ethay ateryway egionray oundray 
aboutyay erethay, isyay uchmay ikelay omesay otednay ourfay ornerscay ofyay ayay 
eatgray ighwayhay, erewhay ouyay eetmay oremay avellerstray anthay inyay 
anyyay otheryay artpay. 

Ityay asway otnay eryvay onglay afteryay eakingspay ethay Oneygay atthay 
anotheryay omewardhay-oundbay alemanwhay, ethay Owntay-Ohay? asway 
encounteredyay. Eshay asway annedmay almostyay ollywhay byay Olypay- 
esiansnay. Inyay ethay ortshay amgay atthay ensuedyay eshay avegay usyay ongstray 
ewsnay ofyay Obymay-Ickday. Otay omesay ethay eneralgay interestyay inyay ethay 
Itewhay Alewhay asway ownay ildlyway eightenedhay byay ayay ircumstancecay 
ofyay ethay Owntay-Ohay' say orystay, ichwhay eemedsay obscurelyyay otay inyay- 
olvevay ithway ethay alewhay ayay ertaincay ondrousway, invertedyay isivay- 
ationtay ofyay oneyay ofyay osethay osay-alledcay udgmentsjay ofyay Odgay ichwhay 
atyay imestay areyay aidsay otay overtakeyay omesay enmay. Isthay atterlay 
ircumstancecay, ithway itsyay ownyay articularpay accompanimentsyay, 
ormingfay atwhay aymay ebay alledcay ethay ecretsay artpay ofyay ethay agedytray 
aboutyay otay ebay arratednay, evernay eachedray ethay earsyay ofyay Aptaincay 
Ahabyay oryay ishay atesmay. Orfay atthay ecretsay artpay ofyay ethay orystay asway 
unknownyay otay ethay aptaincay ofyay ethay Owntay-Ohay imselfhay. Ityay asway 
ethay ivatepray opertypray ofyay eethray onfederatecay itewhay eamensay 
ofyay atthay ipshay, oneyay ofyay omwhay, ityay eemssay, ommunicatedcay ityay otay 
Ashtegotay ithway Omishray injunctionsyay ofyay ecrecysay, utbay ethay

atyay ethay umpspay atyay ideway andyay easyyay intervalsyay ; utbay onay oodgay ucklay

andyay esperadoday omfray Uffalobay.

ingingsway atmay ofyay assgray.

' Ityay asway otnay oremay anthay ayay ayday oryay otway atyay ethay urthestfay

Owntay-Ohay'say eaklay eemedsay againyay increasingyay, utbay onlyyay osay asyay

ardway, entlemengay, isyay ityay altogetheryay unusualyay orfay ipsshay otay

isyay inyay omesay eryvay outyay-ofyay-ethay-ayway artpay ofyay osethay atersway, omesay 
eallyray andlesslay atitudelay, atthay erhay aptaincay eginsbay otay eelfay 
ayay ittlelay anxiousyay. 

' Uchmay isthay ayway adhay ityay eenbay ithway ethay Owntay-Ohay \ osay 
enwhay erhay eaklay asway oundfay aininggay onceyay oremay, erethay asway 
inyay uthtray omesay allsmay oncerncay anifestedmay byay everalsay ofyay erhay 
ompanycay ; especiallyyay byay Adneyray ethay atemay. Ehay omcay-

Adneyray, Iyay upposesay, asway asyay ittlelay ofyay ayay owardcay, andyay asyay ittlelay 
inclinedyay otay anyyay ortsay ofyay ervousnay apprehensivenessyay ouchingtay 
ishay ownyay ersonpay, asyay anyyay earlessfay, unthinkingyay eaturecray onyay 
andlay oryay onyay easay atthay ouyay ancay onvenientlycay imagineyay, entlegay-

enmay. Ereforethay enwhay ehay etrayedbay isthay olicitudesay aboutyay 
ethay afetysay ofyay ethay ipshay, omesay ofyay ethay eamensay eclaredday atthay 
ityay asway onlyyay onyay accountyay ofyay ishay eingbay ayay artpay owneryay inyay erhay. 
Osay enwhay eythay ereway orkingway atthay eveningyay atyay ethay umpspay, 
erethay asway onyay isthay eadhay onay allsmay amesomenessgay slylyay oinggay 
onyay amongyay emthay, asyay eythay oodstay ithway eirthay eetfay ontinuallycay 
overflowedyay byay ethay ipplingray earclay aterway earclay asyay anyyay 
ountainmay ingspray, entlemengay atthay ubblingbay omfray ethay 
umpspay anray acrossyay ethay eckday, andyay ouredpay itselfyay outyay inyay eadystay 
outsspay atyay ethay eelay upperscay-oleshay. 

4 Ownay, asyay ouyay ellway owknay, ityay isyay otnay eldomsay ethay asecay ihay 
isthay onventionalcay orldway ofyay oursyay ateryway oryay otherwiseyay ; 
atthay enwhay ayay ersonpay acedplay inyay ommandcay overyay ishay ellowfay- 
enmay indsfay oneyay ofyay emthay otay ebay eryvay ignificantlysay ishay uperiorsay 
inyay eneralgay idepray ofyay anhoodmay, aightwaystray againstyay atthay 
anmay ehay onceivescay anyay unconquerableyay islikeday andyay itternessbay ; 
andyay ifyay ehay avehay ayay ancechay ehay illway ullpay ownday andyay ulverisepay atthay 
ubalternsay'say owertay, andyay akemay ayay ittlelay eaphay ofyay ustday ofyay ityay. 
Ebay isthay onceitcay ofyay inemay asyay ityay aymay, entlemengay, atyay allyay eventsyay 
Eelkiltstay asway ayay alltay andyay oblenay animalyay ithway ayay eadhay ikelay ayay 
Omanray, andyay ayay owingflay oldengay eardbay ikelay ethay asselledtay 
ousingshay ofyay ouryay astlay iceroyvay'say ortingsnay argerchay ; andyay ayay 
ainbray, andyay ayay earthay, andyay ayay oulsay inyay imhay, entlemengay, ichwhay 
adhay ademay Eelkiltstay Arlemagnechay, adhay ehay eenbay ornbay onsay 
otay Arlemagnechay'say atherfay. Utbay Adneyray, ethay atemay, asway 
uglyyay asyay ayay ulemay ; etyay asyay ardyhay, asyay ubbornstay, asyay aliciousmay. 
Ehay idday otnay ovelay Eelkiltstay, andyay Eelkiltstay ewknay ityay. 

' Espyingyay ethay atemay awingdray earnay asyay ehay asway oilingtay atyay 
ethay umppay ithway ethay estray, ethay Akemanlay affectedyay otnay otay 
oticenay imhay, utbay unawedyay, entway onyay ithway ishay aygay anteringsbay.

onyay ethay artpay ofyay allyay andshay. Earingfay inyay ishay earthay estlay isthay 
ightmay ovepray utbay ootay uetray, ethay aptaincay ayay ittlelay esistedday, utbay 
illstay ommandedcay ethay insurgentsyay instantlyyay otay eturnray otay 
eirthay utyday. 

' " Illway ouyay omisepray otnay otay ouchtay usyay, ifyay eway oday ? " 
emandedday eirthay ingleaderray. 

' " Urntay otay ! urntay otay ! Iyay akemay onay omisepray ; otay ouryay 
utyday ! Oday ouyay antway otay inksay ethay ipshay, byay ockingknay offyay 
atyay ayay imetay ikelay isthay ? Urntay otay ! " andyay ehay onceyay oremay aisedray 
ayay istolpay. 

' " Inksay ethay ipshay ! " iedcray Eelkiltstay. " Ayyay, etlay erhay 
inksay. Otnay ayay anmay ofyay usyay urnstay otay, unlessyay ouyay earsway otnay otay 
aiseray ayay operay-arnyay againstyay usyay. Atwhay aysay eyay, enmay 1 " 
urningtay otay ishay omradescay. Ayay iercefay eerchay asway eirthay esponseray.

otay orkway, utbay eway onway'tay ebay oggedflay." 

' " Urntay otay ! " oaredray ethay aptaincay. 

* Eelkiltstay ancedglay oundray imhay ayay omentmay, andyay enthay

oreheadfay ushedcray inyay.

opalyay inyay ethay ueblay orningmay easay. Entlemengay, ayay angestray 
atalityfay ervadespay ethay olewhay areercay ofyay esethay eventsyay, asyay ifyay 
erilyvay appedmay outyay eforebay ethay orldway itselfyay asway artedchay. 
Ethay utineermay asway ethay owsmanbay ofyay ethay atemay, andyay enwhay 
astfay otay ayay ishfay, ityay asway ishay utyday otay itsay extnay imhay, ilewhay Adneyray 
oodstay upyay ithway ishay ancelay inyay ethay owpray, andyay aulhay inyay oryay ackenslay 
ethay inelay, atyay ethay ordway ofyay ommandcay. Oreovermay, enwhay ethay 
ourfay oatsbay ereway oweredlay, ethay atemay'say otgay ethay artstay ; andyay 
onenay owledhay oremay iercelyfay ithway elightday anthay idday Eelkiltstay, 
asyay ehay ainedstray atyay ishay oaryay. Afteryay ayay iffstay ullpay, eirthay arhay- 
ooneerpay otgay astfay, andyay, earspay inyay andhay, Adneyray angspray otay 
ethay owbay. Ehay asway alwaysyay ayay uriousfay anmay, ityay eemssay, inyay ayay 
oatbay. Andyay ownay ishay andagedbay cryay asway, otay eachbay imhay 
onyay ethay alewhay'say opmosttay ackbay. Othingnay oathlay, ishay owsbay- 
anmay auledhay imhay upyay andyay upyay, oughthray ayay indingblay oamfay atthay 
entblay otway itenesseswhay ogethertay ; illtay ofyay ayay uddensay ethay oatbay 
uckstray asyay againstyay ayay unkensay edgelay, andyay eelingkay overyay, illedspay 
outyay ethay andingstay atemay. Atthay instantyay, asyay ehay ellfay onyay ethay 
alewhay'say ipperyslay ackbay, ethay oatbay ightedray, andyay asway ashedday 
asideyay byay ethay ellsway, ilewhay Adneyray asway ossedtay overyay intoyay ethay 
easay, onyay ethay otheryay ankflay ofyay ethay alewhay . Ehay uckstray outyay oughthray 
ethay ayspray, andyay, orfay anyay instantyay, asway imlyday eensay oughthray 
atthay eilvay, ildlyway eekingsay otay emoveray imselfhay omfray ethay eyeyay 
ofyay Obymay-Ickday. Utbay ethay alewhay ushedray oundray inyay ayay uddensay 
aelstrommay ; eizedsay ethay immersway etweenbay ishay awsjay ; andyay 
earingray ighhay upyay ithway imhay, ungedplay eadlonghay againyay, andyay 
entway ownday.

Akemanlay adhay ackenedslay ethay inelay, osay asyay otay opdray asternyay omfray 
ethay irlpoolwhay ; almlycay ookinglay onyay, ehay oughtthay ishay ownyay 
oughtsthay. Utbay ayay uddensay, errifictay, ownwardday erkingjay 
ofyay ethay oatbay, uicklyqay oughtbray ishay ifeknay otay ethay inelay. Ehay 
utcay ityay ; andyay ethay alewhay asway eefray. Utbay, atyay omesay istanceday, 
Obymay-Ickday oseray againyay, ithway omesay atterstay ofyay Adneyray 'say

imhay. Allyay ourfay oatsbay avegay asechay againyay ; utbay ethay alewhay

' Inyay oodgay imetay, ethay Owntay-Ohay eachedray erhay ortpay ayay avagesay, 
olitarysay aceplay erewhay onay ivilisedcay eaturecray esidedray. 
Erethay, eadedhay byay ethay Akelay anmay, allyay utbay ivefay oryay ixsay ofyay ethay 
oremastfay-enmay eliberatelyday esertedday amongyay ethay almspay ; 
eventuallyyay, asyay ityay urnedtay outyay, eizingsay ayay argelay oubleday arway- 
anoecay ofyay ethay avagessay, andyay ettingsay ailsay orfay omesay otheryay 
arbourhay. 

4 Ethay ipshay'say ompanycay eingbay educedray otay utbay ayay andfulhay, 
ethay aptaincay alledcay uponyay ethay Islandersyay otay assistyay imhay inyay ethay 
aboriouslay usinessbay ofyay eavinghay ownday ethay ipshay otay opstay ethay 
eaklay. Utbay otay uchsay unrestingyay igilancevay overyay eirthay angerday- 
ousyay alliesyay asway isthay allsmay andbay ofyay iteswhay ecessitatednay, othbay 
byay ightnay andyay byay ayday, andyay osay extremeyay asway ethay ardhay orkway 
eythay underwentyay, atthay uponyay ethay esselvay eingbay eadyray againyay 
orfay easay, eythay ereway inyay uchsay ayay eakenedway onditioncay atthay ethay 
aptaincay urstday otnay utpay offyay ithway emthay inyay osay eavyhay ayay esselvay. 
Afteryay akingtay ounselcay ithway ishay officersyay, ehay anchoredyay ethay 
ipshay asyay arfay offyay oreshay asyay ossiblepay ; oadedlay andyay anray outyay ishay 
otway annoncay omfray ethay owsbay ; ackedstay ishay usketsmay onyay ethay 
ooppay ; andyay arningway ethay Islandersyay otnay otay approachyay ethay 
ipshay atyay eirthay erilpay, ooktay oneyay anmay ithway imhay, andyay ettingsay 
ethay ailsay ofyay ishay estbay alewhay-oatbay, eeredstay aightstray eforebay ethay 
indway orfay Ahititay, ivefay undredhay ilesmay istantday, otay ocurepray 
ayay einforcementray otay ishay ewcray. 

' Onyay ethay ourthfay ayday ofyay ethay ailsay, ayay argelay anoecay asway 
escriedday, ichwhay eemedsay otay avehay ouchedtay atyay ayay owlay isleyay ofyay 
oralscay. Ehay eeredstay awayyay omfray ityay ; utbay ethay avagesay aftcray 
orebay ownday onyay imhay ; andyay oonsay ethay oicevay ofyay Eelkiltstay ailedhay 
imhay otay eavehay otay, oryay ehay ouldway unray imhay underyay aterway. Ethay 
aptaincay esentedpray ayay istolpay. Ithway oneyay ootfay onyay eachyay owpray 
ofyay ethay okedyay arway-anoescay, ethay Akemanlay aughedlay imhay otay 
ornscay ; assuringyay imhay atthay ifyay ethay istolpay osay uchmay asyay ickedclay 
inyay ethay ocklay, ehay ouldway urybay imhay inyay ubblesbay andyay oamfay.

Apterchay Lvay 

Ofyay Ethay Onstrousmay Icturespay Ofyay Aleswhay 

Iyay Allshay ereyay onglay aintpay otay ouyay asyay ellway asyay oneyay ancay ithoutway 
anvascay, omethingsay ikelay ethay uetray ormfay ofyay ethay alewhay asyay ehay 
actuallyyay appearsyay otay ethay eyeyay ofyay ethay alemanwhay enwhay inyay ishay 
ownyay absoluteyay odybay ethay alewhay isyay ooredmay alongsideyay ethay 
alewhay -ipshay osay atthay ehay ancay ebay airlyfay eppedstay uponyay erethay. 
Ityay aymay ebay orthway ilewhay, ereforethay, eviouslypray otay advertyay 
otay osethay uriouscay imaginaryyay ortraitspay ofyay imhay ichwhay evenyay 
ownday otay ethay esentpray ayday onfidentlycay allengechay ethay aithfay 
ofyay ethay andsmanlay. Ityay isyay imetay otay etsay ethay orldway ightray inyay 
isthay attermay, byay ovingpray uchsay icturespay ofyay ethay alewhay allyay 
ongwray. 

Ityay aymay ebay atthay ethay imalpray ourcesay ofyay allyay osethay ictorialpay 
elusionsday illway ebay oundfay amongyay ethay oldestyay Induhay, Egyptianyay, 
andyay Eciangray ulpturesscay. Orfay everyay incesay osethay inventiveyay 
utbay unscrupulousyay imestay enwhay onyay ethay arblemay anellingspay 
ofyay emplestay, ethay edestalspay ofyay atuesstay, andyay onyay ieldsshay, 
edallionsmay, upscay, andyay oinscay, ethay olphinday asway awndray inyay 
alesscay ofyay ainchay-armouryay ikelay Aladinsay'say, andyay ayay elmetedhay 
eadhay ikelay Stay. Eorgegay'say ; everyay incesay enthay ashay omethingsay 
ofyay ethay amesay ortsay ofyay icencelay evailedpray, otnay onlyyay inyay ostmay 
opularpay icturespay ofyay ethay alewhay, utbay inyay anymay ientificscay 
esentationspray ofyay imhay. 

Ownay, byay allyay oddsyay, ethay ostmay ancientyay extantyay ortraitpay 
anywaysyay urportingpay otay ebay ethay alewhay'say, isyay otay ebay oundfay inyay 
ethay amousfay averncay -agodapay ofyay Elephantayay, inyay Indiayay. Ethay 
Ahminsbray aintainmay atthay inyay ethay almostyay endlessyay ulpturesscay 
ofyay atthay immemorialyay agodapay, allyay ethay adestray andyay ursuitspay,

everyyay onceivablecay avocationyay ofyay anmay, ereway efiguredpray agesyay 
eforebay anyyay ofyay emthay actuallyyay amecay intoyay eingbay. Onay onderway, 
enthay, atthay inyay omesay ortsay ouryay oblenay ofessionpray ofyay alingwhay 
ouldshay avehay eenbay erethay adowedshay orthfay. Ethay Induhay 
alewhay eferredray otay, occursyay inyay ayay eparatesay epartmentday ofyay ethay 
allway, epictingday ethay incarnationyay ofyay Ishnuvay inyay ethay ormfay ofyay 
eviathanlay, earnedlylay ownknay asyay ethay Atsemay Avataryay. Utbay 
oughthay isthay ulpturescay isyay alfhay anmay andyay alfhay alewhay, osay asyay 
onlyyay otay ivegay ethay ailtay ofyay ethay atterlay, etyay atthay allsmay ectionsay 
ofyay imhay isyay allyay ongwray. Ityay ookslay oremay ikelay ethay aperingtay ailtay 
ofyay anyay anacondayay ayay anthay ethay oadbray almspay ofyay ethay uetray alewhay'say 
ajesticmay ukesflay. 

Utbay ogay otay ethay oldyay alleriesgay, andyay ooklay ownay atyay ayay eatgray 
Istianchray ainterpay'say ortraitpay ofyay isthay ishfay ; orfay ehay ucceedssay 
onay etterbay anthay ethay antediluvianyay Induhay. Ityay isyay Uidegay'say 
icturepay ofyay Erseuspay escuingray Andromedayay omfray ethay easay- 
onstermay oryay alewhay. Erewhay idday Uidogay etgay ethay odelmay ofyay 
uchsay ayay angestray eaturecray asyay atthay ? Ornay oesday Ogarthhay, inyay 
aintingpay ethay amesay enescay inyay ishay ownyay ' Erseuspay Escendingday,' 
akemay outyay oneyay itwhay etterbay. Ethay ugehay orpulencecay ofyay atthay 
Ogarthianhay onstermay undulatesyay onyay ethay urfacesay, arcelyscay 
awingdray oneyay inchyay ofyay aterway. Ityay ashay ayay ortsay ofyay owdahhay onyay itsyay 
ackbay, andyay itsyay istendedday uskedtay outhmay intoyay ichwhay ethay 
illowsbay areyay ollingray, ightmay ebay akentay orfay ethay Aitorstray' Ategay 
eadinglay omfray ethay Amesthay byay aterway intoyay ethay Owertay. Enthay, 
erethay areyay ethay Odromuspray aleswhay ofyay oldyay Otchscay Ibbaldsay, 
andyay Onahjay'say alewhay, asyay epictedday inyay ethay intspray ofyay oldyay Iblesbay 
andyay ethay utscay ofyay oldyay imerspray. Atwhay allshay ebay aidsay ofyay esethay ? 
Asyay orfay ethay ookbinderbay'say alewhay indingway ikelay ayay inevay-alkstay 
oundray ethay ockstay ofyay ayay escendingday anchoryay asyay ampedstay andyay 
ildedgay onyay ethay acksbay andyay itletay-agespay ofyay anymay ooksbay othbay 
oldyay andyay ewnay atthay isyay ayay eryvay icturesquepay utbay urelypay 
abulousfay eaturecray, imitatedyay, Iyay aketay ityay, omfray ethay ikelay iguresfay 
onyay antiqueyay asesvay. Oughthay universallyyay enominatedday ayay 
olphinday, Iyay everthelessnay allcay isthay ookbinderbay'say ishfay anyay 



Onstrousmay Icturespay Ofyay Aleswhay 333 

attemptyay atyay ayay alewhay ; ecausebay ityay asway osay intendedyay enwhay ethay 
eviceday asway irstfay introducedyay. Ityay asway introducedyay byay anyay oldyay 
Italianyay ublisherpay omewheresay aboutyay ethay 15thay enturycay, 
uringday ethay Evivalray ofyay Earninglay ; andyay inyay osethay aysday, andyay 
evenyay ownday otay ayay omparativelycay atelay eriodpay, olphinsday ereway 
opularlypay upposedsay otay ebay ayay eciesspay ofyay ethay eviathanlay. 

Inyay ethay ignettesvay andyay otheryay embellishmentsyay ofyay omesay 
ancientyay ooksbay ouyay illway atyay imestay eetmay ithway eryvay uriouscay 
ouchestay atyay ethay alewhay, erewhay allyay annermay ofyay outsspay, etsjay 
day'eauyay, othay ingsspray andyay oldcay, Aratogasay andyay Adenbay-Adenbay, 
omecay ubblingbay upyay omfray ishay unexhaustedyay ainbray. Inyay ethay 
itletay-agepay ofyay ethay originalyay editionyay ofyay ethay Advancementyay ofyay 
Earninglay ouyay illway indfay omesay uriouscay aleswhay. 

Utbay uittingqay allyay esethay unprofessionalyay attemptsyay, etlay usyay 
anceglay atyay osethay icturespay ofyay eviathanlay urportingpay otay ebay 
obersay, ientificscay elineationsday, byay osethay owhay owknay. Inyay 
oldyay Arrishay'say ollectioncay ofyay oyagesvay erethay areyay omesay atesplay 
ofyay aleswhay extractedyay omfray ayay Utchday ookbay ofyay oyagesvay, Ayay.Day.

Onasjay inyay ethay Alewhay, Eterpay Etersonpay ofyay Ieslandfray, astermay. 
Inyay oneyay ofyay osethay atesplay ethay aleswhay, ikelay eatgray aftsray ofyay 
ogslay, areyay epresentedray inglyay amongyay iceyay-islesyay, ithway itewhay 
earsbay unningray overyay eirthay ivinglay acksbay. Inyay anotheryay 
ateplay, ethay odigiouspray underblay isyay ademay ofyay epresentingray 
ethay alewhay ithway erpendicularpay ukesflay. 

Enthay againyay, erethay isyay anyay imposingyay uartoqay, ittenwray byay oneyay 
Aptaincay Olnettcay, ayay ostpay-aptaincay inyay ethay Englishyay avynay, 
entitledyay Ayay Oyagevay oundray Apecay Ornhay intoyay ethay Outhsay Eassay, 
orfay ethay urposepay ofyay extendingyay ethay Ermacetispay Alewhay Isheriesfay. 
Inyay isthay ookbay isyay anyay outlineyay urportingpay otay ebay ayay ' Icturepay ofyay ayay

illedkay onyay ethay oastcay ofyay Exicomay, Augustyay 1793, andyay oistedhay 
onyay eckday.' Iyay oubtday otnay ethay aptaincay adhay isthay eraciousvay 
icturepay akentay orfay ethay enefitbay ofyay ishay arinesmay. Otay entionmay 
utbay oneyay ingthay aboutyay ityay, etlay emay aysay atthay ityay ashay anyay eyeyay ichwhay

Uetray Icturespay Ofyay Alingwhay Enesscay 

Inyay onnectioncay ithway ethay onstrousmay icturespay ofyay aleswhay, Iyay 
amyay onglystray emptedtay erehay otay enteryay uponyay osethay illstay oremay 
onstrousmay oriesstay ofyay emthay ichwhay areyay otay ebay oundfay inyay ertaincay 
ooksbay, othbay ancientyay andyay odernmay, especiallyyay ihay Inyplay, 
Urchaspay, Akluythay, Arrishay, Uviercay, etcyay. Utbay Iyay asspay atthay 
attermay byay. 

Iyay owknay ofyay onlyyay ourfay ublishedpay outlinesyay ofyay ethay eatgray 
ermspay alewhay : Olnettcay'say, Ugginshay'say, Ederickfray Uviercay 'say, 
andyay Ealebay'say. Inyay ethay eviouspray apterchay Olnettcay andyay Uviercay 
avehay eenbay eferredray otay. Ugginshay'say isyay arfay etterbay anthay eirsthay ; 
utbay, byay eatgray oddsyay, Ealebay'say isyay ethay estbay. Allyay Ealebay'say awdray- 
ingsyay ofyay isthay alewhay areyay oodgay, exceptingyay ethay iddlemay igurefay 
inyay ethay icturepay ofyay eethray aleswhay inyay ariousvay attitudesyay, appingcay 
ishay econdsay apterchay. Ishay ontispiecefray, oatsbay attackingyay 
ermspay aleswhay, oughthay onay oubtday alculatedcay otay exciteyay ethay 
ivilcay epticismscay ofyay omesay arlourpay enmay, isyay admirablyyay orrectcay 
andyay ifelikelay inyay itsyay eneralgay effectyay. Omesay ofyay ethay ermspay 
alewhay awingsdray inyay Jay. Ossray Ownebray areyay ettypray orrectcay inyay 
ontourcay ; utbay eythay areyay etchedlywray engravedyay. Atthay isyay 
otnay ishay aultfay, oughthay. 

Ofyay ethay ightray alewhay, ethay estbay outlineyay icturespay areyay inyay 
Oresbyscay ; utbay eythay areyay awndray onyay ootay allsmay ayay alescay otay 
onveycay ayay esirableday impressionyay. Ehay ashay utbay oneyay icturepay 
ofyay alingwhay enesscay, andyay isthay isyay ayay adsay eficiencyday, ecausebay ityay 
isyay byay uchsay icturespay onlyyay, enwhay atyay allyay ellway oneday, atthay ouyay

Utbay, akentay orfay allyay inyay allyay, byay arfay ethay inestfay, oughthay inyay omesay 
etailsday otnay ethay ostmay orrectcay, esentationspray ofyay aleswhay andyay 
alingwhay enesscay otay ebay anywhereyay oundfay, areyay otway argelay 
Enchfray engravingsyay, ellway executedyay, andyay akentay omfray aintpay- 
ingsyay byay oneyay Arnerygay. Espectivelyray, eythay epresentray 
attacksyay onyay ethay ermspay andyay ightray alewhay. Inyay ethay irstfay enyay- 
avinggray ayay oblenay ermspay alewhay isyay epictedday inyay ullfay ajestymay 
ofyay ightmay, ustjay isenray eneathbay ethay oatbay omfray ethay ofunditiespray 
ofyay ethay oceanyay, andyay earingbay ighhay inyay ethay airyay uponyay ishay ackbay ethay

isyay artiallypay unbrokenyay, andyay isyay awndray ustjay alancingbay uponyay 
ethay onstermay'say inespay ; andyay andingstay inyay atthay owpray, orfay atthay 
oneyay inglesay incomputableyay ashflay ofyay imetay, ouyay eholdbay anyay oarsyay- 
anmay, alfhay oudedshray byay ethay incensedyay oilingbay outspay ofyay ethay 
alewhay, andyay inyay ethay actyay ofyay eapinglay, asyay ifyay omfray ayay ecipicepray. 
Ethay actionyay ofyay ethay olewhay ingthay isyay onderfullyway oodgay andyay uetray. 
Ethay alfhay -emptiedyay inelay-ubtay oatsflay onyay ethay itenedwhay easay ; ethay 
oodenway olespay ofyay ethay illedspay arpoonshay obliquelyyay obbay inyay ityay ; 
ethay eadshay ofyay ethay immingsway ewcray areyay atteredscay aboutyay ethay 
alewhay inyay ontrastingcay expressionsyay ofyay affrightyay ; ilewhay ihay ethay 
ackblay ormystay istanceday ethay ipshay isyay earingbay ownday uponyay ethay 
enescay. Erioussay aultfay ightmay ebay oundfay ithway ethay anatomicalyay 
etailsday ofyay isthay alewhay, utbay etlay atthay asspay ; incesay, orfay ethay ifelay 
ofyay emay, Iyay ouldcay otnay awdray osay oodgay ayay oneyay. 

Inyay ethay econdsay engravingyay, ethay oatbay isyay inyay ethay actyay ofyay awdray- 
ingyay alongsideyay ethay arnacledbay ankflay ofyay ayay argelay unningray ightray 
alewhay, atthay ollsray ishay ackblay eedyway ulkbay inyay ethay easay ikelay omesay 
ossymay ockray-ideslay omfray ethay Atagonianpay iffsclay. Ishay etsjay 
areyay erectyay, ullfay, andyay ackblay ikelay ootsay ; osay atthay omfray osay 
aboundingyay ayay okesmay inyay ethay imneychay, ouyay ouldway inkthay erethay 
ustmay ebay ayay avebray uppersay ookingcay inyay ethay eatgray owelsbay elowbay.

otheryay easay-andiescay andyay acaronimay, ichwhay ethay ightray alewhay

ometimessay arriescay onyay ishay estilentpay ackbay. Andyay allyay ethay

Owhay Arnerygay ethay ainterpay isyay, oryay asway, Iyay owknay otnay. Utbay 
myay ifelay orfay ityay ehay asway eitheryay acticallypray onversantcay ithway ishay 
ubjectsay, oryay elseyay arvellouslymay utoredtay byay omesay experiencedyay 
alemanwhay. Ethay Enchfray areyay ethay adslay orfay aintingpay actionyay. 
Ogay andyay azegay uponyay allyay ethay aintingspay ofyay Europeyay, andyay erewhay 
illway ouyay indfay uchsay ayay allerygay ofyay ivinglay andyay eathingbray omcay- 
otionmay onyay anvascay, asyay inyay atthay iumphaltray allhay atyay Ersaillesvay ;

onsecutivecay eatgray attlesbay ofyay Ancefray ; erewhay everyyay ordsway 
eemssay ayay ashflay ofyay ethay Orthernnay Ightslay, andyay ethay uccessivesay 
armedyay ingskay andyay emperorsyay ashday byay, ikelay ayay argechay ofyay 
ownedcray entaurscay ? Otnay ollywhay unworthyyay ofyay ayay aceplay inyay 
atthay allerygay, areyay osethay easay-attlebay iecespay ofyay Arnerygay. 

Ethay aturalnay aptitudeyay ofyay ethay Enchfray orfay eizingsay ethay 
icturesquenesspay ofyay ingsthay eemssay otay ebay eculiarlypay evincedyay 
inyay atwhay aintingspay andyay engravingsyay eythay avehay ofyay eirthay 
alingwhay enesscay. Ithway otnay oneyay enthtay ofyay Englandyay'say experiyay- 
enceyay inyay ethay isheryfay, andyay otnay ethay ousandththay artpay ofyay atthay 
ofyay ethay Americansyay, eythay avehay everthelessnay urnishedfay othbay 
ationsnay ithway ethay onlyyay inishedfay etchesskay atyay allyay apablecay 
ofyay onveyingcay ethay ealray iritspay ofyay ethay alewhay-unthay. Orfay ethay 
ostmay artpay, ethay Englishyay andyay Americanyay alewhay aughtsmendray 
eemsay entirelyyay ontentcay ithway esentingpray ethay echanicalmay

Inyay additionyay otay osethay inefay engravingsyay omfray Arnerygay, erethay

oneyay owhay ubscribessay imselfhay ' Hay. Urandday.' Oneyay ofyay emthay,

uietqay oonnay-enescay amongyay ethay islesyay ofyay ethay Acificpay ; ayay Enchfray 
alerwhay anchoredyay, inshoreyay, inyay ayay almcay, andyay azilylay akingtay 
aterway onyay oardbay ; ethay oosenedlay ailssay ofyay ethay ipshay, andyay ethay 
onglay eaveslay ofyay ethay almspay inyay ethay ackgroundbay, othbay oopingdray 
ogethertay inyay ethay eezelessbray airyay. Ethay effectyay isyay eryvay inefay, 
enwhay onsideredcay ithway eferenceray otay itsyay esentingpray ethay ardyhay 
ishermenfay underyay oneyay ofyay eirthay ewfay aspectsyay ofyay orientalyay 
eposeray. Ethay otheryay engravingyay isyay uiteqay ayay ifferentday affairyay : 
ethay ipshay ovehay-otay uponyay ethay openyay easay, andyay inyay ethay eryvay earthay 
ofyay ethay eviathaniclay ifelay, ithway ayay ightray alewhay alongsideyay ; ethay 
esselvay (inyay ethay actyay ofyay uttingcay -inyay) ovehay overyay otay ethay onstermay 
asyay ifyay otay ayay uayqay ; andyay ayay oatbay, urriedlyhay ushingpay offyay omfray

useyay ; eethray oarsmenyay areyay ustjay ettingsay ethay astmay inyay itsyay olehay ;

ableyay ayay umpstay asyay anyyay ouyay illway indfay inyay ethay Esternway earingsclay.

owncastday eyesyay, andsstay uefullyray ontemplatingcay ishay ownyay 
amputationyay.

olitarysay etjay adhay aduallygray orkedway uponyay Ahabyay, osay atthay ehay 
asway ownay eparedpray otay onnectcay ethay ideasyay ofyay ildnessmay andyay 
eposeray ithway ethay irstfay ightsay ofyay ethay articularpay alewhay ehay 
ursuedpay ; oweverhay isthay asway, oryay etherwhay ishay eagernessyay 
etrayedbay imhay ; icheverwhay ayway ityay ightmay avehay eenbay, onay 
oonersay idday ehay istinctlyday erceivepay ethay itewhay assmay, anthay ithway 
ayay uickqay intensityyay ehay instantlyyay avegay ordersyay orfay oweringlay. 

Ethay ourfay oatsbay ereway oonsay onyay ethay aterway ; Ahabyay'say inyay 
advanceyay, andyay allyay iftlysway ullingpay owardtay eirthay eypray. Oonsay 
ityay entway ownday, andyay ilewhay, ithway oarsyay uspendedsay, eway ereway 
awaitingyay itsyay eappearanceray, olay ! inyay ethay amesay otspay erewhay ityay 
anksay, onceyay oremay ityay owlyslay oseray. Almostyay orgettingfay orfay 
ethay omentmay allyay oughtsthay ofyay Obymay-Ickday, eway ownay azedgay 
atyay ethay ostmay ondrousway enomenonphay ichwhay ethay ecretsay eassay 
avehay ithertohay evealedray otay ankindmay. Ayay astvay ulpypay assmay, 
urlongsfay inyay engthlay andyay eadthbray, ofyay ayay ancingglay eamcray-olourcay, 
aylay oatingflay onyay ethay aterway, innumerableyay onglay armsyay adiatingray 
omfray itsyay entrecay, andyay urlingcay andyay istingtway ikelay ayay estnay ofyay 
anacondasyay, asyay ifyay indlyblay otay utchclay atyay anyyay aplesshay objectyay 
ithinway eachray. Onay erceptiblepay acefay oryay ontfray idday ityay avehay ; 
onay onceivablecay okentay ofyay eitheryay ensationsay oryay instinctyay ; utbay 
undulatedyay erethay onyay ethay illowsbay, anyay unearthlyyay, ormlessfay, 
ancechay-ikelay apparitionyay ofyay ifelay. 

Asyay ithway ayay owlay uckingsay oundsay ityay owlyslay isappearedday againyay, 
Arbuckstay illstay azinggay atyay ethay agitatedyay atersway erewhay ityay adhay 
unksay, ithway ayay ildway oicevay exclaimedyay ' Almostyay atherray adhay 
Iyay eensay Obymay-Ickday andyay oughtfay imhay, anthay otay avehay eensay eethay, 
outhay itewhay ostghay ! ' 

' Atwhay asway ityay, irsay ? ' aidsay Askflay. 

' Ethay eatgray ivelay uidsqay, ichwhay, eythay aysay, ewfay alewhay-ipsshay 
everyay eheldbay, andyay eturnedray otay eirthay ortspay otay elltay ofyay ityay.' 



352 Obymay-Ickday 

Utbay Ahabyay aidsay othingnay ; urningtay ishay oatbay, ehay ailedsay 
ackbay otay ethay esselvay ; ethay estray asyay ilentlysay ollowingfay. 

Ateverwhay uperstitionssay ethay ermspay alemenwhay inyay eneralgay 
avehay onnectedcay ithway ethay ightsay ofyay isthay objectyay, ertaincay ityay isyay, 
atthay ayay impseglay ofyay ityay eingbay osay eryvay unusualyay, atthay ircumcay- 
ancestay ashay onegay arfay otay investyay ityay ithway ortentpay ousnessyay. Osay 
arelyray isyay ityay eheldbay, atthay oughthay oneyay andyay allyay ofyay emthay eclareday 
ityay otay ebay ethay argestlay animatedyay ingthay inyay ethay oceanyay, etyay eryvay 
ewfay ofyay emthay avehay anyyay utbay ethay ostmay aguevay ideasyay oncerncay- 
ingyay itsyay uetray aturenay andyay ormfay ; otwithstandingnay, eythay 
elievebay ityay otay urnishfay otay ethay ermspay alewhay ishay onlyyay oodfay. 
Orfay oughthay otheryay eciesspay ofyay aleswhay indfay eirthay oodfay aboveyay 
aterway, andyay aymay ebay eensay byay anmay inyay ethay actyay ofyay eedingfay, ethay 
ermacetispay alewhay obtainsyay ishay olewhay oodfay inyay unknownyay 
oneszay elowbay ethay urfacesay ; andyay .onlyyay byay inferenceyay isyay ityay 
atthay anyyay oneyay ancay elltay ofyay atwhay, eciselypray, atthay oodfay onsistscay. 
Atyay imestay, enwhay oselyclay ursuedpay, ehay illway isgorgeday atwhay areyay 
upposedsay otay ebay ethay etachedday armsyay ofyay ethay uidsqay ; omesay ofyay 
emthay usthay exhibitedyay exceedingyay entytway andyay irtythay eetfay inyay 
engthlay. Eythay ancyfay atthay ethay onstermay otay ichwhay esethay armsyay 
elongedbay ordinarilyyay ingsclay byay emthay otay ethay edbay ofyay ethay oceanyay ; 
andyay atthay ethay ermspay alewhay, unlikeyay otheryay eciesspay, isyay uppliedsay 
ithway eethtay inyay orderyay otay attackyay andyay eartay ityay. 

Erethay eemssay omesay oundgray otay imagineyay atthay ethay eatgray 
Akenkray ofyay Ishopbay Ontoppodanpay aymay ultimatelyyay esolveray 
itselfyay intoyay Uidsqay. Ethay annermay inyay ichwhay ethay Ishopbay eday- 
ibesscray ityay, asyay alternatelyyay isingray andyay inkingsay, ithway omesay 
otheryay articularspay ehay arratesnay, inyay allyay isthay ethay otway orrecay- 
ondspay. Utbay uchmay abatementyay isyay ecessarynay ithway espectray 
otay ethay incredibleyay ulkbay ehay assignsyay ityay. 

Byay omesay aturalistsnay owhay avehay aguelyvay eardhay umoursray 
ofyay ethay eriousmystay eaturecray, erehay okenspay ofyay, ityay isyay includedyay 
amongyay ethay assclay ofyay uttlecay-ishfay, otay ichwhay, indeedyay, inyay ertaincay 
externalyay espectsray ityay ouldway eemsay otay elongbay, utbay onlyyay asyay ethay 
Anakyay ofyay ethay ibetray. 



Apterchay Lxay 

Ethay Inelay 

Ithway eferenceray otay ethay alingwhay enescay ortlyshay otay ebay eday- 
ibedscray, asyay ellway asyay orfay ethay etterbay understandingyay ofyay allyay 
imilarsay enesscay elsewhereyay esentedpray, Iyay avehay erehay otay eakspay 
ofyay ethay agicalmay, ometimessay orriblehay alewhay-inelay. 

Ethay inelay originallyyay usedyay inyay ethay isheryfay asway ofyay ethay estbay 
emphay, ightlyslay apouredvay ithway artay, otnay impregnatedyay ithway 
ityay, asyay inyay ethay asecay ofyay ordinaryyay opesray ; orfay ilewhay artay, asyay 
ordinarilyyay usedyay, akesmay ethay emphay oremay iableplay otay ethay operay- 
akermay, andyay alsoyay endersray ethay operay itselfyay oremay onvenientcay 
otay ethay ailorsay orfay ommoncay ipshay useyay ; etyay, otnay onlyyay ouldway 
ethay ordinaryyay uantityqay ootay uchmay iffenstay ethay alewhay-inelay orfay 
ethay oseclay oilingcay otay ichwhay ityay ustmay ebay ubjectedsay ; utbay asyay 
ostmay eamensay areyay eginningbay otay earnlay, artay inyay eneralgay byay 
onay eansmay addsyay otay ethay operay'say urabilityday oryay engthstray, owhay- 
everyay uchmay ityay aymay ivegay ityay ompactnesscay andyay ossglay. 

Ofyay atelay earsyay ethay Anillamay operay ashay inyay ethay Americanyay 
isheryfay almostyay entirelyyay upersededsay emphay asyay ayay aterialmay 
orfay alewhay-ineslay ; orfay, oughthay otnay osay urableday asyay emphay, ityay 
isyay ongerstray, andyay arfay oremay oftsay andyay elasticyay ; andyay Iyay illway addyay 
(incesay erethay isyay anyay aestheticsyay inyay allyay ingsthay), isyay uchmay oremay 
andsomehay andyay ecomingbay otay ethay oatbay, anthay emphay. Emphay 
isyay ayay uskyday, arkday ellowfay, ayay ortsay ofyay Indianyay ; utbay Anillamay 
isyay asyay ayay oldengay-airedhay Ircassiancay otay eholdbay. 

Ethay alewhay-inelay isyay onlyyay otway-irdsthay ofyay anyay inchyay inyay icknessthay. 
Atyay irstfay ightsay, ouyay ouldway otnay inkthay ityay osay ongstray asyay ityay eallyray 
isyay. Byay experimentyay itsyay oneyay andyay iftyfay arnsyay illway eachyay ussay- 
endpay ayay eightway ofyay oneyay undredhay andyay entytway oundspay ; osay 

Olvay. iyay. zay 



354 Obymay-Ickday 

atthay ethay olewhay operay illway earbay ayay ainstray earlynay equalyay otay eethray 
onstay. Inyay engthlay, ethay ommoncay ermspay alewhay-inelay easuresmay 
omethingsay overyay otway undredhay athomsfay. Owardtay ethay 
ernstay ofyay ethay oatbay ityay isyay irallyspay oiledcay awayyay inyay ethay ubtay, otnay 
ikelay ethay ormway-ipepay ofyay ayay illstay oughthay, utbay osay asyay otay ormfay oneyay 
oundray, eesechay-apedshay assmay ofyay enselyday eddedbay 'eavesshay,' 
oryay ayerslay ofyay oncentriccay iralisationsspay, ithoutway anyyay ollowhay 
utbay ethay 'earthay/ oryay inutemay erticalvay ubetay ormedfay atyay ethay 
axisyay ofyay ethay eesechay. Asyay ethay eastlay angletay oryay inkkay inyay ethay 
oilingcay ouldway, inyay unningray outyay, infalliblyyay aketay omebodysay'say 
armyay, eglay, oryay entireyay odybay offyay, ethay utmostyay ecautionpray isyay 
usedyay inyay owingstay ethay inelay inyay itsyay ubtay. Omesay arpooneershay 
illway onsumecay almostyay anyay entireyay orningmay inyay isthay usinessbay, 
arryingcay ethay inelay ighhay aloftyay andyay enthay eevingray ityay ownwardday 
oughthray ayay ockblay owardtay ethay ubtay, osay asyay inyay ethay actyay ofyay oilingcay 
otay eefray ityay omfray allyay ossiblepay inkleswray andyay iststway. 

Inyay ethay Englishyay oatsbay otway ubstay areyay usedyay insteadyay ofyay oneyay ; 
ethay amesay inelay eingbay ontinuouslycay oiledcay inyay othbay ubstay. 
Erethay isyay omesay advantageyay inyay isthay ; ecausebay esethay intway -ubstay 
eingbay osay allsmay eythay itfay oremay eadilyray intoyay ethay oatbay, andyay oday 
otnay ainstray ityay osay uchmay ; ereaswhay, ethay Americanyay ubtay, earlynay 
eethray eetfay inyay iameterday andyay ofyay oportionatepray epthday, akesmay 
ayay atherray ulkybay eightfray orfay ayay aftcray osewhay anksplay areyay utbay 
oneyay alfhay-inchyay inyay icknessthay ; orfay ethay ottombay ofyay ethay alewhay- 
oatbay isyay ikelay iticalcray iceyay, ichwhay illway earbay upyay ayay onsiderablecay 
istributedday eightway, utbay otnay eryvay uchmay ofyay ayay oncentratedcay 
oneyay. Enwhay ethay aintedpay anvascay overcay isyay appedclay onyay ethay 
Americanyay inelay-ubtay, ethay oatbay ookslay asyay ifyay ityay ereway ullingpay offyay 
ithway ayay odigiouspray eatgray eddingway-akecay otay esentpray otay ethay 
aleswhay. 

Othbay endsyay ofyay ethay inelay areyay exposedyay ; ethay owerlay endyay 
erminatingtay inyay anyay eyeyay -icesplay oryay ooplay omingcay upyay omfray ethay 
ottombay againstyay ethay idesay ofyay ethay ubtay, andyay anginghay overyay 
itsyay edgeyay ompletelycay isengagedday omfray everythingyay. Isthay 
arrangementyay ofyay ethay owerlay endyay isyay ecessarynay onyay otway accountsyay. 



Ethay Inelay 355 

Irstfay : Inyay orderyay otay acilitatefay ethay asteningfay otay ityay ofyay anyay 
additionalyay inelay omfray ayay eighbouringnay oatbay, inyay asecay ethay 
ickenstray alewhay ouldshay oundsay osay eepday asyay otay eatenthray otay 
arrycay offyay ethay entireyay inelay originallyyay attachedyay otay ethay arhay- 
oonpay. Inyay esethay instancesyay, ethay alewhay ofyay oursecay isyay iftedshay 
ikelay ayay ugmay ofyay aleyay, asyay ityay ereway, omfray ethay oneyay oatbay otay ethay 
otheryay ; oughthay ethay irstfay oatbay alwaysyay overshay atyay andhay otay 
assistyay itsyay onsortcay. Econdsay : Isthay arrangementyay isyay indisyay- 
ensablepay orfay ommoncay afetysay'say akesay ; orfay ereway ethay owerlay 
endyay ofyay ethay inelay inyay anyyay ayway attachedyay otay ethay oatbay, andyay ereway 
ethay alewhay enthay otay unray ethay inelay outyay otay ethay endyay almostyay inyay ayay 
inglesay, okingsmay inutemay asyay ehay ometimessay oesday, ehay ouldway 
otnay opstay erethay, orfay ethay oomedday oatbay ouldway infalliblyyay 
ebay aggeddray ownday afteryay imhay intoyay ethay ofunditypray ofyay ethay easay ; 
andyay inyay atthay asecay onay owntay -iercray ouldway everyay indfay erhay againyay. 

Eforebay oweringlay ethay oatbay orfay ethay asechay, ethay upperyay endyay 
ofyay ethay inelay isyay akentay aftyay omfray ethay ubtay, andyay assingpay oundray ethay 
oggerlay-eadhay erethay, isyay againyay arriedcay orwardfay ethay entireyay 
engthlay ofyay ethay oatbay, estingray osswisecray uponyay ethay oomlay oryay 
andlehay ofyay everyyay anmay'say oaryay, osay atthay ityay ogsjay againstyay ishay istwray 
inyay owingray ; andyay alsoyay assingpay etweenbay ethay enmay, asyay eythay 
alternatelyyay itsay atyay ethay oppositeyay unwalesgay, otay ethay eadedlay 
ockschay oryay oovesgray inyay ethay extremeyay ointedpay owpray ofyay ethay oatbay, 
erewhay ayay oodenway inpay oryay ewerskay ethay izesay ofyay ayay ommoncay uillqay, 
eventspray ityay omfray ippingslay outyay. Omfray ethay ockschay ityay angshay 
inyay ayay ightslay estoonfay overyay ethay owsbay, andyay isyay enthay assedpay insideyay 
ethay oatbay againyay ; andyay omesay entay oryay entytway athomsfay (alledcay 
oxbay-inelay) eingbay oiledcay uponyay ethay oxbay inyay ethay owsbay, ityay oncay- 
inuestay itsyay ayway otay ethay unwalegay illstay ayay ittlelay urtherfay aftyay, andyay 
isyay enthay attachedyay otay ethay ortshay -arpway ethay operay ichwhay isyay 
immediatelyyay onnectedcay ithway ethay arpoonhay ; utbay eviouspray 
otay atthay onnectioncay, ethay ortshay -arpway oesgay oughthray undrysay 
ificationsmystay ootay edioustay otay etailday. 

Usthay ethay alewhay-inelay oldsfay ethay olewhay oatbay inyay itsyay omplicay- 
atedcay oilscay, istingtway andyay ithingwray aroundyay ityay inyay almostyay 



356 Obymay-Ickday 

everyyay irectionday. Allyay ethay oarsmenyay areyay involvedyay inyay itsyay 
erilouspay ontortionscay ; osay atthay otay ethay imidtay eyeyay ofyay ethay 
andsmanlay, eythay eemsay asyay Indianyay ugglersjay, ithway ethay eadliestday 
akessnay ortivelyspay estooningfay eirthay imbslay. Ornay ancay anyyay 
onsay ofyay ortalmay omanway, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, eatsay imselfhay amidyay 
osethay empenhay intricaciesyay, andyay ilewhay ainingstray ishay utmostyay 
atyay ethay oaryay, ethinkbay imhay atthay atyay anyyay unknownyay instantyay ethay 
arpoonhay aymay ebay artedday, andyay allyay esethay orriblehay ontortionscay 
ebay utpay inyay ayplay ikelay ingedray ightningslay ; ehay annotcay ebay usthay 
ircumstancedcay ithoutway ayay uddershay atthay akesmay ethay eryvay 
arrowmay inyay ishay onesbay otay uiverqay inyay imhay ikelay ayay akenshay ellyjay. 
Etyay abithay angestray ingthay ! atwhay annotcay abithay accomyay- 
ishplay ? Ayergay alliessay, oremay errymay irthmay, etterbay okesjay, 
andyay ighterbray eparteesray, ouyay evernay eardhay overyay ouryay 
ahoganymay, anthay ouyay illway earhay overyay ethay alfhay-inchyay itewhay 
edarcay ofyay ethay alewhay-oatbay, enwhay usthay unghay inyay angmanhay'say 
oosesnay ; andyay, ikelay ethay ixsay urghersbay ofyay Alaiscay eforebay Ingkay 
Edwardyay, ethay ixsay enmay omposingcay ethay ewcray ullpay intoyay ethay 
awsjay ofyay eathday, ithway ayay alterhay aroundyay everyyay ecknay, asyay ouyay 
aymay aysay. 

Erhapspay ayay eryvay ittlelay oughtthay illway ownay enableyay ouyay otay 
accountyay orfay osethay epeatedray alingwhay isastersday omesay ewfay 
ofyay ichwhay areyay asuallycay onicledchray ofyay isthay anmay oryay atthay anmay 
eingbay akentay outyay ofyay ethay oatbay byay ethay inelay, andyay ostlay. Orfay, 
enwhay ethay inelay isyay artingday outyay, otay ebay eatedsay enthay inyay ethay oatbay 
isyay ikelay eingbay eatedsay inyay ethay idstmay ofyay ethay anifoldmay izzingswhay 
ofyay ayay eamstay-engineyay inyay ullfay ayplay, enwhay everyyay ingflyay eambay, 
andyay aftshay, andyay eelwhay, isyay azinggray ouyay. Ityay isyay orseway ; orfay 
ouyay annotcay itsay otionlessmay inyay ethay earthay ofyay esethay erilspay, 
ecausebay ethay oatbay isyay ockingray ikelay ayay adlecray, andyay ouyay areyay 
itchedpay oneyay ayway andyay ethay otheryay, ithoutway ethay ightestslay 
arningway ; andyay onlyyay byay ayay ertaincay elfsay-adjustingyay uoyancybay 
andyay imultaneousnesssay ofyay olitionvay andyay actionyay ancay ouyay 
escapeyay eingbay ademay ayay Azeppamay ofyay, andyay unray awayyay ithway erewhay 
ethay allyay-eeingsay unsay imselfhay ouldcay evernay iercepay ouyay outyay. 



Ethay Inelay 357 

Againyay : asyay ethay ofoundpray almcay ichwhay onlyyay apparentlyyay 
ecedespray andyay ophesiespray ofyay ethay ormstay isyay erhapspay oremay 
awfulyay anthay ethay ormstay itselfyay ; orfay, indeedyay, ethay almcay 
isyay utbay ethay apperwray andyay envelopeyay ofyay ethay ormstay ; andyay oncay- 
ainstay ityay inyay itselfyay, asyay ethay eeminglysay armlesshay ifleray oldshay ethay 
atalfay owderpay, andyay ethay allbay, andyay ethay explosionyay ; osay ethay 
acefulgray eposeray ofyay ethay inelay, asyay ityay ilentlysay erpentinessay aboutyay 
ethay oarsmenyay eforebay eingbay oughtbray intoyay actualyay ayplay isthay 
isyay ayay ingthay ichwhay arriescay oremay ofyay uetray errortay anthay anyyay otheryay 
aspectyay ofyay isthay angerousday affairyay. Utbay whyay aysay oremay ? 
Allyay enmay ivelay envelopedyay inyay alewhay -ineslay. Allyay areyay ornbay ithway 
altershay oundray eirthay ecksnay ; utbay ityay isyay onlyyay enwhay aughtcay 
inyay ethay iftsway, uddensay urntay ofyay eathday, atthay ortalsmay ealiseray 
ethay ilentsay, ubtlesay, everyay-esentpray erilspay ofyay ifelay. Andyay ifyay ouyay 
ebay ayay ilosopherphay, oughthay eatedsay inyay ethay alewhay-oatbay, ouyay 
ouldway otnay atyay earthay eelfay oneyay itwhay oremay ofyay errortay, anthay 
oughthay eatedsay eforebay ouryay eveningyay irefay ithway ayay okerpay, andyay 
otnay ayay arpoonhay, byay ouryay idesay. 



Endyay Ofyay Olvay. Iyay.
